### [1] [How to measure the optimality of word or gesture order with respect to the principle of swap distance minimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01938)
*Ramon Ferrer-i-Cancho*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于置换多面体（permutohedron）的数学框架，用于衡量词序或手势序列相对于交换距离最小化的优化程度，发现跨语言手势序列至少达到77%的优化水平，并将二次分配问题（QAP）引入语言研究作为统一多种优化问题的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在检验语言中词序排列是否遵循交换距离最小化假设，即给定源顺序时，在置换多面体中距离更近的词序排列成本更低、出现概率更高。这为理解语言系统的优化机制提供了理论基础。

Method: 研究提出了一种测量词序变异相对于交换距离最小化优化程度的方法，基于置换多面体（permutohedron）的数学框架，其中顶点表示排列，相邻顶点通过交换相邻元素连接。同时将二次分配问题（quadratic assignment problem, QAP）引入语言研究作为统一框架。

Result: 研究发现跨语言手势序列至少达到77%的优化水平，且多次达到最优解的情况不太可能是偶然现象。这为交换距离最小化假设提供了实证支持，并建立了研究通信系统中词序或手势序列优化程度的理论基础。

Conclusion: 研究建立了基于置换多面体和二次分配问题（QAP）的理论框架，用于分析语言系统中词序或手势序列的优化程度。提出了统一多种语言优化原则的"最优分配一般原则"，为理解语言系统的结构优化提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: The structure of all the permutations of a sequence can be represented as a permutohedron, a graph where vertices are permutations and two vertices are linked if a swap of adjacent elements in the permutation of one of the vertices produces the permutation of the other vertex. It has been hypothesized that word orders in languages minimize the swap distance in the permutohedron: given a source order, word orders that are closer in the permutohedron should be less costly and thus more likely. Here we explain how to measure the degree of optimality of word order variation with respect to swap distance minimization. We illustrate the power of our novel mathematical framework by showing that crosslinguistic gestures are at least $77\%$ optimal. It is unlikely that the multiple times where crosslinguistic gestures hit optimality are due to chance. We establish the theoretical foundations for research on the optimality of word or gesture order with respect to swap distance minimization in communication systems. Finally, we introduce the quadratic assignment problem (QAP) into language research as an umbrella for multiple optimization problems and, accordingly, postulate a general principle of optimal assignment that unifies various linguistic principles including swap distance minimization.

</details>


<div id='physics.ins-det'></div>

# physics.ins-det [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Electrostatic transfer of sub-micron magnetic particles onto cantilevers using a focused ion beam system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01528)
*Peter Sun,George R. Du Laney,Tim M. Fuchs,Tjerk H. Oosterkamp,Malcolm G. Thomas,John A. Marohn*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种聚焦离子束辅助方法，用于制备磁共振力显微镜测量的磁针尖。该方法通过静电转移预制的磁性纳米颗粒到微悬臂梁上，实现了对磁体悬垂部分的精确控制，同时最小化了对针尖磁体前缘的制造损伤。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统制造方法难以实现多种针尖形状、尺寸和材料的制备，且容易对针尖磁体前缘造成损伤。需要开发一种能够精确控制磁体悬垂部分并最小化制造损伤的新方法。

Method: 采用聚焦离子束（focused-ion-beam）辅助的静电转移方法，将预制的磁性纳米颗粒（magnetic nanoparticles）转移到微悬臂梁（microcantilevers）上。该方法通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）确认了离子束损伤的最小化。

Result: 成功制备了尺寸范围从460纳米到2.8微米的磁体，并将其固定在两种类型的悬臂梁上：弹簧常数为800微牛/米的硅悬臂梁和弹簧常数为30微牛/米的单晶硅悬臂梁。静电转移方法实现了传统方法无法达到的多种针尖形状、尺寸和材料。

Conclusion: 该技术具有多功能性，可用于制造定制针尖悬臂梁，适用于更广泛的扫描探针技术（scanning probe techniques）。静电转移方法为磁共振力显微镜（magnetic resonance force microscopy）测量提供了更精确、损伤更小的磁针尖制备方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a focused-ion-beam-assisted method for preparing magnet tips for magnetic resonance force microscopy measurements. The method electrostatically transfers prefabricated magnetic nanoparticles to microcantilevers, achieving precise control over the magnet overhang past the cantilever leading edge while minimizing the fabrication damage to the leading edge of the tip magnet. We demonstrate successful fabrication of magnets ranging in size from 460 nm to 2.8 um. These magnets were affixed to two types of cantilevers: silicon cantilevers with a spring constant of 800 uN/m, and single-crystal silicon cantilevers with a spring constant of 30 uN/m. We show that the electrostatic transfer method enables a wide variety of tip shapes, sizes, and materials that were previously not possible with conventional fabrication methods. The transfer procedure allows us to prefabricate the desired particle geometry with minimal ion-beam damage, as confirmed by Monte Carlo simulations. We show that the technique is versatile and can be used to fabricate custom-tipped cantilevers for a broader range of scanning probe techniques.

</details>

# cond-mat.dis-nn [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Variational Iterative Rotation Algorithm: Combinatorial Optimization with Classical Kicked Tops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01512)
*Flaviano Morone,Andrew D. Kent,Dries Sels*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种经典变分迭代旋转算法（VIRAL），作为量子近似优化算法（QAOA）的经典实现，在Sherrington-Kirkpatrick自旋玻璃基准测试中表现优于量子版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索QAOA类协议有效性的根源，并开发一种经典实现方案。该工作旨在验证经典动力学系统是否能超越量子对应算法，并阐明其底层机制。

Method: 方法是将QAOA经典化为哈密顿动力学系统，称为变分迭代旋转算法（VIRAL）。该系统采用经典受击陀螺（kicked tops）模型，变分参数为电路每层的横向和纵向旋转角度。

Result: 结果显示VIRAL在所有电路深度下均优于QAOA，能量密度以1/p的线性速率收敛到基态值。优化动力学遵循Floquet协议，其中叉形分岔（pitchfork bifurcation）使赤道固定点失稳并驱动自旋朝向极向Ising构型。

Conclusion: 结论表明QAOA类协议的有效性主要源于其底层迭代旋转结构，且经典实现优于量子对应。研究进一步提出纳米尺度磁隧道结（magnetic tunnel junctions）作为实现VIRAL的自然物理平台。

Abstract: We investigate a classical formulation of the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA), realized as a Hamiltonian dynamical system of classical kicked tops, which we call the Variational Iterative Rotation Algorithm (VIRAL). The variational parameters are the transverse and longitudinal rotation angles at each of the p layers of the circuit. We find that VIRAL outperforms QAOA on the canonical Sherrington-Kirkpatrick spin-glass benchmark at all circuit depths, with the energy density converging to the ground state value linearly in 1/p. For large circuit depths, the optimized dynamics follows a Floquet protocol in which a pitchfork bifurcation destabilizes the equatorial fixed point and drives the spins toward polar Ising configurations. Our results demonstrate that the effectiveness of QAOA-like protocols derives primarily from their underlying iterative rotation structure, and that a classical implementation of it outperforms its quantum counterpart. We further elucidate its efficiency by reducing the many-body classical evolution to an effective Landau-Lifshitz dynamics for a single spin in a stochastic magnetic field. In this picture, the covariance matrix of the effective field reveals a nearly rank-one structure in which a single mode dominates the stochastic dynamics. In contrast, quantum fluctuations make the noise covariance of the effective quantum model of higher rank, hampering the control of the system. We propose nanometer-scale magnetic tunnel junctions as a natural physical platform for implementing VIRAL, where spin rotations can be realized using magnetic fields and spin torques.

</details>


### [4] [Isolated extended states and anomalous critical behavior in the generalized SSH model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01649)
*Jia-Ming Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究广义SSH模型的局域化特性，发现无界跃迁（unbounded hopping）保护扩展态（extended states）的存在，但广义非公度零点（generalized incommensurate zeros）会破坏这种保护，使扩展相转变为多重分形相（multifractal phase）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究广义SSH模型的局域化特性，探索无界跃迁对扩展态的保护机制，以及广义非公度零点如何诱导系统从扩展相向多重分形相转变。

Method: 采用数值计算和解析分析相结合的方法，研究广义SSH模型中扩展态的出现和保护机制，分析广义非公度零点对系统相变的影响。

Result: 发现无界跃迁保护扩展态的存在，但广义非公度零点会破坏这种保护，导致扩展相转变为多重分形相；在相区边界仍存在扩展态，这些扩展态与多重分形增强的迁移率边（mobility edges）重合，将多重分形相与局域化相分离。

Conclusion: 这些扩展态源于SSH模型的带边态（band edge states），并影响邻近能量的本征态，导致反常的扩展-多重分形临界转变；研究结果丰富了临界点本征态的行为类型，为深入理解安德森局域化（Anderson localization）和多重分形相的诱导提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the localization properties of a generalized SSH model. Numerical and analytical results indicate the emergence of extended states protected by unbounded hopping in this model. Moreover, this protection effect is disrupted by the appearance of generalized incommensurate zeros, causing the extended phase in the system to transition into a multifractal phase. However, at the boundaries of the phase region, we still observe the existence of extended states. These extended states coincide with multifractality-enriched mobility edges, separating the multifractal phase from the localized phase. Further analysis reveals that this extended states originates from the band edge states of SSH model. In addition, these isolated extended states also influence eigenstates with nearby energies, giving rise to an anomalous extended-to-multifractal critical transition. These findings not only enrich the behavioral repertoire of eigenstates at critical points, but also offer new insights for further understanding Anderson localization and the induction of multifractal phases.

</details>


### [5] [Crossovers from nonlinear wave-packet acceleration to wave-mixing and self-trapping in the Hatano-Nelson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02263)
*Bertin Many Manda,Vassos Achilleos*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文证明波放大（wave amplification）使弱非线性能够重塑非互易系统中的线性波包传输，揭示了非线性与放大相互作用产生的三个动力学区域，为精确控制非互易超材料中的波提供了途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究非线性与非互易系统中波放大之间的相互作用，探索弱非线性如何影响线性波包传输，旨在为非互易超材料（nonreciprocal metamaterials）中的波控制提供理论基础。

Method: 研究Hatano-Nelson模型中具有现场立方非线性（onsite cubic nonlinearity）的体高斯波包（bulk Gaussian wave packets）动力学，通过分析非线性与放大的相互作用来推导波包演化的解析预测。

Result: 非线性与放大相互作用产生增长频率偏移，驱动波包经历三个动力学区域：早期非线性趋肤区域（nonlinear-skin regime）、中间波混合区域（wave-mixing regime）和自陷区域（self-trapping regime）。在非线性趋肤区域内，非线性耦合了放大、色散和非互易性，改变波包加速度大小并引入显式时间依赖性。

Conclusion: 聚焦非线性抑制加速度并使其随时间减小，而散焦非线性增强加速度并使其增加；非线性相互作用通常在非厄米跳跃（non-Hermitian jump）发生前破坏波包，这些结果为精确控制非互易超材料中的波提供了途径。

Abstract: We demonstrate that wave amplification enables even weak nonlinearities to reshape linear wave-packet transport in nonreciprocal systems. We study the dynamics of bulk Gaussian wave packets in the Hatano--Nelson model with onsite cubic nonlinearity. We show that the interplay between nonlinearity and amplification generates growing frequency shifts that drive the wave packet through three successive dynamical regimes: an early nonlinear-skin regime with coherent propagation, an intermediate wave-mixing regime driven by mode resonances, and a self-trapping regime in which part of the packet localizes while the remainder ballistically spreads along the system favored direction. The crossover time scales are set by the width and average spacing of the eigen-frequency spectrum. Crucially, within the nonlinear-skin regime, we derive analytical predictions for the wave-packet dynamics and show that nonlinearity couples amplification, dispersion, and nonreciprocity, thereby modifying the magnitude of the wave-packet acceleration and introducing an explicit time dependence into its evolution. Focusing nonlinearities suppress the acceleration and cause it to decrease in time, whereas defocusing nonlinearities enhance it and cause it to increase. We further show that nonlinear interactions typically break down the wave packet before the non-Hermitian jump can occur. Our results provide a route toward accurate control of waves in nonreciprocal metamaterials.

</details>


### [6] [Robust Correlation-Induced Localization Under Time-Reversal Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02321)
*Bikram Pain,Sthitadhi Roy,Jens H. Bardarson,Ivan M. Khaymovich*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 研究一维无序系统中具有长程关联跳跃的安德森局域化（Anderson localization），其中跳跃幅度随距离按1/r^a衰减且具有破坏时间反演对称性的复跳跃幅度。发现关联诱导的代数局域化对有限强度的时间反演对称性破坏参数具有鲁棒性，超过该阈值后所有态退局域化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究长程关联跳跃与时间反演对称性破坏之间的相互作用如何影响一维无序系统中的安德森局域化。探索这两个因素共同作用下的局域化-退局域化转变。

Method: 分析研究具有长程关联跳跃的一维无序系统，其中跳跃幅度随距离按1/r^a衰减，且具有可调参数的复跳跃幅度以破坏时间反演对称性。通过解析方法研究静态局域化相图，并通过波包扩散视角研究动力学相图。

Result: 发现关联诱导的代数局域化对有限强度的时间反演对称性破坏参数具有鲁棒性，超过该阈值后所有态退局域化。在动力学方面，时间反演对称情况下的波包均方位移随时间呈亚扩散增长，而任何有限值的时间反演对称性破坏参数都会使其变为扩散增长。

Conclusion: 长程关联跳跃与时间反演对称性破坏之间的相互作用驱动了局域化-退局域化转变。该研究建立了由这两个因素共同作用的相变机制，并揭示了静态与动力学相图之间的对应关系。

Abstract: We study Anderson localization in a one-dimensional disordered system with long-range correlated hopping decaying as $1/r^{a}$ with complex hopping amplitudes that break time-reversal symmetry in a tunable fashion by varying their argument. We find analytically a corelation-induced algebraic localization that is robust to a finite strength of the time-reversal-symmetry-breaking parameter, beyond which all states delocalize. This establishes a localization--delocalization transition driven by the interplay between long-ranged correlated hopping and time-reversal symmetry breaking. In addition to obtaining the static localization phase diagram, we also investigate the dynamical phase diagram through the lens of wavepacket spreading. We find that the growth in time of the mean-squared displacement of a wavepacket, which is subdiffusive for the time-reversal symmetric case, becomes diffusive for any finite value of the time-reversal-symmetry-breaking parameter.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [ATLAS and CMS measurements of the $t\bar{t}$ cross section, including off-shell and near threshold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01984)
*Baptiste Ravina*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文总结了ATLAS和CMS合作组对顶夸克对（$t\bar{t}$）截面的最新测量结果，包括包容性和微分测量，并探讨了离壳效应、蒙特卡洛生成器建模，以及在阈值区域对顶夸克汤川耦合和准束缚态形成的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在报告ATLAS和CMS合作组对顶夸克对产生截面的最新测量进展，特别关注离壳效应（off-shell effects）的探测和阈值区域（threshold）的物理现象，以深化对顶夸克性质及其相互作用的理解。

Method: 研究方法包括对$pp\to W^+bW^-\bar{b}$和$pp\to e^\pmμ^\mp +b\bar{b}$过程的离壳效应分析，讨论POWHEG bb4$\ell$蒙特卡洛生成器（Monte Carlo generator）的建模方面，并在阈值区域进行截面和性质测量。

Result: 测量结果显示了对顶夸克对截面的包容性和微分结果，间接提取了顶夸克汤川耦合（top quark Yukawa coupling），并在阈值附近观测到与准束缚态（quasi-bound states）形成一致的事件超出（excess of events）。

Conclusion: 论文总结了ATLAS和CMS合作组在顶夸克对产生截面测量方面的最新成果，特别是离壳效应研究和阈值区域物理的进展，为理解顶夸克性质和可能的准束缚态形成提供了重要实验证据。

Abstract: Recent measurements of the $t\bar{t}$ cross section, performed both inclusively and differentially by the ATLAS and CMS Collaborations, are reported. In particular, off-shell effects are probed in the $pp\to W^+bW^-\bar{b}$ and $pp\to e^\pmμ^\mp +b\bar{b}$ processes, and modelling aspects of the POWHEG bb4$\ell$ Monte Carlo generator are discussed. Cross section and properties measurements are also performed at the threshold: we review an indirect extraction of the top quark Yukawa coupling, as well as the recent observations by both experiments of an excess of events near the top pair production threshold that is consistent with the formation of quasi-bound states.

</details>


### [8] [Search for Higgs boson pair production in the $\mathrm{b\bar{b}WW}$ decay channel with two leptons in the final state using proton-proton collision data at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02127)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文首次利用LHC在13.6 TeV能量下的质子-质子对撞数据，搜索希格斯玻色子对产生过程，其中一对希格斯玻色子衰变为底夸克对，另一对衰变为两个W玻色子并最终产生轻子和中微子。结果与标准模型预测一致，并设定了希格斯玻色子对产生截面的上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在搜索希格斯玻色子对（Higgs boson pair）产生过程，这是探测希格斯玻色子自耦合（trilinear self-coupling）的关键通道。通过分析特定衰变模式，可以约束希格斯玻色子的自相互作用强度，这对验证标准模型（Standard Model）和探索新物理具有重要意义。

Method: 研究使用CMS探测器记录的质子-质子对撞数据，对撞能量为13.6 TeV，对应积分亮度62 fb⁻¹。搜索针对特定衰变通道：一个希格斯玻色子衰变为底夸克对（bottom quarks），另一个衰变为两个W玻色子，后者进一步轻子衰变（leptonically）为电子或μ子及中微子。

Result: 结果与标准模型预测一致，未发现显著超出。在95%置信水平下，希格斯玻色子对产生截面上限设定为标准模型预测值的12.0倍，预期上限为18.5倍。结果同时用于约束希格斯玻色子的三重自耦合强度以及两个希格斯玻色子与两个矢量玻色子之间的四重耦合（quartic coupling）。

Conclusion: 本研究首次利用13.6 TeV对撞数据对希格斯玻色子对产生过程进行了搜索，结果与标准模型兼容。设定的截面上限为进一步研究希格斯玻色子自相互作用提供了重要约束，为未来更高统计量的分析奠定了基础。

Abstract: A search for Higgs boson pair production is presented, targeting final states where one Higgs boson decays to a pair of bottom quarks and the other Higgs boson decays to two W bosons, both of which decay leptonically, to an electron or a muon, and a neutrino. For the first time, the search is conducted with proton-proton collision data from the LHC at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13.6 TeV, recorded with the CMS detector in 2022 and 2023 and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 62 fb$^{-1}$. The results are consistent with the standard model predictions. An upper limit of 12.0 times the standard model prediction at 95% confidence level is set on the Higgs boson pair production cross section, with an expected limit of 18.5. The results are also used to constrain the strength of the trilinear self-coupling of the Higgs boson, as well as of the quartic coupling between two Higgs bosons and two vector bosons.

</details>


### [9] [A forward-angle large-acceptance magnetic spectrometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02136)
*B. Wojtsekhowski,G. Cates,E. Cisbani,M. Jones,G. Franklin,N. Liyanage,L. Pentchev,A. J. R. Puckett,R. Wines*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要建造一台适用于高亮度实验和前向散射角的大型固体角磁谱仪，以支持当前和未来的物理实验项目。

Method: 谱仪采用水平狭缝开口设计，允许束流线穿过谱仪磁铁轭铁；通过两层磁屏蔽系统减少狭缝内的残余磁场，外层由一组铁环构成；在偶极磁铁前后使用两个校正磁铁补偿轭铁外部的边缘场横向分量；采用重型配重确保靠近靶点的高大偶极磁铁的机械稳定性。

Result: 成功建造了一台具有70毫立体角接受度的大型固体角磁谱仪，该谱仪已用于多项物理实验，并有大量未来实验项目已获批准。

Conclusion: 该磁谱仪的设计和建造实现了高亮度、前向散射角实验的需求，其创新设计解决了束流线穿过磁铁、磁场屏蔽和机械稳定性等关键技术挑战。

Abstract: A large solid angle magnetic spectrometer for high luminosity and forward scattering angles was constructed at the Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility. A number of physics experiments have used this spectrometer, and a significant physics program of future experiments has already been approved. A key feature of the spectrometer concept is a horizontal slit opening that allows the beamline to pass through the yoke of the spectrometer magnet. This design enables a short distance between the target and spectrometer, resulting in a 70~msr solid angle acceptance. The residual magnetic-field on the beamline inside the slit is reduced by a two-layer magnetic shielding system, with the external layer comprising a set of iron rings. Two correcting magnets, before and after the dipole, were used to compensate for the transverse component of the fringe field outside of the dipole yoke. The mechanical stability of the tall dipole magnet in close proximity to the target was provided by means of a heavy counterweight.

In this work, we have developed a Q\&A application inspired by the Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG), which is comprised of an in-house database indexed on the arXiv articles related to the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) experiment - one of the largest international scientific collaboration and incorporated an open-source LLaMA model for answer generation. This is an extension to it's proceeding application built on proprietary model and Cloud-hosted external knowledge-base for the EIC experiment. This locally-deployed RAG-system offers a cost-effective, resource-constraint alternative solution to build a RAG-assisted Q\&A application on answering domain-specific queries in the field of experimental nuclear physics. This set-up facilitates data-privacy, avoids sending any pre-publication scientific data and information to public domain. Future improvement will expand the knowledge base to encompass heterogeneous EIC-related publications and reports and upgrade the application pipeline orchestration to the LangGraph framework.

### [11] [Thermodynamic connectivity reveals functional specialization and multiplex organization of extrasynaptic signaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02057)
*Giridhar Sunil,Habib Benali,Elkaïoum M. Moutuou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经通信同时涉及快速的突触传递和较慢的弥散性突触外信号，但两种模式如何共同组织大脑功能尚不清楚。研究旨在开发一个统一框架，将解剖连接与功能通信联系起来。

Method: 利用秀丽隐杆线虫的完整突触和神经肽连接组，开发统一的多层（multiplex）框架。从突触连接组推断结构衍生的功能连接性，使用统计物理学的平衡原理，生成跨所有突触通路的信息流概率图，并与突触外连接组直接比较。

Result: 揭示了四种原则性功能特化的通信机制：拓扑依赖层强化稳定突触运动回路；拓扑弹性调节层支持全局调控和行为状态控制；纯突触外网络维持生存和稳态；纯突触机制介导快速低延迟感觉运动处理。

Conclusion: 突触和突触外信号形成互补架构，分别优化速度、调节、鲁棒性和生存功能。该研究提供了整合结构和调节连接组的通用策略，以理解不同通信模式如何协同维持连贯的大脑功能。

Abstract: Neural communication operates on both fast synaptic transmission and slower, diffusive extrasynaptic signaling, yet how these two modes jointly organize brain function remains unclear. Here, using the complete synaptic and neuropeptidergic connectomes of \emph{Caenorhabditis elegans}, we develop a unified multiplex framework linking anatomical wiring to functional communication. We infer structure-derived functional connectivity from the synaptic connectome using equilibrium principles from statistical physics, yielding a probabilistic map of information flow across all synaptic pathways, and compare this functional layer directly with the extrasynaptic connectome. This reveals a principled functional specialization across four communication regimes: (i) a topology-dependent layer that reinforces and stabilizes synaptic motor circuits, (ii) a topology-resilient modulatory layer supporting global regulation and behavioral state control, (iii) a purely extrasynaptic network sustaining survival and homeostasis, and (iv) a purely synaptic regime mediating rapid, low-latency sensorimotor processing. Together, these findings reveal that synaptic and extrasynaptic signaling form complementary architectures optimized for speed, modulation, robustness, and survival, and provide a general strategy for integrating structural and modulatory connectomes to understand how distinct communication modes cooperate to sustain coherent brain function.

### [12] [Osmotically Induced Shape Changes in Membrane Vesicles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01435)
*Rajiv G Pereira,Biswaroop Mukherjee,Sanjeev Gautam,Mattiangelo D'Agnese,Subhadip Biswas,Rachel Meeker,Buddhapriya Chakrabarti*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个自洽的自由能框架，在有限储层中同时确定膜形状和渗透压，通过最小化弯曲弹性和溶质熵实现。该框架修正了球形囊泡的经典稳定性条件，临界压力与Helfrich预测相差数个数量级，并与实验模拟结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有膜力学模型通常将渗透压作为外部预设参数，忽略了溶质守恒对渗透压的热力学影响。该研究旨在建立膜形状与渗透压之间的非线性耦合框架，更准确地描述有限储层中的囊泡稳定性。

Method: 开发了一个自洽的自由能（free-energy）框架，通过最小化弯曲弹性（bending elasticity）和溶质熵（solute entropy）同时确定膜形状和渗透压。该框架将渗透压视为热力学变量而非外部参数，建立了膜力学与溶剂熵之间的非线性耦合。

Result: 该框架修正了球形囊泡的经典稳定性条件：不稳定性源于全局自由能竞争而非线性Helfrich稳定性判据（Helfrich stability criterion）。所得临界压力与Helfrich预测相差数个数量级，且与小单层囊泡（small unilamellar vesicles）和大单层囊泡（large unilamellar vesicles）的模拟结果一致。

Conclusion: 该自洽自由能框架适用于涉及生物分子凝聚物（biomolecular condensate）限制的细胞环境、合成囊泡以及渗透压驱动封装平台（osmotic-pressure-driven encapsulation platforms）的开发，为有限储层中的膜力学研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We develop a self-consistent free-energy framework in which membrane shape and osmotic pressure are determined simultaneously in a finite reservoir by minimizing bending elasticity and solute entropy. Solute conservation makes osmotic pressure a thermodynamic variable rather than an externally prescribed parameter, producing a nonlinear coupling between membrane mechanics and solvent entropy. This coupling modifies the classical stability condition for spherical vesicles: instability emerges from global free-energy competition rather than the linear Helfrich stability criterion. The resulting critical pressures differ by orders of magnitude from Helfrich predictions and agree with simulations for small and large unilamellar vesicles. The framework is relevant to cellular environments involving biomolecular condensate confinement as well as synthetic vesicles and the development of osmotic-pressure-driven encapsulation platforms.

### [13] [A Residence-Time Approach for Determining Position-Dependent Diffusivities from Biased Molecular Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01940)
*Rinto Thomas,Praveen Ranganath Prabhakar,Michael von Domaros*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于停留时间（residence-time approach, RTA）的新方法，用于从偏置分子动力学模拟中确定位置依赖的扩散系数（position-dependent diffusivities）。该方法在有效漂移可忽略的轨迹段中直接通过平均首次逃逸时间计算局部扩散系数，避免了传统波动方法所需的约束模拟或噪声时间相关函数积分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于波动（fluctuation-based）的方法需要专门的谐波约束模拟或对噪声时间相关函数进行数值积分，计算过程复杂且易受噪声影响。需要一种更直接、实用的方法来从偏置分子动力学模拟中提取位置依赖的扩散系数。

Method: 该方法基于停留时间方法（residence-time approach, RTA），在有效漂移（effective drift）可忽略的轨迹段中，通过平均首次逃逸时间（mean first-exit times）从有限空间区间直接获取局部扩散系数。该方法在自适应偏置力（adaptive biasing force）模拟中实现，无需专门的约束模拟或噪声时间相关函数积分。

Result: 在氧穿过十六烷板、水穿过脂质双层以及水和挥发性有机化合物穿过模型皮肤屏障膜等系统中评估了该方法。在板系统中，RTA在统计不确定度范围内重现了独立确定的体相扩散系数；在膜系统中，推断的扩散系数分布得到了传播子水平（propagator-level）验证的支持。

Conclusion: 停留时间方法（RTA）被确立为从偏置分子模拟中提取位置依赖扩散系数的实用方法，避免了传统方法的复杂性，并在多个生物物理系统中得到了验证。

Abstract: We introduce a residence-time approach (RTA) for determining position-dependent diffusivities from biased molecular dynamics simulations. The method is formulated for trajectory segments in which the effective drift along the transport coordinate is negligible, as realized here using adaptive biasing force simulations. In this regime, local diffusivities are obtained directly from mean first-exit times out of finite spatial intervals. Unlike conventional fluctuation-based approaches, the RTA does not require dedicated harmonically restrained simulations or numerical integration of noisy time-correlation functions. We assess the method for oxygen diffusion across a hexadecane slab, water permeation across a lipid bilayer, and permeation of water and selected volatile organic compounds through a model skin-barrier membrane. In the slab system, the RTA reproduces independently determined bulk diffusivities within statistical uncertainty. In the membrane systems, the inferred diffusivity profiles are supported by propagator-level validation. These results establish the RTA as a practical approach for extracting position-dependent diffusivities from biased molecular simulations.

</details>


### [14] [Gaussian closure and dynamical mean-field theory for self-avoiding heteropolymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02085)
*Andriy Goychuk*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种聚合物动力学的分析框架，通过动态平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）统一描述构象演化、接触概率和涨落，并预测了染色质等活性聚合物中的超压缩分形态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物动力学的分析处理大多局限于基于微扰场论的线性响应理论。本文旨在超越这一限制，建立能够统一描述构象演化、接触概率和涨落的分析框架。

Method: 从流体力学耦合且自回避的杂聚物（heteropolymer）的朗之万方程（Langevin equation）出发，以两点关联函数（two-point correlator）作为最低阶相关可观测量。通过高斯闭合（Gaussian closure）截断高阶关联，得到链关联的自洽扩散方程（self-consistent diffusion equation）。

Result: 该理论在单一动力学框架内验证了卷曲、球状和自回避聚合物（self-avoiding polymers）的行为，并预测了流体力学耦合活性聚合物（如染色质）中的超压缩分形态（hyper-compacted fractal states）。

Conclusion: 本文发展的动态平均场理论为聚合物动力学提供了超越线性响应的统一分析框架，能够描述复杂聚合物系统的构象演化和涨落行为，特别适用于染色质等活性聚合物系统。

Abstract: Analytical treatments of polymer dynamics have mostly been restricted to linear response theory around some steady state obtained via perturbative field theory. Here, I derive an analytical framework that yields unified access to the evolution of conformations, contact probabilities, and fluctuations within a dynamical mean-field theory. Starting with the Langevin equation of a hydrodynamically coupled and self-avoiding heteropolymer, the key idea is to focus on the two-point correlator as the lowest-order relevant observable. Truncating higher-order correlations via a Gaussian closure leads to a self-consistent diffusion equation for the chain correlations. The theory is validated by contrasting coiled, globular, and self-avoiding polymers within a single dynamical framework, and predicts hyper-compacted fractal states in hydrodynamically coupled active polymers such as chromatin.

</details>


### [15] [The "Intensity" Countoscope: Measuring particle dynamics in real space from microscopy images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02271)
*Sophie Hermann,Seyed Saman Banarooei,Adam Carter,Carlos A. Silvera Batista,Sophie Marbach*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于显微图像强度波动分析的新方法，通过分析不同尺寸虚拟观测框中的强度变化，揭示粒子扩散动力学特征，可直接从图像强度提取扩散系数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于强度的显微技术（intensity-based microscopy techniques）虽能量化微观尺度粒子运动，但现有方法在分析粒子扩散和集体动力学方面仍有局限。需要发展能够直接从图像强度提取物理信息的新方法，特别是在无法分辨单个粒子的系统中。

Method: 提出一种新颖的实空间（real-space）分析方法，在显微图像上设置可变尺寸的虚拟观测框（virtual observation boxes），分析框内强度波动信号。通过关联这些信号，研究强度均方变化$\langle ΔI^2(t) \rangle$的时间依赖性，并建立理论框架解释观测结果。

Result: 发现$\langle ΔI^2(t) \rangle$呈现明显的时间区域依赖性：小观测框或短时间尺度下，$\langle ΔI^2(t) \rangle$与均方位移（mean-square displacement）成比例；长时间尺度或大观测框下，则与其平方根成比例。在稀胶体悬浮液（dilute colloidal suspension）的共聚焦显微成像（confocal microscopy）实验中验证了该框架。

Conclusion: 该方法为基于强度的实空间分析提供了补充工具，能够直接从图像强度稳健地提取扩散系数（diffusion coefficients）并获得粒子动力学物理洞察，即使在无法分辨单个粒子的系统中也能研究个体和潜在集体行为。

Abstract: Advances in intensity-based microscopy techniques have improved our ability to quantify particle motion at microscopic scales, enabling insight into diffusion and collective dynamics. Building on this foundation, we introduce a novel real-space approach that analyses intensity fluctuations within virtual observation boxes of variable size on microscopy images. By correlating these signals, we uncover distinct temporal regimes in the mean square changes of intensity, $\langle ΔI^2(t) \rangle$, which are strongly dependent on the box size compared to the particle width. For small boxes or short timescales, $\langle ΔI^2(t) \rangle$ scales with the mean-square displacement, while for longer timescales and larger boxes, it scales with its square root. We develop a general theoretical framework that captures these regimes and explicitly apply it to a dilute colloidal suspension imaged with confocal microscopy as an experimental model system. This allows for a robust extraction of diffusion coefficients and physical insights into particle dynamics. Our method complements intensity-based and real-space analysis, offering a tool for studying individual and potentially collective behaviour directly from image intensities, even in systems where individual particles cannot be resolved.

</details>

### [16] [Plummer Dark Matter Black Hole with Topological Defects: Shadow, Greybody Factors, Quasinormal Modes, and Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01255)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Faizuddin Ahmed,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在带核的Plummer暗物质晕和Letelier弦云中构建了一个静态球对称黑洞解，系统分析了其几何结构、光子轨道、弱偏折角、标量扰动、热力学性质，发现弦云张力参数α主导所有可观测量的主要修正，而Plummer晕密度ρ₀提供次要的附加修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究在cored Plummer暗物质晕和Letelier弦云共同影响下的黑洞物理性质，探索这两种物质成分对黑洞几何、动力学和热力学行为的相对贡献。

Method: 从Plummer-Schwarzschild度规出发，引入弦云张力参数α到流逝函数中，获得新的时空解；随后系统分析事件视界、光子球、弱偏折角（通过Gauss-Bonnet定理）、最内稳定圆轨道、标量扰动（包括有效势、灰体因子界限、Hawking发射谱和准正规模频率）以及热力学性质。

Result: 当α<1时存在单一非简并事件视界，α≥1时出现裸奇点；热容量对所有参数值均为严格负值，排除了Davies型相变；所有六项分析均显示一致的分层结构：弦云张力α主导各可观测量的主要修正，Plummer晕密度ρ₀提供次要的附加修正。

Conclusion: 在cored Plummer暗物质晕和Letelier弦云共同影响下的黑洞系统中，弦云张力参数α是决定黑洞物理性质的主导因素，而暗物质晕密度仅提供次要修正，这为理解不同物质成分对黑洞行为的相对重要性提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We construct a static, spherically symmetric black hole (BH) solution embedded in a cored Plummer dark matter (DM) halo and a Letelier cloud of strings (CoS). Starting from the Plummer-Schwarzschild metric of Senjaya et al.~\cite{Senjaya2026}, we incorporate the string-cloud tension parameter $α$ into the lapse function, obtaining $A(r) = h_{\rm Plummer}(r) - α$. The resulting spacetime admits a single, non-degenerate event horizon (EH) for $α< 1$ and a naked singularity for $α\ge 1$. We determine the photon sphere (PS) and BH shadow radii, compute the weak deflection angle via the Gauss-Bonnet theorem (GBT), and analyze the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). Scalar perturbations are studied through the effective potential, greybody factor (GF) bounds obtained from the Boonserm-Visser method, the Hawking emission spectrum, and quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies computed with the WKB approximation. The thermodynamic analysis covers the Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy; the heat capacity is found to be strictly negative for all parameter values, confirming the absence of any Davies-type phase transition. A consistent hierarchy emerges across all six analyses: the CoS tension $α$ governs the leading-order modifications to every observable, while the Plummer halo density $ρ_0$ provides a subdominant, additive correction.

</details>


### [17] [A framework for creating galaxy models in the geometry of the conservation group with dark matter halos and flat rotation curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01270)
*Edward Lee Green*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Pandres理论通过引入正交标架场（orthonormal tetrads）和守恒群（conservation group）扩展了四维时空的几何结构。该理论在弱场近似下预测引力波以光速传播，并通过球对称解建立了包含重子物质、暗物质和外部区域的三区域星系模型，能够解释平坦的旋转曲线（flat rotation curves）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过扩展时空的几何结构来发展新的引力理论。Pandres理论通过引入具有扩大协变群的正交标架场，将微分同胚群（diffeomorphisms）作为其真子群包含在内，从而构建更一般的理论框架。

Method: 方法基于Pandres的几何理论，其自由场拉格朗日密度（free-field Lagrangian density）仅涉及曲率矢量（curvature vector）。当存在大质量物体时，在拉格朗日密度中添加源项（source term）。研究采用弱场近似（weak-field approximation）并寻找球对称解（spherically symmetric solutions）。

Result: 弱场近似表明引力波以光速传播。研究发现自由场情况下的场方程需要非零的应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensors），但可接受的模型必须在拉格朗日量中包含源项。通过将星系划分为三个球对称区域：重子物质主导的中心隆起（baryonic matter-dominated central bulge）、暗物质主导的中层（dark matter-dominated mesosphere）和两者均不主导的外部区域，建立了连续的三区域模型。

Conclusion: 通过等温条件（isothermal condition）建立了中层模型，该模型暗示了具有一个自由参数的平坦旋转曲线。结合径向加速度关系（radial acceleration relation），该理论框架能够为旋转支撑星系（rotationally supported galaxy）建立完整的星系模型。

Abstract: Pandres has developed a theory which extends the geometrical structure of a real four-dimensional space-time via a field of orthonormal tetrads with an enlarged covariance group. This new group, called the conservation group, contains the group of diffeomorphisms as a proper subgroup. The free-field Lagrangian density involves only the curvature vector which is a vector which measures curvature. When massive objects are present a source term is added to this Lagrangian density. The weak-field approximation implies that gravitational waves travel at the speed of light. Spherically symmetric solutions for both the free field and the field with sources are found. In the free-field case, the field equations require nonzero stress-energy tensors. However, we find that for our model to be an acceptable model, we must have a source term in the Lagrangian. In our framework, we divide up the galaxy into three spherically symmetric regions: a baryonic matter-dominated central bulge, a dark matter-dominated mesosphere and an outside region where neither type dominates. Assuming the density of baryonic matter has a central cusp, we show how to model the bulge. Via an isothermal condition we find a model for the mesosphere and show this model implies flat rotation curves with one free parameter. The outside region is readily modeled via previously published results. The models for the bulge, mesosphere and outside region are combined into one continuous model. Using the radial acceleration relation we then show how a galaxy model may be set up for a rotationally supported galaxy.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙结构的起源通常被认为是量子的，但现今宇宙呈现经典特性。传统观点将此归因于暴胀期间超视界尺度上的"量子-经典"转变，但作者质疑这些机制是否总是充分的，需要重新审视该问题并识别传统论证中的假设和局限性。

Method: 论文采用相空间分析方法，基于维格纳函数（Wigner function）作为具体途径来识别和探测量子特征。该方法旨在超越传统的慢滚（slow roll）近似，考虑宇宙扰动的非线性动力学效应。

Result: 研究发现，在慢滚之外的情况下，宇宙扰动的非线性动力学可以产生非经典特征，这些特征可能在可观测量中存活。这提出了量子特征可能在宇宙结构中持续存在的可能性，挑战了传统关于量子-经典转变完全性的假设。

Conclusion: 论文结论指出，宇宙结构中的量子-经典转变可能并非总是完全的，非线性动力学可能允许量子特征在可观测量中持续存在。基于维格纳函数的相空间分析为探测这些量子特征提供了具体的研究方向。

Abstract: The origin of cosmic structure is widely regarded as quantum, yet the Universe today appears classical. Standard lore attributes this to a "quantum-to-classical" transition on super-horizon scales during inflation. Gravity plays a central role: super-horizon dynamics squeeze quantum states, while the cosmological horizon enforces a system-environment split, leading to decoherence. But are these mechanisms always sufficient? We revisit this question, identifying assumptions and limitations in conventional arguments. We highlight recent work showing that beyond slow roll, non-linear dynamics of cosmological perturbations can generate non-classical features that may survive in observables. This raises the tantalizing possibility that quantum signatures may persist in cosmic structure. We propose a phase-space analysis based on the Wigner function as a concrete route to identifying and probing such signatures.

### [19] [Corrected Hawking Temperature and Final State of Black Hole Evaporation Under GEVAG Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01286)

Method: 采用GEVAG（广义熵变G）框架，将有效引力常数（$G_\text{eff}$）推广到视界邻域，推导出包含两项修正的霍金温度表达式。特别关注熵的对数修正（logarithmic correction）情况，并与广义不确定原理（GUP）结果进行比较。

Abstract: In the GEVAG (Generalized Entropy Varying-G) framework, any generalization to horizon entropy leads to a varying gravitational "constant" $G_\text{eff}$ that is a function the horizon area. In this work, it is shown that if we promote $G_\text{eff}$ to be valid in the neighborhood of the horizon, then Hawking temperature consists of two terms, the second of which is related to the variation of $G_\text{eff}$. When applied to the logarithmic correction of the entropy, as is common across various quantum gravity approaches, the first term in the Schwarzschild black hole temperature exactly agrees with that obtained from utilizing generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), while the second term improves on the GUP result by driving the Hawking temperature to zero as the black hole approaches a minimum mass. This resolves the inconsistency in the GUP result concerning a nonzero temperature minimum mass remnant. This work also derives simple general formulas for both the thermodynamic energy and the Bekenstein bound for any correction to the area law under the same assumption that $G_\text{eff}$ can be extended off-shell in the horizon neighborhood. The (generalized) Bekenstein bound can be interpreted as a statement regarding the renormalization group scaling dimension of the entropy functional $f(A)$ and the naturalness of the theory.

Abstract: The Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for a massless fluid take the form of a pair of coupled autonomous first order differential equations, which can be employed in a model for a ``dynamical gravastar'' black hole mimicker. The mimicker has no true horizon, but rather a ``simulated horizon'', outside which the geometry resembles a Schwarzschild black hole, but inside which the $g_{00}$ component of the metric is always positive and becomes exponentially small. Collins has reinterpreted the relevant TOV equations in terms of a two-dimensional flow with a spiral form, and Zöllner and Kämpfer have mapped the simulated horizon to a specific segment of the Collins spiral. We give here results of an asymptotic analysis, relating initial values at the small radius end of this spiral segment to the black hole mimicker mass and other parameters that emerge at the large radius kink in the TOV solution, which corresponds to the simulated horizon.

### [21] [High-frequency gravitational wave transients from superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01407)
*Henry Su,Lucas Brown,Christopher Ewasiuk,Stefano Profumo*

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了超轻玻色子围绕旋转黑洞形成的引力原子云产生的引力波辐射，包括孤立系统和双星扰动系统两种情况，并评估了其在当前实验条件下的可探测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻玻色子（ultralight bosons）可通过超辐射（superradiance）在旋转黑洞周围形成宏观引力原子云（gravitational-atom clouds），产生准单色引力波。原初黑洞（primordial black holes）为此类系统提供了天然环境，其频率范围与谐振腔实验相关。

Method: 论文对孤立系统和双星扰动引力原子云的引力波辐射进行了统一处理。对于孤立系统，推导了跃迁（transition）和湮灭（annihilation）通道在时域和频域的应变解析表达式。对于双星系统，采用朗道-齐纳形式（Landau--Zener formalism）模拟共振驱动的能级跃迁，并计算相应的瞬态信号。

Result: 研究发现，双星驱动的跃迁产生的信号持续时间与探测器响应时间兼容，但其特征应变远低于当前实验在合理天体物理距离下的灵敏度。事件发生率因需要源处于不现实的小间距而进一步抑制了可探测性。论文量化了使这些信号可观测所需的灵敏度、带宽和响应改进。

Conclusion: 原初黑洞周围的引力原子系统是未来高频引力波搜索的理论上有充分动机的目标。尽管当前实验难以探测双星扰动系统的信号，但通过改进灵敏度、带宽和响应，这些信号有望在未来被观测到。

Abstract: Ultralight bosons can form macroscopic gravitational-atom clouds around rotating black holes via superradiance, sourcing quasi-monochromatic gravitational waves through level transitions and annihilation. Primordial black holes provide a natural setting for such systems in a frequency range relevant for resonant-cavity experiments. We present a unified treatment of gravitational-wave emission from both isolated and binary-perturbed gravitational atoms in this regime. For isolated systems, we derive analytic expressions for the time- and frequency-domain strain from transition and annihilation channels, emphasizing their narrow-band structure. For binaries, we model resonantly driven level transitions using the Landau--Zener formalism and compute the resulting transient signals. We find that, while binary-driven transitions generically yield signals with durations compatible with detector response times, their characteristic strain lies well below the sensitivity of current experiments at astrophysically plausible distances, and event rates further suppress detectability by requiring sources at unrealistically small separations. We quantify the improvements in sensitivity, bandwidth, and response needed to render these signals observable, and identify gravitational-atom systems around primordial black holes as a theoretically well-motivated target for future high-frequency gravitational-wave searches.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We explore the connection between black hole shadows, thermodynamic phase structure, and microstructure of charged and rotating black holes within General Relativity and Geometrothermodynamics. Focusing on Reissner-Nordström and Kerr solutions, we establish a criterion to select the most suitable Geometrothermodynamic metric for a system, revealing that the first metric from enthalpy and the second from mass correctly reproduce heat capacity singularities. We show that the shadow radius encodes the same phase information as entropy and introduce Shadow-Microstructure diagrams to extract insights into stability and microscopic interaction types directly from observational bounds. Applying this framework to Sagittarius A*, we constrain the macroscopic parameters and the allowed microscopic thermodynamic phases. Our findings indicate that shadow measurements offer a novel probe of thermodynamic and microscopic aspects of black holes, enabling tests of alternative theories of gravity and thermodynamic frameworks.

### [23] [Geometric origin of the cosmological constant from Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity compactified to four dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01536)
*M. Cataldo,S. Lepe,C. Riquelme,P. Salgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出一个模型，其中宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）作为纯几何效应从五维爱因斯坦-陈-西蒙斯（Einstein-Chern-Simons）引力的四维紧致化中涌现。该模型通过额外维度的紧致化产生有效宇宙学常数Λ，而非将其作为自由参数引入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是提供宇宙学常数问题的几何重构框架。传统方法将Λ作为自由参数引入，而本文旨在从更高维引力理论的紧致化中自然地推导出Λ，从而重新表述宇宙学常数问题。

Method: 方法基于五维爱因斯坦-陈-西蒙斯引力的四维紧致化。通过紧致额外维度，从紧致化半径r_c、耦合参数l和紧致场h^a的迹˜h推导出有效宇宙学常数Λ，而非将其作为自由参数引入。

Result: 研究识别了两个动力学区域：弱场区域Λ∝l²˜h/r_c³，其符号由l²˜h控制；强场区域Λ≈3/(4r_c²)，与陈-西蒙斯耦合无关。强场区域自然地再现观测值Λ_obs，对应r_c≈0.78H₀⁻¹≈8.2×10²⁵m，无需精细调节。

Conclusion: 该框架几何地重构了宇宙学常数问题：从询问"为什么Λ很小"转变为询问"为什么r_c很大"。这种重新表述与大型额外维度兼容，且不违反已建立的引力测试，为宇宙学常数问题提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: We present a model in which the cosmological constant emerges as a purely geometric effect from the four-dimensional compactification of five-dimensional Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity. The compactification of the extra dimension generates an effective cosmological constant $Λ$ depending on the compactification radius $r_c$, the coupling parameter $l$, and the trace $\tilde{h}$ of the compactified field $h^a$, rather than being introduced as a free parameter. The resulting field equations are structurally equivalent to those of General Relativity with a cosmological constant, so all known vacuum solutions -- Schwarzschild--de Sitter, Kerr--de Sitter, and FLRW spacetimes -- remain valid. As a concrete application, we derive the Kottler (Schwarzschild--de Sitter) black hole solution.
  We identify two dynamical regimes. In the weak-field regime, $Λ\propto l^{2}\tilde{h}/r_{c}^{3}$, whose sign is controlled by $l^2\tilde{h}$, requiring fine-tuning to reproduce $Λ_{\text{obs}} \approx 10^{-52}\,\text{m}^{-2}$. In the strong-field regime, dependence on $l$ and $\tilde{h}$ cancels algebraically, yielding $Λ\approx 3/(4r_{c}^{2})$ independently of the Chern-Simons coupling. This regime naturally reproduces $Λ_{\rm obs}$ for $r_{c} \approx 0.78\,H_{0}^{-1} \approx 8.2 \times 10^{25}\,\text{m}$, without fine-tuning. The Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of the cosmological horizon gives $S_{\rm cosm} = 4πk_B r_c^2/l_{\rm Pl}^2 \sim 10^{122}\,k_B$, consistent with the Gibbons-Hawking result and admitting a direct geometric interpretation in terms of $r_c$. This framework geometrically reframes the cosmological constant problem: rather than asking why $Λ$ is small, one asks why $r_c$ is large -- a reformulation compatible with a large extra dimension without violating established gravitational tests.

</details>


### [24] [Nonperturbative suppression of beyond-General-Relativity effects in quadratic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01631)
*Georgios Antoniou,Leonardo Gualtieri,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 二次引力理论（quadratic gravity）中，点粒子坠入史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）产生的引力波辐射与广义相对论（GR）的观测偏差在GR极限下呈指数级抑制，这非微扰地实现了有效场论框架预测的两种理论等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次引力理论是广义相对论（GR）的一个有物理动机的扩展，其在爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）基础上增加了二次曲率项。该理论与GR在有效场论（effective-field-theory）框架下等价，但在非微扰（non-perturbative）层面存在差异。

Method: 通过研究点粒子（point particles）坠入二次引力理论中的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）所产生的引力波辐射（gravitational-wave emission），分析其与广义相对论预测的偏差。

Result: 观测到的与广义相对论的偏差在GR极限下呈指数级抑制（exponentially suppressed）。这一发现提供了二次引力理论与GR在有效场论框架下预测的等价性的非微扰实现（nonperturbative realization）。

Conclusion: 研究证实了二次引力理论与广义相对论在有效场论框架下的等价性，即使在非微扰层面，观测偏差也会在GR极限下被指数级抑制，支持了两种理论在物理可观测性上的高度一致性。

Abstract: Quadratic gravity is a well-motivated extension of general relativity~(GR) wherein the Einstein-Hilbert action is augmented by quadratic curvature terms. This theory is equivalent to GR in an effective-field-theory framework, while the two theories are different at the non-perturbative level. As we have recently shown, black holes in quadratic gravity have a rich linear response, including extra scalar, vector, and tensor quasinormal modes that can be excited in physical processes, even when the stationary solution is the same as in GR. Here, by studying the gravitational-wave emission from point particles plunging into a Schwarzschild black hole in quadratic gravity, we show that observable deviations from GR are exponentially suppressed in the GR limit. This provides a nonperturbative realization of the equivalence between quadratic gravity and GR predicted in the effective-field-theory framework.

</details>

At this level the presence of a radiation-reaction force manifests, modifying the fall with a corresponding bremsstrahlung radiation. We evaluate then all emissions: energy, angular momentum (vanishing identically) and linear momentum. ### [26] [Interior geometry of black holes as a probe of first-order phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01818)
*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Zhang-Yu Nie,Shao-Wen Wei,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出黑洞奇点附近的几何结构可作为探测相变的新诊断工具，发现标量化AdS黑洞的一级相变会导致Kasner指数$p_t$在温度变化时呈现振荡或平滑两种截然不同的行为，并在超临界区域形成独立的"Kasner交叉线"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统黑洞相变诊断依赖于事件视界或渐近边界的热力学量，本文旨在探索奇点附近几何结构能否提供独立、敏锐的相变探针，揭示宏观热力学状态变化如何根本性地重塑时空最深处的内部结构。

Method: 通过分析标量化AdS黑洞（scalarized AdS black holes）在奇点附近的几何特性，研究表征趋近奇点的Kasner指数$p_t$随温度的变化行为，特别关注一级相变（first-order phase transition）和超临界交叉（supercritical crossover）区域。

Result: 在一级相变的一侧，$p_t$随温度强烈振荡，反映剧烈的内部动力学；在另一侧则变为平滑单调函数。两种行为在临界点附近收敛。超临界区域中，$p_t(T)$形成独特极值点，定义了完全独立于传统热力学（Widom线）或动力学（Frenkel线）标准的"Kasner交叉线"。

Conclusion: 黑洞奇点可作为相变诊断的新类别，宏观热力学状态的改变会根本性地重塑时空最深处的内部结构，奇点附近几何提供了独立于传统方法的相变探针。

Abstract: Traditional diagnostics of black hole phase transitions rely on thermodynamic quantities defined at the event horizon or asymptotic boundary. Here, we demonstrate that the near-singularity geometry offers a sharp, independent probe of both first-order phase transitions and supercritical crossover. For scalarized AdS black holes exhibiting a first-order phase transition, the Kasner exponent $p_t$, which characterizes the approach to the singularity, undergoes a dramatic transformation. On one side of the transition, $p_t$ oscillates strongly with temperature, reflecting violent interior dynamics. On the other side, it becomes a smooth, monotonically varying function. These two distinct behaviors converge as the critical point is approached. Beyond the critical point, in the supercritical region, $p_t(T)$ develops a distinct extremum, defining a ''Kasner crossover line'' that is entirely independent of traditional thermodynamic (Widom line) or dynamic (Frenkel line) criteria. Our work establishes the black hole singularity as a novel class of diagnostics for phase transitions, revealing that a change in the macroscopic thermodynamic state fundamentally reshapes the deepest interior structure of spacetime.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于自适应网络相干分析的无监督缓解框架，选择性抑制局部伪迹同时保留全局潜在天体物理信号。使用Advanced LIGO O3数据进行验证，分析1、3、5天积分时间的清理性能。

Result: 对于5天数据集，该流程识别并缓解了汉福德和利文斯顿探测器中总谱线的89%和77%，同时有效保留了与天体物理形态一致的相干群体。在20Hz至2000Hz的分析带宽中修改少于7%。

Abstract: The sensitivity of continuous gravitational-wave searches is strictly limited by non-Gaussian spectral artefacts that accumulate coherent power over long observation baselines. In this paper, we present an unsupervised mitigation framework based on adaptive network coherence analysis. Unlike traditional veto methods that discard entire frequency bands, our pipeline selectively suppresses local artefacts while preserving global potentially astrophysical signals. We validate the method using Advanced LIGO O3 data, analysing the cleaning performance across integration times of 1, 3, and 5 days. For the 5-day dataset, the pipeline identifies and mitigates 89\% and 77\% of the total spectral lines in the Hanford and Livingston detectors, respectively, while effectively preserving the coherent population consistent with astrophysical morphologies. This is achieved while modifying less than 7\% of the analysis bandwidth spanning 20~Hz to 2000~Hz. Rigorous statistical verification demonstrates that the mitigation effectively suppresses the non-Gaussian tail of the noise distribution while strictly preserving the statistical integrity of coherent signal candidates. By recovering detector sensitivity in parameter spaces previously contaminated by the spectral forest, this framework provides a robust preprocessing strategy for all-sky searches.

### [28] [Case studies with GPBilby of glitch-contaminated transient gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02018)
*Mattia Emma,Ann-Kristin Malz,Adriana Dias,Gregory Ashton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍了使用GPBilby参数估计工具进行引力波数据分析的案例研究，该工具通过高斯过程（Gaussian process）联合建模天体物理信号和非高斯噪声，能够有效处理瞬态噪声干扰（glitches）并评估波形建模系统误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA引力波观测站在第四次观测运行中发现了数百个新信号，但许多信号受到非高斯瞬态噪声干扰（glitches）的污染。这些干扰若不处理，会偏差参数推断并导致误导性的天体物理结论。

Method: 研究使用GPBilby参数估计工具，该工具采用时域似然函数联合建模：使用物理波形建模天体物理信号，同时使用高斯过程（Gaussian process）建模非高斯噪声。研究通过多个案例进行分析，包括使用IMRPhenomXPHM和NRSur7dq4等波形模型。

Result: 对于GW231123（迄今观测到的最高质量双黑洞候选体），使用IMRPhenomXPHM分析显示存在相干残差结构，导致推断源参数发生可测量偏移；而使用NRSur7dq4分析则未显示显著过量残差功率。对于GW191109，自旋错位证据在双LIGO探测器存在glitches的情况下保持稳健。对于GW230630_070659，数据与双黑洞波形模型一致，高斯过程分量未识别出额外残差功率。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明GPBilby可用于执行glitch-稳健推断，并作为理解波形建模系统误差的工具。研究同时揭示了波形系统误差与灵活噪声建模之间存在内在耦合，因为高斯过程项可以部分吸收相干波形失配。

Abstract: In their fourth observing run, the LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA gravitational-wave observatories have found hundreds of new signals, but many are contaminated by non-Gaussian transient noise artefacts known as glitches. Left unaddressed, glitches can bias parameter inference and lead to misleading astrophysical conclusions. We present a series of case studies using GPBilby, a parameter estimation tool that employs a time-domain likelihood jointly modelling the astrophysical signal with a physical waveform and non-Gaussian noise with a Gaussian process. We first show that when the detector noise is Gaussian, GPBilby produces results consistent with those obtained with the standard Gaussian-noise likelihood, and then consider events affected by non-Gaussian features. For GW231123, the highest-mass binary black hole candidate observed to date, analyses using IMRPhenomXPHM reveal coherent residual structure that leads to measurable shifts in inferred source parameters. In contrast, analyses employing NRSur7dq4 show no significant excess residual power and remain consistent across likelihood choices. This demonstrates that waveform systematics and flexible noise modelling are intrinsically coupled, as the Gaussian process terms can partially absorb coherent waveform mismatches. For GW191109, we find that evidence for spin misalignment remains robust despite glitches in both LIGO detectors. For GW230630_070659, excluded from GWTC-4.0 owing to poor data quality, we find the data to be consistent with a BBH waveform model, with no additional residual power identified by the Gaussian process component. Overall, these results highlight how GPBilby can be used to perform glitch-robust inference and as a tool to understand waveform modelling systematics.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究揭示了引力波极化模式与运动学张量之间的具体对应关系：剪切张量的横向分量对应横向张量极化模式；膨胀对应横向标量和纵向极化模式；剪切和涡度的纵向-横向分量对应矢量极化模式。这些关系为解释极化模式提供了基于运动学张量的新视角。

Conclusion: 该研究从理论角度提供了通过运动学张量解释引力波极化模式的新见解。将运动学张量纳入引力波研究可能为其现象学提供新的研究视角，建立了引力波观测特征与基础运动学量之间的理论联系。

Abstract: Relations between the kinematical tensors (the expansion, the shear, and the vorticity) and the polarization modes of gravitational waves are studied within the context of metric theories of gravity by considering freely falling test particles. After analyzing exact relations, we consider slowly moving particles under the influence of a weak gravitational field. Linearized plane waves of theories representative of those determined by a general second-order Lagrangian, including General Relativity, are shown to exemplify the following interconnections: between the transverse components of the shear and the transverse tensor polarization mode; between the expansion, and both the transverse scalar and the longitudinal polarization modes; and between the longitudinal-transverse components of both the shear and the vorticity, and the vector polarization mode. These relations, from the theoretical point of view, offer a novel insight into the interpretation of the polarization modes in terms of the kinematical tensors. Additionally, the inclusion of the kinematical tensors in the study of gravitational waves might provide a new outlook on their phenomenology.

### [30] [Asymptotic Symmetries of the Holst Action at Spatial Infinity: Including Supertranslations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02052)
*Sepideh Bakhoda,Hongguang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究在空间无穷远处基于Holst作用量的广义相对论渐近对称性分析中，提出了允许完整BMS群（包括非平凡超平移）的边界条件，解决了对数发散问题，并证明了Holst项对洛伦兹荷有贡献但保持超平移荷不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索广义相对论在空间无穷远处的渐近对称性，特别是在Holst作用量的一阶形式主义框架下。传统处理通常会消除非平凡超平移（supertranslations），本研究旨在建立允许完整BMS群（Bondi-Metzner-Sachs group）的边界条件。

Method: 采用协变相空间方法（covariant phase space method），为余标架（co-tetrad）和洛伦兹联络（Lorentz connection）提出了一套松弛边界条件。通过施加特定的对称性保持宇称条件来消除辛结构中的对数发散，并使用补偿性内部洛伦兹规范变换来正则化线性发散。

Result: 研究结果表明，Holst项由于洛伦兹生成元的线性增长而对荷变分有非平凡贡献。虽然Holst修正会改变与洛伦兹推动（boosts）和旋转相关的荷，但超平移荷保持完全不变。最终获得的荷是有限且可积的。

Conclusion: 该框架为在空间无穷远处使用Ashtekar-Barbero变量推导完整BMS代数提供了自洽方案，为Immirzi参数在经典和量子引力中的作用提供了新见解。成功解决了发散问题并保持了超平移对称性。

Abstract: We investigate the asymptotic symmetries of General Relativity at spatial infinity within the first-order formalism described by the Holst action. Employing the covariant phase space method, we propose a set of relaxed boundary conditions for the co-tetrad and Lorentz connection that admit the full Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) group, including non-trivial supertranslations, which are typically eliminated in standard treatments. We demonstrate that the logarithmic divergences appearing in the symplectic structure can be removed by imposing specific, symmetry-preserving parity conditions on the asymptotic fields without suppressing the supertranslation sector. A detailed analysis of the conserved charges reveals that the Holst term contributes non-trivially to the charge variations due to the linear growth of Lorentz generators. We show that the naive surface integrals for the Holst charges exhibit linear divergences arising from the rotation of the background tetrad. These divergences are successfully regularized by supplementing the asymptotic symmetry generator with a compensating internal Lorentz gauge transformation defined to preserve the background structure. The resulting charges are manifestly finite and integrable. Crucially, we prove that while the Holst modification shifts the charges associated with Lorentz boosts and rotations, it leaves the supertranslation charges identically invariant. This framework provides a consistent derivation of the full BMS algebra at spatial infinity in terms of Ashtekar-Barbero variables, offering new insights into the role of the Immirzi parameter in classical and quantum gravity.

### [31] [Massive scalar field perturbations in noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02066)
*Wen-Hao Bian,Zhu-Fang Cui*

Main category: gr-qc

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究非对易几何启发的史瓦西黑洞在质量标量场扰动下的动力学行为，特别是准正则模频率、灰体因子和吸收截面的特性，为黑洞微扰动力学提供理论依据。

Method: 采用三阶WKB近似方法（third-order WKB approximation approach）系统计算非对易几何启发的史瓦西黑洞在质量标量场（massive scalar field）扰动下的准正则模频率、灰体因子和吸收截面。

Result: 准正则模频率的虚部满足Im(ω)<0，证实了黑洞在扰动下的稳定性。非对易参数θ增加会降低频率实部和虚部的绝对值，而质量μ增加会提高实部并降低虚部。灰体因子和吸收截面随θ增加而增加，随μ增加而减少。

Conclusion: 非对易参数θ和质量μ对黑洞动力学特性具有相反的调制效应。在角量子数ℓ=1和大质量μ条件下，极端黑洞的准正则模频率趋近于经典史瓦西黑洞的相应值，表明质量和非对易几何量子修正效应在一定程度上相互抵消。

Abstract: In this paper, based on noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole, we employ a third-order WKB approximation approach to systematically calculate the quasinormal mode frequencies (QNFs), greybody factors (GFs), and absorption cross section (ACS) under massive scalar field perturbations. The results show that the QNFs satisfy Im($ω$)<0, confirming the stability of the black hole under perturbations. Furthermore, increasing the noncommutative parameter $θ$ reduces the absolute values of both the real and imaginary parts of the frequency, while increasing mass $μ$ increases the real part and reduces the imaginary part. The GFs and ACS increase with increasing $θ$ and decrease with increasing $μ$, indicating opposite modulation effects of these two types of parameters. It is worth emphasizing that the QNFs of the extreme black hole approach the corresponding values of the classical Schwarzschild black hole at angular quantum number $\ell=1$ and large $μ$, suggesting that, the effects of mass and noncommutative geometry quantum corrections cancel each other out to some extent. It is hoped that these results provide a viable theoretical basis for both the theoretical and experimental aspects of the perturbative dynamics of black hole.

### [32] [Emergence of volume-law scaling for entanglement negativity from the Hawking radiation of analogue black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02075)
*S. Mahesh Chandran,Uwe R. Fischer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格正则化方法，首次证明了霍金辐射（Hawking radiation）在1+1维模拟黑洞背景下，对数负性（logarithmic negativity）会获得一个紫外有限（UV-finite）的体积项，该体积项编码了纠缠霍金对（entangled Hawking pairs）的数量密度和空间分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 霍金辐射的量子信息内容对于理解黑洞蒸发和幺正性（unitarity）的命运至关重要。受冷原子实验（cold-atom experiments）最新进展的启发，本研究旨在模拟量子场在1+1维模拟黑洞（analogue black-hole）背景下的粗粒化纠缠标度行为。

Method: 研究开发了一种晶格正则化方法（lattice-regularization approach），用于模拟量子场在1+1维模拟黑洞背景下的粗粒化纠缠标度（coarse-grained entanglement scaling）。该方法特别关注对数负性这一纠缠单调（entanglement monotone）。

Result: 首次具体证明了对数负性——这一通常在共形真空（conformal vacuum）中表现出紫外发散对数标度（UV-divergent log-scaling）的纠缠单调——会从霍金辐射播种的非局域关联中获得一个紫外有限的体积项（UV-finite volume term）。该体积项编码了纠缠霍金对沿黑洞内部和外部的数量密度和空间分布。

Conclusion: 该体积项在目前可实现的实验中具有可探测的前景，其意义超越了模拟范式（analogue paradigm），特别是对黑洞热力学（black-hole thermodynamics）具有重要启示。

Abstract: The quantum information content of Hawking radiation holds the key to understanding black-hole evaporation and the fate of unitarity. Motivated by recent advances in cold-atom experiments, we develop a lattice-regularization approach aimed at simulating the coarse-grained entanglement scaling of a quantum field in a 1+1D analogue black-hole background. We provide the first concrete demonstration that logarithmic negativity -- an entanglement monotone that typically exhibits a UV-divergent log-scaling for the conformal vacuum -- acquires a UV-finite volume term from the nonlocal correlations seeded by Hawking radiation. We show that this volume term encodes both the number density and spatial distribution of entangled Hawking pairs along the black-hole interior and exterior. We highlight its prospective detection in currently realizable experiments as well as its implications beyond the analogue paradigm, in particular for black-hole thermodynamics.

</details>


### [33] [Boundedness and decay for the conformal wave equation in Schwarzschild-AdS under dissipative boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02084)
*Alex Tullini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了四维史瓦西-反德西特时空（Schwarzschild-Anti de Sitter spacetimes）中满足耗散边界条件（dissipative boundary conditions）的共形波动方程（conformal wave equation）的解的衰减特性，证明了非退化能量（non-degenerate energy）可以以任意多项式速率衰减，这与狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）下的对数衰减形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索史瓦西-反德西特时空中波动方程的能量衰减行为，特别关注耗散边界条件与狄利克雷边界条件在衰减速率上的差异。该研究旨在理解边界条件类型如何影响波动能量的长期演化。

Method: 研究方法基于对共形波动方程 $\square_g ψ+ \frac{2}{l^2} ψ= 0$ 在四维史瓦西-反德西特时空中的分析，采用耗散边界条件而非传统的狄利克雷边界条件。通过控制 $n$ 次 $T$-对易能量（$T$-commuted energy）来证明非退化能量的衰减。

Result: 主要结果表明，在耗散边界条件下，非退化能量可以以任意多项式速率 $(1+v)^{-n}$ 衰减，这与纯反德西特时空（pure Anti-de Sitter case）的结果一致。值得注意的是，光子球（photon sphere）处的额外俘获现象不影响衰减速率，这与狄利克雷边界条件下的逆对数衰减形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 结论指出耗散边界条件能够实现多项式衰减，而狄利克雷边界条件仅能获得对数衰减。这表明边界条件的选择对波动方程在史瓦西-反德西特时空中的长期行为具有决定性影响，且光子球处的俘获现象在耗散边界条件下不影响衰减特性。

Abstract: We study the conformal wave equation $\square_g ψ+ \frac{2}{l^2} ψ= 0$ on 4-dimensional Schwarzschild--Anti de Sitter spacetimes under dissipative boundary conditions. We prove boundedness and decay of the non-degenerate energy of $ψ$ at an arbitrary polynomial rate of $(1+v)^{-n}$ provided that we control the (up to) $n$-times $T$-commuted energy. This contrasts with the inverse logarithmic decay obtained under Dirichlet boundary conditions and is in line with the result obtained in the pure Anti-de Sitter case under dissipative boundary conditions. In particular, the decay is not affected by the additional trapping at the photon sphere.

</details>


### [34] [Localized formation of quiescent big bang singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02104)
*Andrés Franco-Grisales*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了无需接近背景解的局部大爆炸形成结果，通过引入满足特定二阶微分方程的时间函数构造类空超曲面叶状结构，实现了奇点的局部化与同步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大爆炸形成结果通常要求初始数据接近某个背景解，本文旨在消除这一限制，建立不依赖背景解接近性的局部大爆炸形成理论。

Method: 引入一种新的类空超曲面叶状结构（foliation），其由满足特定二阶微分方程的时间函数的水平集给出；该时间函数实现了奇点同步，同时导出了爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equations）的对称双曲形式（symmetric hyperbolic formulation）。

Result: 在初始数据满足特定条件的足够大邻域内，相应的最大整体双曲发展（maximal globally hyperbolic development）在x点过去方向具有局部静止大爆炸奇点（local quiescent big bang singularity）和曲率发散（curvature blow up）；新方法独立于物质模型，并能在奇点上诱导几何初始数据。

Conclusion: 新方法相比先前局部大爆炸稳定性结果具有两个关键优势：独立于物质模型，可能适用于标量场以外的物质模型；能够得出解在奇点上诱导几何初始数据的结论，从而完整描述了大爆炸的渐近行为。

Abstract: We prove a localized big bang formation result, which does not require proximity of the initial data to any background solution. Suppose that we are given initial data for the Einstein--nonlinear scalar field equations on an open set $U \subset \mathbb{R}^3$. We identify a general condition on the initial data such that if the condition is satisfied in a large enough neighborhood of $x \in U$, then the corresponding maximal globally hyperbolic development has a local quiescent big bang singularity with curvature blow up to the past of $x$. We achieve the localization by introducing a new kind of foliation by spacelike hypersurfaces, given by the level sets of a time function satisfying a certain second order differential equation. This time function allows us to synchronize the singularity while at the same time yielding a symmetric hyperbolic formulation of Einstein's equations. Our new formulation also has two key advantages over previous localized big bang stability results. First, it is independent of the matter model, so it is possible that it could be used to prove big bang formation with matter models different from a scalar field. And second, it allows us to conclude that our solutions induce geometric initial data on the singularity, thus giving a complete description of the asymptotics towards the big bang.

</details>


### [35] [Axial gravitational perturbations and echo-like signals of a hairy black hole from gravitational decoupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02164)
*Yi Yang,Ali Ovgun,Gaetano Lambiase,Dong Liu,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了引力解耦框架下构建的毛状黑洞（hairy black hole）的轴向引力扰动，揭示了该时空几何中回波样晚期信号的几何起源，为通过引力波衰荡探测黑洞毛发提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究引力解耦框架下构建的毛状黑洞的轴向引力扰动，旨在探索该时空中回波样晚期信号的几何起源，为通过引力波衰荡（gravitational-wave ringdown）探测黑洞毛发（black-hole hair）提供理论工具。

Method: 推导了奇宇称主方程（odd-parity master equation）及相应的有效势（effective potential），采用频域（frequency-domain）和时域（time-domain）方法计算准正规模（quasinormal-mode）谱，分析参数空间中有效势的双峰结构（double-peak structure）。

Result: 在合适的参数空间区域，轴向势能形成支持俘获腔（trapping cavity）的双峰结构，产生回波样晚期波形（echo-like late-time waveforms）；这些延迟脉冲源于有效势的几何结构而非人为设定的近地平反射率。回波区域与弱能量条件（weak energy condition）满足区域不一定重合。

Conclusion: 研究结果为通过引力波衰荡探测黑洞毛发提供了有用框架，有助于探索标准无毛定理（no-hair paradigm）的可能观测偏离；在解释解的物理状态时必须考虑回波区域与弱能量条件满足区域的区别。

Abstract: We study axial gravitational perturbations of a hairy black hole constructed in the framework of gravitational decoupling and investigate the geometric origin of echo-like late-time signals in this spacetime. We derive the odd-parity master equation and the corresponding effective potential, and we compute the quasinormal-mode spectrum by using frequency-domain and time-domain methods. We show that, in a suitable region of parameter space, the axial potential develops a double-peak structure that supports a trapping cavity and gives rise to echo-like late-time waveforms. Rather than imposing near-horizon reflectivity by hand, the delayed pulses therefore arise dynamically from the geometry of the effective potential. We also clarify that the parameter region exhibiting echoes need not coincide with the region in which the weak energy condition is satisfied everywhere outside the event horizon, and this distinction must be taken into account when interpreting the physical status of the solution. Our results provide a useful framework for probing black-hole hair through gravitational-wave ringdown and for exploring possible observational departures from the standard no-hair paradigm.

### [36] [Quadratic gravity corrections to scalar QNMs of rapidly rotating black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02214)
*Stef J. B. Husken,Tom van der Steen,Simon Maenaut,Kelvin Ka-Ho Lam,Maxim D. Jockwer,Adrian Ka-Wai Chung,Thomas Hertog,Tjonnie G. F. Li,Nicolás Yunes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前在有效场论框架下计算黑洞准正则模谱的修正仅限于中等自旋，因为相应的背景解依赖于自旋参数展开。需要利用适用于大自旋的数值黑洞解来扩展计算范围。

Method: 使用最近构建的适用于大自旋的数值黑洞解，计算标量高斯-邦尼和动力学陈-西蒙斯引力中旋转黑洞标量准正则模谱相对于广义相对论的领先阶偏差。采用伪谱配置方法（pseudo-spectral collocation methods）求解扰动方程。

Result: 计算了无量纲自旋高达a/M=0.99的准正则模修正，对于l=m=0模的精度优于~10^{-3}，对于更高多极矩的精度优于~10^{-6}。当自旋a/M>0.9时，某些模式的修正可增加数个数量级。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将准正则模修正计算扩展到高自旋区域，揭示了在极端自旋条件下修正显著增强的现象，为检验广义相对论修正理论提供了更全面的理论预测。

Abstract: In an effective-field-theory framework for gravity, black-hole quasinormal mode spectra acquire corrections in quadratic-curvature, scalar-tensor extensions of general relativity. Previous calculations of such corrections were limited to moderate spins, since the corresponding background solutions relied on expansions in the spin parameter. Using recently constructed numerical black-hole solutions valid for large spin, we compute the leading-order deviations from general relativity in the scalar quasinormal mode spectrum of rotating black holes in scalar Gauss-Bonnet and dynamical Chern-Simons gravity. We solve the resulting perturbation equations with pseudo-spectral collocation methods, allowing us to determine the quasinormal-mode corrections for dimensionless spins up to $a/M=0.99$, with accuracy better than $\lesssim 10^{-3}$ for the $l=m=0$ mode and $\lesssim 10^{-6}$ for higher multipoles. For spins $a/M>0.9$, the corrections to certain modes can increase by orders of magnitude.

### [37] [Fluid perturbations from expanding bubbles in first-order phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02240)
*Chiara Caprini,Antonino S. Midiri,Simona Procacci,Alberto Roper Pol*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究辐射主导时期一级相变（first-order phase transition）中速度场的功率谱（power spectrum），重点关注气泡膨胀阶段，并提出了声波相（sound-wave phase）开始时速度谱的精确模板，用于研究各向异性应力和引力波产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究辐射主导时期一级相变过程中速度场的功率谱，旨在为后续研究各向异性应力（anisotropic stresses）和引力波产生（gravitational wave production）提供更精确的理论基础。特别关注气泡膨胀阶段，假设该阶段以声波相的开始为结束。

Method: 通过分析气泡膨胀阶段的速度场，推导出声波相开始时速度功率谱的精确模板。研究重点包括速度谱中的断点（breaks）与气泡大小、声壳厚度（sound shell thickness）以及不连续性（discontinuities）位置的关系，并考察了超音速爆燃（supersonic deflagrations）的特殊情况。

Result: 研究发现速度谱中的断点并非如先前所认为的与气泡大小和声壳厚度相关，而是与不连续性的位置相关。对于超音速爆燃，当壁速度（wall velocity）趋近查普曼-儒盖速度（Chapman-Jouget speed）而非声速时，中间斜率（intermediate slope）更为显著且两个断点分离更明显。此外，速度功率谱的渐近分支由大尺度下单气泡轮廓的积分和小尺度下速度轮廓的不连续性决定。

Conclusion: 本文提供了辐射主导时期一级相变中速度场功率谱的精确模板，修正了先前关于断点来源的认识，并研究了气泡成核时间分布函数（exponential and simultaneous）对断点和中间斜率的影响。所有结果已整合到公开的Python软件包CosmoGW中。

Abstract: We study the power spectrum of the velocity field induced during a first-order phase transition occurring in the radiation-dominated era. We focus on the phase of bubble expansion, assuming that it ends with the onset of the sound-wave regime. The main result we present is a refined template for the velocity spectrum at the beginning of the sound-wave phase, which can be used for studying the resulting anisotropic stresses and gravitational wave production. In particular, we find that the breaks in the velocity spectrum are not associated to the bubble size and the sound shell thickness, as previously proposed, but to the position of the discontinuities. This distinction is particularly relevant for supersonic deflagrations, as it implies that the intermediate slope is more pronounced and the two breaks are more separated when the wall velocity approaches the Chapman-Jouget speed, instead of the sound speed. We also show that the asymptotic branches of the velocity power spectrum are determined by the integral over the single-bubble profiles at large scales, and by the discontinuities of the velocity profiles at small scales. Furthermore, we study the dependence of the two breaks and the intermediate slope on the distribution function of the times of bubble nucleation (exponential and simultaneous). All the results presented in this work have been included in the public Python package CosmoGW.

</details>

### [38] [Electronic-Structure Correlations Governing Superconductivity in Nb-Based High-Entropy Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01446)
*Md Sabbir Hossen Bijoy,Vladislav Korostelev,Deva Prasaad Neelakandan,Harshil Goyal,Steven E. Porterfield,Youming Xu,Shuchen Li,Xi Chen,Mark Adams,Barton C. Prorok,Konstantin Klyukin,Chanho Lee,Fariborz Kargar*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过系统实验和理论分析，揭示了铌基体心立方高熵合金中超导性能的非单调演化规律，发现铌d带相对于费米能级的位置是决定电子-声子耦合、临界温度和上临界场的主要因素，而晶格畸变作为次要调节因素通常削弱耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高熵合金（high-entropy alloys）作为探索高度无序金属系统中超导性的新平台，其超导机制特别是晶格畸变和复杂局部有序性的作用尚不明确。传统的价电子浓度规则无法可靠预测超导行为，因此需要建立性能与电子结构和晶格无序之间的关联分析。

Method: 研究设计了从二元到五元成分的铌基体心立方（body-centered-cubic）高熵合金系列，通过实验测量超导临界性质，并结合第一性原理计算和Eliashberg分析来探究电子和结构效应。

Result: 实验结果显示超导临界性质随合金复杂度呈非单调演化。有趣的是，具有更大晶格畸变的合金仍能实现更高的临界温度和上临界场。理论分析表明，铌d带相对于费米能级的位置是电子-声子耦合、临界温度和上临界场的主要驱动力，而晶格畸变作为次要调节因素通常削弱耦合。

Conclusion: 研究将这些发现整合为详细的关联图谱，将超导性质与电子结构指纹和振动特征联系起来，建立了基于机制的高熵合金设计策略，旨在增强临界温度和临界场。

Abstract: Superconducting high-entropy alloys have recently emerged as a new platform for exploring superconductivity in highly disordered metallic systems and may offer advantages for applications requiring mechanical robustness and tolerance to extreme environments. Yet the mechanisms that govern their superconductivity, particularly the roles of lattice distortion and complex local order, both inherent to high-entropy alloys, remain unclear. The conventional valence-electron-concentration rule fails to reliably predict superconducting behavior, motivating a correlation analysis that links performance to electronic structure and lattice disorder. Here, we study a systematic series of niobium-based body-centered-cubic high-entropy alloys, from binary to quinary compositions, designed to investigate the electronic and structural effects and identify the dominant factors controlling superconductivity. Our experimental results reveal that the superconducting critical properties evolve non-monotonically with alloy complexity. Interestingly, alloys with greater lattice distortion can still achieve higher critical temperature and upper critical field. These observations are corroborated by first-principles and Eliashberg analyses, which identify the position of the niobium d-band relative to the Fermi level as the primary driver of electron-phonon coupling, critical temperature, and upper critical field, with lattice distortion serving as a secondary modifier that generally weakens coupling. We consolidate these findings into a detailed correlation map linking superconducting properties to electronic-structure fingerprints and vibrational signatures, establishing a mechanism-informed design strategy for superconducting high-entropy alloys with enhanced critical temperature and field.

</details>


### [39] [Chiral Superconductivity in Periodically Driven Altermagnet/Superconductor Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01596)
*Xiaolin Wan,Zheng Qin,Fangyang Zhan,Junjie Zeng,Dong-Hui Xu,Rui Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁性与超导性的相互作用为工程化奇异拓扑相提供了丰富平台，而周期性驱动的动力学控制则为访问静态平衡下无法达到的量子态提供了独特途径。该研究旨在探索光驱动反铁磁异质结作为实现高陈数手性拓扑超导性的多功能平台。

Method: 提出在椭圆偏振光驱动的反铁磁-超导异质结中实现弗洛凯手性拓扑超导性的策略。研究分析了s波配对和混合s+d波配对两种情况下的系统行为。

Result: 对于s波配对，系统经历从平凡相到手性拓扑超导相的转变。引入混合s+d波配对后，系统可访问具有高度可调陈数（高达N=4）的弗洛凯手性拓扑超导相。这些奇异相源于反铁磁性、超导配对和周期性驱动场的交织作用。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了光驱动反铁磁异质结作为探索和操控高陈数手性拓扑超导性的多功能平台，为拓扑量子态的动态控制提供了新途径。

Abstract: The interplay between magnetism and superconductivity provides a fertile ground for engineering exotic topological phases, while dynamical control via periodic driving offers a unique avenue to access quantum states that are inaccessible in static equilibrium. Here, we propose a strategy to achieve the Floquet chiral topological superconductivity in an altermagnet-superconductor heterostructure driven by elliptically polarized light. We show that for $s$-wave pairing, the system undergoes a transition from a trivial to a chiral topological superconducting phase. More strikingly, with the introduction of mixed $s+d$-wave pairing, we find that the system can access Floquet chiral topological superconducting phases with highly tunable Chern numbers up to N=4. These exotic phases are attributed to the intertwining of altermagnetism, superconducting pairing, and the periodic driving field. Our work establishes the light-driven altermagnetic heterostructure as a versatile platform for exploring and manipulating high-Chern-number chiral topological superconductivity.
