### [40] [Dissecting superconductivity in the Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates: The role of electron correlation and interlayer magnetic exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01902)
*Xiaoyang Chen,Zezhong Li,Mei Xie,Deyuan Hu,Yiu-Fung Chiu,Stefano Agrestini,Wenliang Zhang,Yi Lu,Meng Wang,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Donglai Feng,Ke-Jin Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）对比分析三层和双层镍酸盐的超导特性差异，发现三层La₄Ni₃O₁₀具有更强的巡游性、更弱的电子关联和层间交换作用，这共同解释了其较低的超导转变温度（~30 K vs 80 K）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper（RP）镍酸盐家族中，尽管具有共同的NiO₂结构单元，但超导转变温度（T_c）存在显著差异（三层~30 K vs 双层80 K）。理解控制该家族T_c的关键因素至关重要。

Method: 采用共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic x-ray scattering, RIXS）技术，直接对比研究La₄Ni₃O₁₀（三层）与其双层对应物的电子和磁激发特性，并使用线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）提取层间超交换相互作用参数。

Result: La₄Ni₃O₁₀表现出更强的巡游特性，具有更宽的Ni dd轨道激发和强Ni 3d荧光连续谱，表明电子关联较弱。同时存在明确的集体自旋激发，包括色散的声学和光学磁振子支以及非公度自旋密度波。层间超交换相互作用（J_z）约为22 meV，远小于双层体系。

Conclusion: 较弱的电子关联和减小的层间交换相互作用共同解释了三层化合物显著较低的T_c。研究确立了层间磁耦合和电子关联作为控制层状镍酸盐超导性的关键参数，为理解该新兴家族中的配对机制提供了重要约束。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity in the Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelates has opened a new chapter in the search for high superconducting transition temperatures ($T_\mathrm{c}$) materials. A central and puzzling feature of this family is the wide variation in $T_\mathrm{c}$ despite their common NiO$_2$ building blocks, as highlighted by the recent observation of superconductivity at $\sim$ 30 K in trilayer $\mathrm{La_4Ni_3O_{10}}$, significantly lower than 80 K reported in bilayer $\mathrm{La_3Ni_2O_7}$. Understanding the factors that control $T_\mathrm{c}$ in this family is therefore of paramount importance. Here, we use resonant inelastic x-ray scattering (RIXS) to investigate the electronic and magnetic excitations of $\mathrm{La_4Ni_3O_{10}}$ in direct comparison with its bilayer counterpart. Our results reveal a markedly different landscape. $\mathrm{La_4Ni_3O_{10}}$ exhibits a more itinerant character, evidenced by broader Ni $dd$ orbital excitations and a strong Ni 3$d$ fluorescence continuum, suggesting weaker electronic correlations than in the bilayer. Despite this, well-defined collective spin excitations persist, including dispersive acoustic and optical magnon branches alongside an incommensurate spin density wave. Using linear spin wave theory, we extract the interlayer superexchange interaction ($J_z$) to be $\sim$ 22 meV, much smaller than that in $\mathrm{La_3Ni_2O_7}$. The weaker correlation and reduced interlayer exchange together provide a consistent explanation for the substantially lower $T_\mathrm{c}$ in the trilayer compound. Our findings establish interlayer magnetic coupling and electronic correlation as key parameters governing superconductivity in layered nickelates and offer critical constraints for understanding the pairing mechanism in this emerging family.

</details>


### [41] [Jahn-Teller distortion on strained La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02191)
*Yuxin Wang,Zhan Wang,Fu-Chun Zhang,Kun Jiang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了应变La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜的电子结构，发现双轴压缩应变主要通过增强Jahn-Teller畸变来调控超导性，而层间dz²轨道跳跃变化微弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在阐明应变对La₃Ni₂O₇薄膜电子结构的影响机制，特别是理解为何超导性仅在低于临界面内晶格常数时出现，从而识别关键的微观调控参数。

Method: 采用系统性的电子结构研究，分析双轴压缩应变对Ni-O键长的影响，计算Jahn-Teller分裂ΔJT和层间dz²轨道跳跃t⊥z的变化，并通过计算费米面和霍尔响应与实验测量对比验证。

Result: 双轴压缩应变主要拉长外层顶端Ni-O键而内层键长几乎不变，导致Jahn-Teller分裂显著增强而层间dz²轨道跳跃变化微弱。计算结果显示应变增强的ΔJT是调控超导性的关键微观参数。

Conclusion: Jahn-Teller畸变被确认为应变La₃Ni₂O₇中的关键调控参数，支持其在优化双层镍酸盐超导性中的核心作用，为理解应变调控超导机制提供了微观基础。

Abstract: We present a systematic study of the electronic structure of strained La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films. We show that biaxial compressive strain mainly elongates the outer apical Ni-O bond while leaving the inner apical Ni-O bond nearly unchanged. As a result, the Jahn-Teller splitting $Δ_{JT}$ is strongly enhanced, whereas the interlayer $d_{z^2}$ hopping $t_\perp^z$ changes only weakly. Since superconductivity is widely believed to emerge only below a critical in-plane lattice constant, our results identify the strain-enhanced $Δ_{JT}$ as the relevant microscopic tuning parameter. Consistently, the calculated Fermi surfaces and Hall response for LaAlO$_3$ and SrLaAlO$_4$ substrates agree with ARPES and Hall measurements. Our results identify Jahn-Teller distortion as a key tuning parameter in strained La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ and support its central role in optimizing superconductivity in bilayer nickelates.

### [42] [Chiral skyrmionic superconductivity from doping a Chern Ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02298)
*Miguel Gonçalves,Kun Yang,Shi-Zeng Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究展示通过空穴掺杂Chern铁磁体可实现手性超导性。在Kane-Mele-Hubbard模型中，强相互作用和足够大的Ising自旋轨道耦合下，磁子（自旋翻转激发）与两个空穴形成的库珀对表现出有限自旋手性和手性f波对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索手性超导性（chiral superconductivity）的新微观机制，特别是通过空穴掺杂Chern铁磁体（Chern ferromagnet）来实现。这一机制可能与MoTe₂莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中最近观测到的超导性相关。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix-renormalization-group）方法，研究相对于每晶胞填充ν=1电子的空穴掺杂下的排斥性Kane-Mele-Hubbard模型。

Result: 在足够强的相互作用和足够大的Ising自旋轨道耦合下，磁子（magnon）与两个空穴形成的库珀对（Cooper pair）被稳定化。该库珀对表现出有限自旋手性（spin chirality）——标志着非共面斯格明子自旋纹理（skyrmionic spin texture）——以及手性f波对称性（chiral f-wave symmetry）。配对和自旋手性由母体Chern铁磁体的陈数/极化决定。

Conclusion: 随着Ising自旋轨道耦合增加，斯格明子库珀对之间的相互作用从排斥转变为吸引，揭示了中间自旋轨道耦合区域中手性超导性可从空穴-斯格明子库珀对的凝聚中涌现。这一发现为手性超导性提供了新的微观机制。

Abstract: We show that chiral superconductivity can be stabilized by hole doping a Chern ferromagnet. Performing exact diagonalization and density-matrix-renormalization-group calculations on the repulsive Kane-Mele-Hubbard model at hole doping relative to filling $ν=1$ electron per unit cell, we find that a Cooper pair formed by a magnon (spin-flip excitation) bound to two holes is stabilized at sufficiently strong interactions and sufficiently large Ising spin-orbit coupling (SOC). This Cooper pair exhibits both finite spin chirality -- signaling a noncoplanar skyrmionic spin texture -- and chiral $f$-wave symmetry. The pairing and spin chirality are set by the Chern number/polarization of the parent Chern ferromagnet. We further find that interactions between skyrmion Cooper pairs evolve from repulsive to attractive as the Ising SOC increases, revealing an intermediate-SOC region where chiral superconductivity can emerge from the condensation of hole-skyrmion Cooper pairs. Our findings provide a novel microscopic mechanism for chiral superconductivity and may be relevant for the recent observation of superconductivity in the MoTe$_2$ moiré superlattice.

</details>

### [43] [Three-form lifting of dilaton flat direction without and with gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01272)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将标度子（dilaton）与三形式场（three-form field）以兼容规范不变性（gauge invariance）和标度变换（dilatations）的方式耦合，构建有效动力学（effective dynamics）。该方法在不引入显式标度破坏算符（explicit scale-violating operators）的前提下提升平坦方向。

Result: 该耦合机制有效提升了平坦方向（lifts the flat direction）。当包含引力时，相应的势能（potential）呈现指数平台形式（exponential plateau）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，自发标度对称性破缺不一定需要平坦方向；通过三形式场与标度子的适当耦合，可以在保持规范不变性和标度变换的前提下实现平坦方向的提升，并在引力背景下产生指数平台势。

Abstract: Spontaneous scale symmetry breaking is commonly associated with a flat direction in the action. We show that this need not be so if the dilaton is coupled to a three-form field in a manner compatible with gauge invariance and dilatations. The resulting effective dynamics lifts the flat direction without introducing explicit scale-violating operators. When gravity is included, the corresponding potential takes the form of an exponential plateau.

### [45] [Descending into the Modular Bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01275)
*Nathan Benjamin,A. Liam Fitzpatrick,Wei Li,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文采用机器学习优化方法高效搜索二维共形场论（2d CFTs）的模自举方程数值解，探索中心荷在1到8/7范围内的理论景观，提出了新的谱截断不确定性估计方法和优化算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索二维共形场论（2d CFTs）的理论景观，特别是在中心荷c>1且缺乏已知例子的1到8/7范围内，通过数值方法寻找可能的共形场论。

Method: 方法包括：1）将环面配分函数的模不变性要求转化为损失函数；2）提出谱截断不确定性估计策略；3）使用基于奇异值的新优化器（Sven）替代梯度下降，以更好地处理损失函数景观的层次结构。

Result: 数值构造了中心荷在1到8/7范围内的候选截断CFT配分函数，并论证这些候选解可能来自模自举解的连续空间；同时提供了证据表明在c≈1附近存在比现有界限Δ_gap ≤ c/6 + 1/3更严格的谱隙约束。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了机器学习风格优化在探索二维共形场论景观中的有效性，特别是在缺乏已知理论的参数区域，为理解模自举方程的解空间结构提供了新见解。

Abstract: In this paper, we attempt to explore the landscape of two-dimensional conformal field theories (2d CFTs) by efficiently searching for numerical solutions to the modular bootstrap equation using machine-learning-style optimization. The torus partition function of a 2d CFT is fixed by the spectrum of its primary operators and its chiral algebra, which we take to be the Virasoro algebra with $c>1$. We translate the requirement that this partition function is modular invariant into a loss function, which we then minimize to identify possible primary spectra. Our approach involves two technical innovations that facilitate finding reliable candidate CFTs. The first is a strategy to estimate the uncertainty associated with truncating the spectrum to the lowest dimension operators. The second is the use of a new singular-value-based optimizer (Sven) that is more effective than gradient descent at navigating the hierarchical structure of the loss landscape. We numerically construct candidate truncated CFT partition functions with central charges between 1 and $\frac{8}{7}$, a range devoid of known examples, and argue that these candidates likely come from a continuous space of modular bootstrap solutions. We also provide evidence for a more stringent constraint on the spectral gap near $c = 1$ than the existing bound of $Δ_{\rm gap} \le \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3}$.

### [46] [Solving Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01320)
*Budhaditya Bhattacharjee,William. E. Salazar,Alexei Andreanov,Dario Rosa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在large-$N$极限下精确求解了Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (LSYK)模型，其中耦合参数服从Lévy稳定分布（tail exponent $μ∈[0,2]$）。该模型在$μ=0$时为自由理论，在$μ=2$时恢复为标准高斯SYK模型，中间区域表现出非最大混沌行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Lévy稳定分布耦合的SYK模型，旨在探索非高斯分布对量子混沌和热力学性质的影响。通过参数$μ$在自由理论和最大混沌高斯SYK模型之间的连续插值，可以系统研究混沌行为的演化。

Method: 从哈密顿量及其配分函数出发，采用玻色子振子表示作用量，推导large-$N$ Schwinger-Dyson方程。在large-$q$和红外极限下进行数值和解析求解，并通过大$q$格林函数计算Krylov指数，从四点函数提取Lyapunov指数来分析混沌特性。

Result: 参数$μ$在$0<μ<2$区间内产生非最大混沌行为，混沌程度随$μ$变化连续变化。计算了熵、自由能、平均能量和比热容等热力学量，并与高斯SYK模型进行比较。通过Lévy稳定分布的不同分解建立了与高斯SYK模型的非平凡联系。

Conclusion: LSYK模型提供了从自由理论到最大混沌SYK模型的连续插值框架，揭示了非高斯耦合分布对量子混沌和热力学性质的系统性影响。该模型为全息对偶和非费米液体理论提供了新的研究视角。

Abstract: We present an exact solution in the large-$N$ limit of the Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (LSYK) model introduced in Ref. [1], wherein the couplings are drawn from a Lévy Stable distribution parameterized by a tail exponent $μ\in [0, 2]$. Starting from the Hamiltonian and its associated partition function, we highlight the key differences from the standard Gaussian SYK model and derive the large-$N$ Schwinger-Dyson equations via a bosonic oscillator representation of the action. These equations are solved both numerically and analytically in the large-$q$ and infrared limits. We subsequently analyze the chaotic properties of the model by computing the Krylov exponent from the large-$q$ Green's function and extracting the Lyapunov exponent from the $4$-point function. The parameter $μ$ continuously interpolates between a free theory at $μ= 0$ and the conventional, maximally chaotic Gaussian SYK model at $μ= 2$, with non-maximal chaos persisting throughout the intermediate regime $0 < μ< 2$. Thermodynamic quantities, including the entropy, free energy, average energy, and specific heat capacity, are computed and compared with their Gaussian SYK counterparts. The interpretations of the thermodynamics are discussed with respect to the holographic dual and non-Fermi liquid theory. Finally, we discuss an alternative representation of the LSYK model based on a distinct decomposition of the Lévy Stable distribution, which establishes a non-trivial connection to Gaussian SYK, and provide supporting analytical and numerical results in the appendices.

</details>

Abstract: These proceedings start with a discussion of my recent experiences with large language models and potential implications for their usage in our field. The focus is on four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ Minkowski vacua in type IIB compactifications that live deep in the interior of moduli space and admit an exact worldsheet description in terms of Landau--Ginzburg models. The main examples are the $1^9$ and $2^6$ models, mirror to rigid Calabi--Yau threefolds and therefore free of Kähler moduli. This makes them ideal laboratories for testing whether fluxes can stabilize all fields and for probing conjectures about the string landscape and the swampland. Based mostly on arXiv:2406.03435, arXiv:2407.16756, we review how higher-order terms in the flux superpotential can stabilize fields that remain massless at quadratic order, how isolated Minkowski vacua arise in the $2^6$ model, and why these constructions provide sharp data for the tadpole and massless Minkowski conjectures. ### [48] [Entanglement entropy and conformal bounds for $d=5$ CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01436)
*Pablo Bueno,Adam Fernández García,Francesco Gentile,Oscar Lasso Andino,Javier Moreno*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了五维共形场论（CFT₅）中时空区域纠缠熵的普适常数项F(A)的性质，发现其在三维CFT中的有界性在五维中失效，但针对球形纠缠面的小形变提出了一个可能的弱约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在奇维共形场论（CFTs）中，时空区域A的纠缠熵包含一个普适常数项F(A)。先前研究表明，在三维CFT中F(A)具有正定性和下界性质，且自由标量场理论可能最大化F(A)/F₀比值。本文旨在探究这些性质在五维CFT中的适用性。

Method: 通过分析球形纠缠面（∂A=𝕊³）的小形变，研究F(A)在五维CFT中的行为。使用互信息（mutual information）方法稳健定义F(A)，并考察应力张量两点函数C_T与球面欧几里得分区函数之间的关系。

Result: 研究发现，在五维CFT中，F(A)对于球形纠缠面的小形变保持局部最小值，但对于更一般的区域可以取任意大的正值或负值，因此既无上界也无下界。三维CFT中关于F(A)/F₀极值化的猜想在五维中失效，但提出了一个涉及C_T/F₀比值的弱约束。

Conclusion: 五维CFT中F(A)的有界性性质与三维情况显著不同，但针对球形纠缠面小形变，所有已知CFT₅都满足C_T/F₀ ≤ [C_T/F₀]_{自由标量场} ≈ 0.314的约束。这一结果可能推广到更高维度。

Abstract: The entanglement entropy of spacetime regions $A$ in odd-dimensional conformal field theories (CFTs) contains a universal constant term, $(-1)^{\frac{d-1}{2}}F(A)$. This quantity can be robustly defined by considering the mutual information of pairs of slightly deformed versions of $A$. In the case of general three-dimensional CFTs, $F(A)$ is positive definite and bounded below by the round disk result, $F(A)\geq F_0\equiv F(\partial A=\mathbb{S}^1)$. Additionally, strong evidence has been provided that for every region $A$, $F(A)/F_0$ is maximized, within the space of CFT$_3$'s, by the free scalar field result. In this paper we show that while $F(A)$ remains a local minimum around $F_0\equiv F(\partial A=\mathbb{S}^3)$ for small deformations of the spherical entangling surface, it can take values of arbitrarily large magnitude with either sign for more general regions, and hence it is neither upper- nor lower-bounded in general CFT$_5$'s. We argue that an analogous conjecture regarding the extremization of $F(A)/F_0$ for general regions within the space of theories fails in $d=5$. We instead analyze the viability of the weaker bound, $F_ε/F_0\leq \left[F_ε/F_0\right]_{\text{free scalar}}$, $\forall$CFT$_5$ for general small geometric deformations of the spherical entangling surface. This is equivalent to a general constraint involving the stress-tensor two-point function $C_T$ and the Euclidean partition function on the sphere, namely, $C_T/F_0\leq \left[C_T/F_0\right]_{\text{ free scalar}}\approx 0.314$, which we show to hold for all known CFT$_5$'s. We also comment on possible extensions of this result to higher dimensions.

</details>


### [49] [The $W_n$ Light One-Point Torus Conformal Block](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01804)
*Armen Poghosyan,Hasmik Poghosyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了$A_{n-1}$ Toda场论中单点环面（torus）共形块（conformal block）的光渐近极限（light asymptotic limit），通过AGT对应（AGT correspondence）将其转化为四维${\cal N}=2^{\ast}$ $U(n)$超对称杨-米尔斯理论（supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory）的瞬子配分函数（instanton partition function）计算，并在$b\to 0$极限下推导出适用于任意$n\ge 2$的显式表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究$A_{n-1}$ Toda场论中单点环面共形块的光渐近极限，这一极限通过AGT对应与四维${\cal N}=2^{\ast}$ $U(n)$超对称杨-米尔斯理论的瞬子配分函数计算相关联，旨在理解该极限下共形块的简化结构。

Method: 利用AGT对应将Toda场论的共形块问题转化为四维超对称杨-米尔斯理论的瞬子配分函数计算；在$b\to 0$极限下分析瞬子求和（instanton sum）的简化特性，发现只有特定臂长（arm lengths）的杨图（Young diagram）盒子对双基本因子（bifundamental factors）有贡献。

Result: 推导出适用于任意$n\ge 2$的光单点环面$W_n$共形块的显式表示；在$n=2$的Liouville情况下与已知的超几何表示（hypergeometric representation）一致；讨论了$W_3$情况及其与通过影子形式（shadow formalism）获得的替代表示的关系。

Conclusion: 成功获得了$A_{n-1}$ Toda场论中光渐近极限下单点环面共形块的显式表示，验证了其在Liouville情况下的自洽性，并建立了与影子形式表示的联系，为相关理论研究提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: We study the light asymptotic limit of the one-point torus conformal block in $A_{n-1}$ Toda field theory. Through the AGT correspondence, this problem can be translated into the computation of the instanton partition function of four-dimensional ${\cal N}=2^{\ast}$ $U(n)$ supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory, which we then examine in the limit $b\to 0$ at fixed conformal dimensions. We show that, in this regime, the instanton sum simplifies drastically: for each Young diagram, only boxes with specific arm lengths contribute to the bifundamental factors. Exploiting this property, we derive an explicit representation for the light one-point torus $W_n$ conformal block valid for arbitrary $n\ge 2$.
  As a consistency check, we specialize our construction to the Liouville case $n=2$ and compare it with the previously known hypergeometric representation of the torus block in the light limit. We also discuss the $W_3$ case and its relation to a known alternative representation obtained by the shadow formalism.

</details>


### [50] [Symmetries and Critical Dimensions of Tensionless Branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01883)
*Bin Chen,Zezhou Hu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了玻色膜理论（bosonic brane theories）在无张力极限（tensionless limit）下的世界面对称性（worldsheet symmetry）及其量子一致性。通过引入bc鬼系统（bc ghost system）和BRST电荷（BRST charge），计算了$g^{(p)}_λ$代数的量子反常（quantum anomaly），并推导出玻色膜理论的临界维度（critical dimensions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究玻色膜理论在无张力极限下的世界面对称性及其量子一致性。研究关注特定规范固定（gauge fixing）后的剩余对称性，并分析其量子反常的消除条件。

Method: 研究方法包括：引入bc鬼系统以完全量子化无张力膜，推导整体BRST电荷；在正则量子化（canonical quantization）框架下，计算$g^{(p)}_λ$代数对一般参数$p$和$λ$的量子反常。

Result: 研究发现剩余世界面对称性由新型代数$g^{(p)}_λ$生成。通过要求量子反常消失，成功推导出玻色膜理论的临界维度，特别是获得了非平凡解：当$λ=-3$时，$p=3$对应$D=4$时空维度；当$λ=3$时，$p=6$对应$D=7$时空维度。

Conclusion: 本文系统研究了无张力玻色膜的世界面对称性，通过量子反常消除条件确定了理论的临界维度。所得结果揭示了特定参数组合下玻色膜理论的一致性条件，为相关研究提供了重要理论依据。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the worldsheet symmetry of bosonic brane theories and its quantum consistency in the tensionless limit. We find that the residual worldsheet symmetry after specific gauge fixing is generated by a novel algebra, denoted as $g^{(p)}_λ$. To achieve full quantization of the tensionless brane, we introduce a $bc$ ghost system and derive the overall BRST charge. Moreover, we calculate the quantum anomaly of the $g^{(p)}_λ$ algebra for general parameters $p$ and $λ$ in the framework of canonical quantization. After demanding that this quantum anomaly vanishes, we successfully derive the critical dimensions of the bosonic brane theories. Especially, we obtain nontrivial solutions: $p=3$ in $D=4$ spacetime dimensions when $λ=-3$ and $p=6$ in $D=7$ spacetime dimensions when $λ=3$.

</details>


### [51] [Effective Field Theory for Superconducting Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02133)
*Yanyan Bu,Zexin Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 基于Schwinger-Keldysh形式体系，构建了s波超导相变的有效场论，包含电磁规范场和复标量序参量。该理论系统处理耗散和涨落，重现Ginzburg-Landau方程，并通过全息超导体验证了有效作用量结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为s波超导相变构建一个包含耗散和涨落的实时动力学有效场论框架。通过Schwinger-Keldysh形式体系，系统处理临界点附近的物理过程，特别是高阶项对动力学的影响。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh形式体系，构建以电磁规范场（electromagnetic gauge field）和复标量序参量（complex scalar order parameter）为动力学变量的有效场论。通过对称性约束的有效作用量系统处理耗散和涨落，并利用全息Schwinger-Keldysh技术在全息超导体中进行严格验证。

Result: 有效场论在适当截断下重现了唯象的Ginzburg-Landau方程。低于临界温度时，序参量凝聚导致电磁规范对称性自发破缺。集体激发分析显示，Higgs模在临界点附近表现为过阻尼扩散模，而相位涨落通过Higgs机制被规范场吸收。全息验证确认了有效作用量结构并量化了Wilson系数，揭示了表征强耦合系统的振荡动力学特征。

Conclusion: 成功构建了s波超导相变的实时动力学有效场论框架，系统处理了耗散和涨落效应。该理论不仅重现了经典Ginzburg-Landau方程，还通过全息超导体验证了其有效性，揭示了强耦合系统中的复杂弛豫行为。

Abstract: Employing the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, we formulate an effective field theory for s-wave superconducting phase transition, where the dynamical variables consist of electromagnetic gauge field and a complex scalar order parameter. Symmetry-constrained effective action allows systematic handling of dissipations and fluctuations. In particular, we explore the physical implications of higher-order terms, including those involving additional dynamical fields as well as higher time derivatives, for the real-time dynamics near the superconducting critical point. When appropriately truncated, the effective field theory reproduces the phenomenological Ginzburg-Landau equations. Upon crossing the critical temperature into the low-temperature phase, the electromagnetic gauge symmetry undergoes spontaneous breaking induced by the condensate of the order parameter. Collective excitation analysis reveals that the Higgs mode behaves as an overdamped diffusive mode near the critical point, while the phase fluctuation is absorbed into the gauge field via the Higgs mechanism. Via the holographic Schwinger-Keldysh technique, rigorous validation in a holographic superconductor confirms the structure of the effective action and quantifies the Wilsonian coefficients. The holographic results uncover a complex relaxation parameter that is indicative of oscillatory dynamics, a hallmark of strongly coupled systems.

### [52] [Gravitational null rays: Covariant Quantization and the Dressing Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02228)
*Laurent Freidel,Josh Kirklin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过将着装时间（dressing time）作为量子参考系（QRF），以完全规范不变的方式量化了引力零射线段上的自由度。该方法超越了先前模型，通过引入协变正规序（covariant normal ordering）这一关键工具，在量子层面恢复了微分同胚协变性，并构建了携带Virasoro交叉积（Virasoro crossed product）结构的规范不变可观测量代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是超越先前模型，采用引力场本身构建量子参考系（QRF），并处理沿零射线段的完整微分同胚群（diffeomorphisms group），而不仅仅是局部紧致子群。这旨在实现完全规范不变的量子化，消除量子层面的虚假自由度。

Method: 核心方法是引入协变正规序（covariant normal ordering），这是一种依赖于量子参考系但独立于背景的重整化方案。该方法恢复了量子层面的微分同胚协变性，从而定义了量子着装映射（quantum dressing map），其像构成了规范不变可观测量代数。

Result: 研究发现该代数携带Virasoro交叉积（Virasoro crossed product）结构，且着装映射在规范固定算符上诱导了一个变形积，可理解为狄拉克括号（Dirac bracket）的量子化。通过经典层面的变形消除了物理希尔伯特空间表示中的反常（anomalies），着装时间作为非理想量子参考系，其不同相干态具有由Teo-Takhtajan能量（即Virasoro余伴随轨道的凯勒势）支配的非零重叠。

Conclusion: 该研究实现了引力零射线段自由度的完全规范不变量子化，通过引力场自身构建的量子参考系和协变正规序方案，在量子层面恢复了微分同胚协变性。所得物理希尔伯特空间允许通过Page-Wootters约化映射到着装时间视角，为量子引力中的规范不变性提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We quantize the degrees of freedom on a gravitational null ray segment in a fully gauge-invariant manner by using the dressing time as a quantum reference frame (QRF). Our work goes beyond previous models in that the QRF we employ is made out of the gravitational field itself, and accounts for the full group of diffeomorphisms along the ray, not just a locally compact subgroup. The key tool we introduce is covariant normal ordering, a QRF-dependent but background-independent renormalization prescription that restores diffeomorphism covariance at the quantum level. This enables the definition of a quantum dressing map whose image is the algebra of gauge-invariant observables. We find that this algebra carries the structure of a Virasoro crossed product, and that the dressing map induces a deformed product on gauge-fixed operators which can be understood as a quantization of the Dirac bracket, with consequences for the fluctuations of observables. We explain how to cancel anomalies in the physical Hilbert space representation of the gauge-invariant algebra by including a deformation at the classical level, thereby eliminating all spurious degrees of freedom at the quantum level. The physical Hilbert space admits a Page-Wootters reduction map to the perspective of the dressing time, and we show that the dressing time is non-ideal in the sense that its distinct coherent states have non-vanishing overlaps governed by the Teo-Takhtajan energy, i.e. the Kähler potential for Virasoro coadjoint orbits.

</details>

Result: 微分同胚不变性的主要结果是建立了一组递推关系，这些关系连接了有效拉格朗日量场展开中的相邻阶次，为理解扰动理论的结构提供了系统框架。

We recover the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transition, including the spin-wave critical line and the proliferation of vortices at high temperatures. We also verify the T-duality of the bosonic string, showing invariance under the exchange of momentum and winding on $S^1$, the transformation of the sigma model couplings according to the Buscher rules on constant toroidal backgrounds, the enhancement of the current algebra at self-dual radius, and non-geometric T-fold transition functions.

### [55] [Equivalence of toral Chern-Simons and Reshetikhin-Turaev theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01982)
*Daniel Galviz*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We prove a natural isomorphism between toral Chern-Simons theory with gauge group $\mathbb T=\mathcal t/Λ\cong U(1)^n$ and the Reshetikhin-Turaev theory associated with the finite quadratic module determined by an even, integral, nondegenerate symmetric bilinear form $K:Λ\timesΛ\to\mathbb Z.$ More precisely, let $G_K=Λ^*/KΛ$ be the discriminant group of $K$, equipped with its induced quadratic form $q_K$, and let $C(G_K,q_K)$ be the corresponding pointed modular category. Using the geometric quantization formulation of toral Chern-Simons theory, we show that the resulting toral TQFT is naturally isomorphic to the Reshetikhin-Turaev TQFT determined by $C(G_K,q_K)$. The comparison is established both for closed $3$-manifold invariants and for bordisms with boundary, yielding an isomorphism of extended $(2+1)$-dimensional TQFTs.

### [56] [Hyperscaling of spatial fluctuations constrains the development of urban populations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01969)
*Wout Merbis,Fernando A. N. Santos,Jay Armas,Frank Pijpers,Mike Lees*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析全球477个城市区域的人口网格数据，揭示了城市人口分布的分形（fractal）特征与均值-方差标度关系。研究发现城市人口分布的均值标度指数β与方差标度指数γ之间存在稳健的超标度（hyperscaling）关系，且该关系随时间演变趋向γ≈2+β的极限形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管城市人口展现出分形组织和系统性标度规律，但不同城市报告的标度指数存在显著差异，这对现有理论构成了挑战。研究旨在通过分析城市人口分布的均值与方差标度关系，揭示城市形态与波动之间的内在联系。

Method: 研究使用100米网格化人口地图，分析了荷兰（2000-2023年）和世界主要城市（1975-2020年）共477个城市区域。通过递归粗粒化（coarse-grain）每个城市，量化了边长为ℓ的方形网格单元中居民数量的均值⟨N_ℓ⟩和方差Var(N_ℓ)随ℓ的标度行为，分别得到标度指数β和γ。

Result: 研究发现城市间的γ与β存在线性依赖关系，即超标度关系。基于50年间超过10,000个指数估计的汇编显示，该关系稳健但非普适：其斜率和截距随大陆和时间变化，并随时间演变趋向γ≈2+β的极限形式。平均场（independent-cell）理论无法重现观测到的β-γ依赖关系，表明存在强空间相关性。

Conclusion: 研究推导了考虑相关性的方差分解，其中γ由相关维度D_c控制。在相关性主导的区域，γ=2+D_c。如果大型成熟城市演化为有效的单分形（monofractal）城市（D_c≈β），则渐近预测变为γ≈2+β，与观测到的时间漂移一致。这种相互依赖性连接了城市形态与波动，约束了机制性增长模型，并为基于局部均值和方差的空间指标提供了标度预测。

Abstract: Urban populations exhibit fractal organization and systematic scaling regularities, yet the scaling exponents reported across cities vary substantially, challenging existing theory. Using 100~m gridded population maps for 477 urban areas spanning the Netherlands (2000--2023) and major world cities (1975--2020), we recursively coarse-grain each city and quantify how the mean and variance of inhabitants in square grid cells of side length $\ell$ scale with $\ell$. This yields two exponents, $β$ from $\langle N_\ell\rangle\sim \ell^β$ and $γ$ from $\mathrm{Var}(N_\ell)\sim \ell^γ$, where in the small-$\ell$ limit $β$ equals the planar fractal dimension of populated space. Across cities within a given year, $γ$ depends linearly on $β$. Compiling $>$10,000 exponent estimates over five decades shows that this hyperscaling relation is robust yet non-universal: its slope and intercept vary across continents and drift systematically in time, trending toward the limiting form $γ\simeq 2+β$. A mean-field (independent-cell) argument predicts a quadratic mean--variance mapping and cannot reproduce the observed $β$--$γ$ dependence, implying strong spatial correlations. We derive a correlation-aware variance decomposition in which $γ$ is controlled by a correlation dimension $D_c$; in the correlation-dominated regime $γ=2+D_c$. If large maturing cities, as are the ones selected in our dataset, evolve to effective monofractal ($D_c\simeq β$) cities, the asymptotic prediction becomes $γ\simeq 2+β$, consistent with the observed temporal drift. This interdependence links urban form and fluctuations, constrains mechanistic growth models, and implies scaling predictions for spatial indicators built from local means and variances.

</details>


### [57] [Collective attention under digital exposure: A dynamical systems approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02059)
*Nuno Crokidakis*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个最小动力学框架，描述数字设备持续暴露下群体注意力的集体演化，将数字环境视为外部控制参数，分析其对持续注意力水平的单调递减影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字设备的广泛使用引发了对其在群体水平上影响持续注意力（sustained attention）的日益关注，需要理论框架来理解数字刺激环境下的注意力集体演化。

Method: 引入代表平均持续注意力水平的宏观变量，建模其动力学为内在认知恢复与数字刺激诱导退化之间的竞争机制；首先分析线性公式，然后扩展模型加入非线性退化项以捕捉高强度刺激下的放大效应。

Result: 推导出稳态的显式表达式，显示平衡注意力水平随暴露增加而单调递减；引入有效势能公式，揭示数字过度刺激逐渐改变动力学景观，将稳定状态移向注意力降低的机制。

Conclusion: 数字技术对注意力的影响可理解为持续外部刺激产生的渐进宏观效应，而非竞争行为状态间的转变；该模型不依赖社会传染或交互驱动的双稳态，而是描述环境压力下集体认知机制的连续位移。

Abstract: The widespread use of digital devices has raised growing concerns about its impact on sustained attention at the population level. In this work, we propose a minimal dynamical framework to describe the collective evolution of attention under continuous exposure to screen-mediated environments. We introduce a macroscopic variable representing the average level of sustained attention and model its dynamics as the result of competing mechanisms: intrinsic cognitive recovery and degradation induced by digital stimulation. The digital environment is treated as an external control parameter that continuously perturbs the system, leading to a relaxational dynamics. The proposed mechanisms are consistent with empirical findings on attentional dynamics under digital exposure. We first analyze a linear formulation, which provides an analytically tractable baseline, and then extend the model by incorporating a nonlinear degradation term that captures amplification effects under high-intensity stimulation. We derive an explicit expression for the stationary state and show that the equilibrium attention level decreases monotonically with increasing exposure. An effective potential formulation is introduced, revealing that digital overstimulation progressively deforms the dynamical landscape, shifting the stable state toward regimes of reduced attention without generating multiple equilibria. Importantly, the model does not rely on social contagion or interaction-driven bistability, but instead describes a continuous displacement of the collective cognitive regime under environmental pressure. Our results suggest that the impact of digital technologies on attention may be understood as a gradual macroscopic effect emerging from persistent external stimulation, rather than as a transition between competing behavioral states.

</details>

### [58] [Reconciling hadronic and partonic analyticity in $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01284)
*Martin Hoferichter,Bastian Kubis,Simon Mutke*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了B介子稀有衰变中涉及粲夸克圈（charm loops）的非局域矩阵元，证明了在微扰描述适用的参数空间区域中，部分子计算能够正确处理反常阈（anomalous thresholds）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B介子稀有衰变中的$b\to s\ell\ell$跃迁是探测标准模型之外新物理的灵敏探针。由于存在偏离标准模型预测的迹象，需要严格控制涉及粲夸克圈的非局域矩阵元，以确立超出合理怀疑的差异。

Method: 研究采用大空间类虚度下的算符乘积展开（operator product expansion），其系数已知至双圈阶。通过分析简单三角形拓扑结构，理解部分子计算的分析结构，并明确展示色散关系（dispersion relations）即使在反常阈情况下如何得到满足。

Result: 研究发现反常贡献与考虑强子自由度时的预期相匹配，证明部分子计算不会遗漏反常效应。这为在微扰描述适用的参数空间区域中使用该计算提供了理论依据。

Conclusion: 该分析证实了部分子计算在处理粲夸克圈非局域矩阵元时的可靠性，特别是在反常阈存在的情况下，为B介子稀有衰变中新物理搜索提供了更坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: Rare $B$-meson decays mediated by $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions constitute sensitive probes of physics beyond the Standard Model, and have triggered considerable interest due to hints for deviations from the Standard-Model prediction. To establish a discrepancy beyond a reasonable doubt, control over the nonlocal matrix elements involving charm loops is essential, which, for large spacelike virtualities, can be constrained by an operator product expansion with coefficients known at two-loop order. We observe that the analytic structure of this partonic calculation, whose understanding is important to put forward rigorous parameterizations, follows from simple triangle topologies and demonstrate explicitly how dispersion relations are fulfilled even in the case of anomalous thresholds. Crucially, these anomalous contributions match onto the ones expected when considering hadronic degrees of freedom, proving that the partonic calculation does not miss anomalous effects and justifying its use in regions of parameter space in which a perturbative description applies.

### [59] [New physics in multi-lepton tau decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01465)
*Yohei Ema,Patrick J. Fox,Matheus Hostert,Tony Menzo,Maxim Pospelov,Anupam Ray,Jure Zupan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了具有轻子味破坏（lepton-flavor-violating）耦合的暗粒子如何引发罕见的多体τ衰变，包括五体或七体衰变通道，这些通道包含多个可重建共振态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索暗粒子（dark particles）通过轻子味破坏耦合到τ轻子时，如何引发罕见的中微子缺失τ衰变（neutrinoless τ decays）。这些过程可能产生具有大终态多重性的衰变链，为寻找新物理（new physics）提供新途径。

Method: 研究方法包括分析几种代表性模型：动力学混合暗光子（kinetically mixed dark photon）、规范化的$L_i-L_j$模型（gauged $L_i-L_j$ models），以及更奇异的电荷分配如手征$U(1)'$标准模型扩展（chiral $U(1)'$ extensions of the Standard Model）。核心新要素是考虑极高能标下的味破坏可能性。

Result: 研究结果显示，在暗区（dark sector）衰变链中，多个实验上尚未搜索的通道通常主导先前考虑的衰变模式。这些主导通道包括$τ\to 5μ$、$τ\to 3μ\,2e$、$τ\to μ\,4e$等轻子通道，以及$τ\to μ\,4π$等强子通道，它们通常超越$τ\to 3μ$等先前考虑的衰变信号。

Conclusion: 结论指出，虽然某些模型（如规范化的$L_i-L_j$模型）包含因衰变到中微子而产生的更挑战性的丢失能量通道，但仍可通过完全可见通道进行搜索。这些多体τ衰变为探测暗区物理提供了新的实验搜索方向。

Abstract: Dark particles with lepton-flavor-violating couplings to the tau lepton can induce rare neutrinoless $τ$ decays with large final state multiplicities. We study models where transitions of the type $τ^\pm\to \ell^\pm\,φ$, with $φ$ a light new particle, initiate a chain of decays in the dark sector that terminate with decays into electrons, muons, or pions. These decay cascades appear as rare five or even seven-body $τ$ decays with multiple reconstructable resonances. We survey several representative models: kinetically mixed dark photon, gauged $L_i-L_j$ models, and other more exotic charge assignments such as chiral $U(1)'$ extensions of the Standard Model. The main new ingredient is the possibility of flavor violation at very high scales. In these models, a number of channels that have not yet been searched for experimentally, such as $τ\to 5μ$, $τ\to 3μ\,2e$, $τ\to μ\,4e$, and hadronic channels like $τ\to μ\,4π$, typically dominate over the previously-considered signatures such as $τ\to 3μ$. While some of the models, such as the gauged $L_i-L_j$ ones, also contain more challenging channels with missing energy due to decays to neutrinos, they can still be searched for via fully visible channels.

</details>

*V. O. Galkin,I. S. Sukhanov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究J/ψ介子的半轻子和非轻子衰变过程，旨在在相对论性夸克模型框架下，基于准势方法和量子色动力学（QCD）对这些衰变进行系统分析。

Method: 采用基于准势方法和量子色动力学（QCD）的相对论性夸克模型，完全考虑相对论效应计算弱流强子矩阵元的形状因子，并将其表达为介子波函数的重叠积分。

Result: 计算得到的衰变分支比在10^{-9}~10^{-12}量级，涵盖了电子和μ子参与的半轻子衰变，并在颜色数N_c→∞极限下采用因子化近似处理非轻子衰变。

Conclusion: 研究结果与先前理论预测和现有实验上限进行了比较，为J/ψ介子衰变提供了系统的理论计算框架和数值预测。

Abstract: Exclusive semileptonic and nonleptonic $J/ψ$ decays are investigated in the framework of the relativistic quark model based on the quasipotential approach and quantum chromodynamics. The form factors parameterizing the hadronic matrix element of the weak current are calculated with the complete account of the relativistic effects. These form factors are expressed as the overlap integrals of the meson wave functions and are determined in the whole accessible kinematic range. On this basis the semileptonic decay branching fractions are evaluated for decays involving both electrons and muons. The nonleptonic decays are considered in the factorization approximation in the limit for the number of colors $N_c\to \infty$. The obtain branching fractions are found to be of the order $10^{-9}\sim 10^{-12}$. They are compared with the previous theoretical predictions and available experimental upper bounds.

Abstract: We investigate the high-energy production of tetraquark-jet systems at the LHC and its forthcoming High-Luminosity upgrade. Our analysis relies on the hadron-structure-oriented TQ4Q1.1 fragmentation functions, built within a nonrelativistic QCD framework that incorporates both gluon- and heavy-quark-initiated channels. Threshold-consistent DGLAP evolution is performed through the HF-NRevo scheme, enabling a unified treatment of mass thresholds and scale variations. We also provide a systematic discussion of uncertainties arising from color-composite long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs) and from perturbative hard- and fragmentation-scale inputs (H- and F-MHOUs). Phenomenological predictions are obtained using the (sym)Jethad framework at NLL/NLO$^+$ accuracy for semi-inclusive tetraquark-jet production at the LHC and beyond. This review connects the emerging spectroscopy of fully heavy exotics with modern fragmentation-based approaches to hadron structure and high-energy QCD.

### [64] [Many Wrongs Make a Right: Leveraging Biased Simulations Towards Unbiased Parameter Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02219)
*Ezequiel Alvarez,Sean Benevedes,Manuel Szewc,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模板自适应混合模型（Template-Adapted Mixture Model），用于在存在模拟-数据失配偏差的情况下进行信号分数估计，通过利用多个有偏模拟来减少域偏移引起的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理等科学领域中，参数推断依赖模拟连接理论与实验，但模拟-数据失配（simulation-data mismodeling）导致的偏差在标准推断流程中难以控制。特别是在信号分数估计（signal fraction estimation）中，需要从信号和背景的混合样本中推断信号比例，而两者分布可能极其复杂。

Method: 提出模板自适应混合模型（Template-Adapted Mixture Model），利用多个有偏模拟（biased simulations）对信号区域中每个过程分布进行数据驱动估计。该方法探索了模型选择、特征表示和统计方法等不同方法论选择，并在高斯玩具示例和半现实双希格斯测量中进行了应用。

Result: 所提出的方法成功利用有偏模拟提供了具有良好校准不确定性（well-calibrated uncertainties）的估计。该方法显著减少了由于模拟与现实之间的域偏移（domain shift）导致的信号分数偏差。

Conclusion: 模板自适应混合模型能够有效应对模拟-数据失配问题，通过数据驱动方法利用有偏模拟资源，在信号分数估计中实现偏差减少和不确定性校准，为粒子物理等领域的参数推断提供了改进方案。

Abstract: In particle physics, as in many areas of science, parameter inference relies on simulations to bridge the gap between theory and experiment. Recent developments in simulation-based inference have boosted the sensitivity of analyses; however, biases induced by simulation-data mismodeling can be difficult to control within standard inference pipelines. In this work, we propose a Template-Adapted Mixture Model to confront this problem in the context of signal fraction estimation: inferring the population proportion of signal in a mixed sample of signal and background, both of which follow arbitrarily complex distributions. We harness many biased simulations to perform data-driven estimates of each process distribution in the signal region, substantially reducing the bias on the signal fraction due to the domain shift between simulation and reality. We explore different methodological choices, including model selection, feature representation, and statistical method, and apply them to a Gaussian toy example and to a semi-realistic di-Higgs measurement. We find that the presented methods successfully leverage the biased simulations to provide estimates with well-calibrated uncertainties.

</details>


### [65] [Laser-assisted production of the light charged Higgs boson from top quark decay in the type-I two Higgs doublet model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01243)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用狄拉克-沃尔科夫形式（Dirac-Volkov formalism）对带电粒子与激光场的相互作用进行建模，并分析激光存在下衰变分支比的变化情况。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of a circularly polarized laser field on the top quark decay process into a charged Higgs boson ($t\rightarrow bH^+$) within the type-I two Higgs doublet model. Our study aims to explore how an external electromagnetic field can modify key observables and potentially facilitate the experimental detection of the charged Higgs boson, addressing challenges related to missing energy in collider experiments such as the LHC. Employing the Dirac-Volkov formalism, we model the interaction between charged particles and the laser field and demonstrate that the presence of the laser can notably influence the decay branching ratios under suitable conditions. The analysis reveals that both the intensity and frequency of the laser field play a crucial role in determining the decay width. In particular, for a laser field strength of $3.8\times 10^{14}$ V/cm and a photon energy of $0.117$ eV, the branching ratio of the top quark decaying into a charged Higgs boson with mass in the range $80$-$150$ GeV and a bottom quark reaches $0.97$, surpassing the standard $t\rightarrow bW^+$ channel. These results suggest that strong electromagnetic fields can serve as an effective mechanism to enhance signals of new particles, offering promising avenues for experimental searches beyond the Standard Model.

### [66] [Origin of the Covariant Wigner Operator as a Quantum Amplitude in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01248)
*Chueng-Ryong Ji,Daniel W. Piasecki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan（KvNS）经典力学表述扩展到相对论量子色动力学（QCD），证明Wigner函数可作为投影到经典相空间的量子概率幅（quantum probability amplitude）而非准概率密度，为QCD中的部分子分布函数提供了更清晰的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wigner函数在QCD中作为编码夸克、反夸克和胶子关联的相空间对象具有核心作用，但其准概率性质和可能的负值使其解释仍具微妙性。近期基于KvNS经典力学希尔伯特空间表述的研究表明，Wigner函数应被视为投影到经典相空间的量子概率幅，而非准概率密度。

Method: 通过构建夸克Wigner算符的Koopman描述，将KvNS视角扩展到相对论QCD。证明Wigner算符通过幂等投影（idempotent projection）自然同构于相空间旋量，提供了一个统一框架，其中经典和量子动力学均可表达。

Result: 在此表述中，Wigner函数即使在相对论区域仍保持其作为概率幅的解释。该视角阐明了负值和其他非经典特征的起源，并为QCD中的部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions）提供了更透明的基础。值得注意的是，相对论Koopman框架重现了QCD的经典极限。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan框架扩展到相对论量子色动力学，为Wigner函数提供了作为量子概率幅而非准概率密度的新解释，澄清了其非经典特征，并为QCD中的部分子分布函数建立了更清晰的理论基础。

Abstract: The Wigner function plays a central role in QCD as a phase space object encoding correlations among quarks, antiquarks, and gluons, yet its interpretation remains subtle due to its quasiprobabilistic nature and possible negativity. Recent work based on the Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan (KvNS) Hilbert space formulation of classical mechanics suggests the Wigner function arises as a \textit{quantum probability amplitude} projected onto classical phase space, rather than a quasiprobability density \citep{wignerphasespace, wave_operator}. In the classical limit, this amplitude reduces to the classical Koopman wavefunction. In this work, we extend this perspective to relativistic QCD by constructing a Koopman description of the quark Wigner operator. We show that the Wigner operator is naturally isomorphic to a phase space spinor via an idempotent projection, providing a unified framework in which both classical and quantum dynamics are expressed. Within this formulation, the Wigner function retains its interpretation as an amplitude even in the relativistic regime. This viewpoint clarifies the origin of negativity and other nonclassical features, and provides a more transparent foundation for parton distribution functions in QCD. Remarkably, the relativistic Koopman framework reproduces the classical limit of QCD.

</details>

*Dusty Aiello,Julian Heeck*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了Q-ball（Q-球）在任意空间维度d中的性质，包括一维精确解和高维薄壁近似，并将结果应用于真空衰变（vacuum decay）的反弹解（bounce solutions）。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将通常分析的三维Q-ball（Q-球）推广到任意空间维度d，并寻求解析解或近似解，同时探索其在真空衰变（vacuum decay）物理中的潜在应用。

Method: 研究方法包括：对于d=1维度，解析求解单场势（single-field potentials）的非线性微分方程；对于d>1维度，在薄壁或大Q-ball（thin-wall or large Q-ball）区域进行解析近似，并一致地包含第一阶次领头修正。

Result: 研究结果获得了d=1维度的精确解析解，以及d>1维度的薄壁近似解（thin-wall approximation），包括一致处理的第一阶次领头修正（first sub-leading correction）。

Conclusion: 由于Q-ball（Q-球）的微分方程形式与真空衰变反弹解（vacuum-decay bounce solutions）相同，该研究结果可直接应用于真空衰变（vacuum decay）领域。

Abstract: Scalars carrying a conserved global charge $Q$ can form stable localized field configurations composed of a large number of particles. These non-topological solitons are spherically symmetric and are called Q-balls. While usually analyzed in three spatial dimensions, these solitons can be straightforwardly generalized to $d$ spatial dimensions. For $d=1$, we can analytically solve the non-linear differential equation for an important class of single-field potentials; for $d>1$, we can analytically approximate the solutions in the thin-wall or large Q-ball regime, including the first sub-leading correction consistently. Since the underlying differential equations have the same form as vacuum-decay bounce solutions, our results find applications there, too.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用薄壁近似（thin-wall approximation）进行解析分析，并通过数值求解反弹解（bounce solutions）和计算相应的欧几里得作用量（Euclidean action）来研究厚壁情况。

Result: 对于足够大的过密度扰动，反弹解在气泡壁附近出现振荡中间阶段；小扰动情况下，过密度增强真空衰变率并减小初始气泡半径，欠密度则起抑制作用。数值计算在厚壁情况下进一步证实了这一行为。

Abstract: We investigate vacuum decays in the early Universe in the presence of curvature perturbations. For sufficiently large perturbations associated with over-densities, we find that the bounce solution develops an oscillating middle stage near the bubble wall. For small perturbations, we analytically show within the thin-wall approximation that an over- (under-) density would enhance (suppress) the vacuum decay rate with a smaller (larger) initial bubble radius. By numerically solving for the bounce solutions and evaluating the corresponding Euclidean action, we further confirm this behaviour in thick-wall cases. Our results indicate that over-densities can generically trigger vacuum decay at an earlier moment.

*Taushif Ahmed,Syed Mehedi Hasan,Andreas Rapakoulias*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用维度正规化（dimensional regularisation）和Mellin-Barnes（MB）表示法，将多重MB积分转化为实参数积分。通过部分分式分解处理多质量动量情况，并推导了高次分母积分与主积分之间的递推关系。

Result: 对于三分母情况：无质量结果计算至$\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$阶，单质量情况计算至$\mathcal{O}(ε)$阶；对于四分母情况：无质量和单质量情况均计算至$\mathcal{O}(ε^0)$阶。所有结果均用Goncharov多重对数（GPLs）表示。

Conclusion: 该方法成功解析计算了角相空间积分，为求解完整相空间积分提供了关键要素。通过部分分式分解和递推关系，能够处理更复杂的多质量动量情况。

Abstract: We compute angular phase-space integrals with three and four denominators analytically, working within dimensional regularisation via the Mellin-Barnes (MB) representation. The approach converts multifold MB integrals into real parametric integrals and expresses all results in terms of Goncharov polylogarithms (GPLs). For three denominators, all-massless results are obtained to $\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$ and the single-massive case to $\mathcal{O}(ε)$; for four denominators, both the massless and single-massive cases are solved to $\mathcal{O}(ε^0)$. Integrals with multiple massive momenta follow from a partial fraction decomposition reducing them to the single-massive case. Recursion relations relating integrals with higher denominator powers to master integrals are derived. These are essential ingredients to solving full phase-space integrals.

*R. Peschanski,B. G. Giraud*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现该振幅能够准确描述LHC能量下动量转移的凹陷-凸起（dip-bump）区域，与实验数据一致。振幅的解析形式展现出特定的标度性质，除了在$l_t$实轴上分数值处存在一系列极点（poles）外无其他奇异性。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了基于Regge理论的标度性描述框架，为正号振幅（Pomeron）在LHC能量下的pp弹性散射行为提供了理论解释，并揭示了振幅在$l_t$复平面中的解析结构特性。

Abstract: We examine the Regge theoretical properties for the scaling observed in pp elastic scattering differential cross-sections at the LHC. A positive signature amplitude (i.e. the Pomeron) with scaling properties has been derived. It is found to describe the dip-bump region of momentum transfer at LHC energies in agreement with data. We derive the analytic continuation in the whole plane of the t-channel partial waves of index $l_t$ specific to the Regge formalism. The analytic form of the amplitude exhibits a specific scaling property without singularities, except for a series of poles in the $l_t$ real axis at fractional values.

Abstract: A modification of the Einstein-Hilbert Lagrangian by introducing a coupling between the Weyl tensor and the stress-energy tensor was proposed to explain flat galactic rotation curves without the exotic (non-baryonic) dark matter (DM) [1]. The proposed coupling constant was previously determined by fitting the rotational velocities of the Milky Way and M31 modeled with constant density, yielding the same coupling constant for both [2,3]. ### [72] [Symmetries of (quasi)periodic materials: Superposability vs. Indistinguishability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01387)

Method: 通过材料空间自相关函数（autocorrelation functions）的傅里叶空间表示，获取周期和准周期材料的空间群（space groups）。提出一种图像处理方法，直接从介观结构的傅里叶变换中识别材料空间群的关键特征，包括点群（point group）和同态性（symmorphism）。

Result: 该方法在合成的二维（准）周期结构材料图像上得到验证。作为示例，研究明确指出经典彭罗斯拼图（Penrose tiling）具有十阶旋转对称性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种基于傅里叶分析的图像处理框架，能够有效识别（准）周期结构材料的空间群对称性特征，为材料对称性分析提供了实用工具。

Abstract: This work is devoted to the study of the symmetries of (quasi)periodic architectured materials. For this purpose, the weaker symmetry criterion of indistinguishability is used. It relies on a statistical description of the mesostructure and is defined in terms of the spatial autocorrelation functions of the material under consideration. By using the representation of these autocorrelation functions in Fourier space, the space groups of both periodic and quasiperiodic materials can be obtained. In this context, an image processing methodology is proposed to identify the key characteristics of a material's space group (i.e its point group and its symmorphism) directly from the Fourier transform of the mesostructure. The method is validated on synthetic two-dimensional images of (quasi)periodic architectured materials and it is pointed out, as an illustrative example, that the rotational symmetry of the classical Penrose tiling is of order ten.

### [73] [A Note on the Resolvent Algebra and Functional Integral Approach to the Free Bose Einstein Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01424)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从算子代数和泛函积分两种表述的对应关系出发，系统理解自由玻色气体中玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚的结构。这为分析相变的一般特征（如序参量（order parameters）的出现、态的分解和聚类性质）提供了具体范例。

Method: 方法基于基于解析子代数（resolvent algebra）的算子代数表述与泛函积分表示之间的对应关系。通过阐明有限温度BEC态的表示论结构，并严格分析其直积分分解（direct integral decomposition）与相关概率测度的遍历分解（ergodic decomposition）之间的对应关系。

Result: 建立了泛函积分方法中测度分解与算子代数表示分解之间的详细对应关系，从而确立了概率方面与代数方面的等价性。这为分离处理相互作用系统中红外奇异性（infrared singularities）时产生的额外数学复杂性提供了指导原则。

Conclusion: 这些结果为非相对论性构造性量子场论（non-relativistic constructive quantum field theory）和量子统计力学（quantum statistical mechanics）中相变的严格分析奠定了基础，并为扩展到相互作用模型提供了起点。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a systematic description of the structure of Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) in the free Bose gas from the viewpoint of the correspondence between the operator-algebraic formulation based on the resolvent algebra and the functional integral representation. By clarifying the representation-theoretic structure of finite-temperature BEC states and rigorously analyzing the correspondence between their direct integral decomposition and the ergodic decomposition of the associated probability measures, we provide a framework in which general features of phase transitions-such as the emergence of order parameters, the decomposition of states, and clustering properties-are explicitly described using BEC in the free Bose gas as a concrete example. Furthermore, we construct in detail the correspondence between the decomposition of measures in the functional integral approach and that of operator-algebraic representations, thereby establishing the equivalence between the probabilistic and algebraic aspects, and providing a guiding principle for isolating the essential structures by disentangling the additional mathematical complications arising from the treatment of infrared singularities in interacting systems. These results lay a foundation for the rigorous analysis of phase transitions in non-relativistic constructive quantum field theory and quantum statistical mechanics, and serve as a starting point for extensions to interacting models.

### [74] [Edge localization and Lifshitz tails for graphs with Ahlfors regular volume growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01584)
*Laura Shou,Wei Wang,Shiwen Zhang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究将安德森模型（Anderson model）从晶格推广到具有Ahlfors α-正则体积增长的图上，证明了在随机分布满足温和正则性条件下，谱底附近的Lifshitz尾估计导致格林函数分数矩的指数衰减，从而在低能区实现谱和动力学局域化。特别验证了谢尔宾斯基垫图（Sierpinski gasket graph）满足所有条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将安德森模型中关于局域化的现有结果从晶格$\mathbb{Z}^d$推广到更一般的Ahlfors α-正则图上。这类图具有分形结构，其体积增长特性与欧几里得空间不同，需要发展新的分析方法来理解无序系统中的电子局域化现象。

Method: 研究方法基于对具有Ahlfors α-正则体积增长图上的安德森模型进行分析。核心方法包括：1）利用Lifshitz尾（Lifshitz-tail）类型估计研究谱底附近的行为；2）证明格林函数（Green's function）分数矩的指数衰减；3）建立积分态密度（integrated density of states）的Lifshitz尾估计，其中Lifshitz指数由体积增长率与图上随机游走维度的比值决定。

Result: 主要结果包括：1）在随机分布满足温和正则性条件下，谱底附近的Lifshitz尾估计导致格林函数分数矩的指数衰减，从而在低能区实现谱局域化（spectral localization）和动力学局域化（dynamical localization）；2）建立了积分态密度的Lifshitz尾估计；3）验证了谢尔宾斯基垫图满足所有条件，证明在该图上，对于任意固定的无序强度，安德森模型在谱底附近具有纯点谱（pure point spectrum）并表现出强动力学局域化。

Conclusion: 该研究成功将安德森模型的局域化结果从晶格推广到Ahlfors α-正则图上，为理解分形结构上的无序系统提供了理论框架。特别地，在谢尔宾斯基垫图上的应用验证了理论的有效性，表明在温和正则性条件下，即使对于任意固定的无序强度，系统在低能区也会出现局域化现象。

Abstract: In this work, we study the Anderson model on graphs with Ahlfors $α$-regular volume growth. We show that, under mild regularity assumptions of the random distribution, Lifshitz-tail type estimates near the bottom of the spectrum lead to exponential decay of fractional moments of the Green's function and thus spectral and dynamical localization at low energies. This generalizes the result of [4] from the lattice $\mathbb{Z}^d$ to Ahlfors $α$-regular graphs. In addition, we establish Lifshitz tail estimates for the integrated density of states, with the Lifshitz exponent determined by the ratio of the volume growth rate and the random walk dimension of the underlying graphs, under certain assumptions on low lying eigenvalues of the Dirichlet and Neumann Laplacian on the graph. As an application, we verify all conditions on the Sierpinski gasket graph and obtain that, under mild regularity assumptions of the random distribution, for any fixed disorder, the Anderson model on the Sierpinski gasket graph has pure point spectrum and exhibits strong dynamical localization near the bottom of the spectrum.

### [75] [Functional relations in renormalization group methods for a class of ordinary differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01744)
*Atsuo Kuniba,Rurika Motohashi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文为包含半单或幂零线性部分的一阶系统及高阶标量方程，开发了基于重整化群（RG）的微扰方案。核心发现是朴素微扰理论中的长期项系数满足精确函数关系，从而统一推导出RG方法的基本特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为特定类型的常微分方程（ordinary differential equations）建立系统化的重整化群微扰方法。该方法旨在统一处理一阶系统（包括半单或幂零线性部分）和高阶标量方程，扩展先前针对二阶标量方程的研究成果。

Method: 方法基于重整化群（renormalization group, RG）框架，通过分析朴素微扰理论中产生的长期项（secular terms）系数。关键观察是这些系数满足精确的函数关系，从而能够统一推导RG方法的基本特征。

Result: 研究结果表明：重整化振幅满足具有群状结构的封闭函数关系；直接获得控制其慢动力学的RG方程；确保所有阶数均无长期项；裸振幅与重整化振幅之间的关系可显式求逆。这些结果扩展了先前对二阶标量方程的研究。

Conclusion: 结论是成功开发了基于重整化群的统一微扰方案，为处理包含半单或幂零线性部分的常微分方程提供了系统方法。该方法不仅统一推导了RG方法的基本特征，还确保了微扰展开的收敛性，并扩展了先前的研究范围。

Abstract: We develop a renormalization group (RG)-based perturbation scheme for a class of ordinary differential equations, including first-order systems with semisimple or nilpotent linear parts, as well as scalar higher-order equations. The key observation is that the secular coefficients arising in naive perturbation theory satisfy an exact functional relation. This yields, in a unified manner, several fundamental features of the RG method: the renormalized amplitudes satisfy a closed functional relation with a group-like structure, the RG equation governing their slow dynamics is obtained directly, the absence of secular terms is ensured to all orders, and the relation between bare and renormalized amplitudes admits an explicit inversion. The results extend earlier ones for second-order scalar equations.

</details>


### [76] [A Rigorous Functional-Integral Construction of Toral Chern-Simons Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02013)
*Daniel Galviz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过精确的zeta正则化高斯积分方法，构建了具有环面规范群（toral gauge group）的阿贝尔陈-西蒙斯理论（Abelian Chern-Simons theory）的泛函积分，并证明其在闭3-流形上产生拓扑不变量，在带边界流形上产生规范边界态，满足(2+1)维拓扑量子场论（TQFT）的公理。

Method: 采用zeta正则化高斯积分（zeta-regularized Gaussian evaluation）方法，对连接模规范（connections modulo gauge）的形式商积分进行精确计算。该方法通过严格的数学处理，避免了传统泛函积分中的发散问题，为拓扑量子场论提供了可靠的数学基础。

Result: 对于闭3-流形，该构造产生了一个拓扑不变量；对于带边界的流形，相对泛函积分（relative functional integral）产生了规范的边界态（canonical boundary state）。所得到的理论满足(2+1)维拓扑量子场论（TQFT）的所有必要公理。

Abstract: We construct the functional integral of Abelian Chern-Simons theory with toral gauge group $\mathbb T=\mathfrak t/Λ\cong U(1)^n$ at level $K$, where $K:Λ\timesΛ\to\mathbb Z$ is an even, integral, nondegenerate symmetric bilinear form, by exact zeta-regularized Gaussian evaluation of the formal quotient integral over connections modulo gauge. For closed $3$-manifolds, this yields a topological invariant; for manifolds with boundary, the relative functional integral produces the canonical boundary state. The resulting theory satisfies the required axioms of a $(2+1)$-dimensional TQFT.

### [77] [Tensor invariants for multipartite entanglement classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02269)
*Sylvain Carrozza,Johann Chevrier,Luca Lionni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入迹不变量（trace-invariants）及其对应的彩色图（colored graphs）组合对象，系统分析了多体量子系统的纠缠结构分类问题，特别关注参考态（reference states）的局部幺正轨道（LU-orbits）分离和纠缠资源理论中的关系表征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子系统的纠缠结构组织比两体情况更具挑战性：两体纯态的局部幺正轨道可由纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）方便地表征，而多体纠缠不变量（multipartite entanglement invariants）则难以定义和处理。这种差异的根本原因在于两体问题可简化为矩阵不变量分析，而多体版本则由更丰富的张量不变量（tensor invariants）空间所支配。

Method: 研究通过迹不变量（trace-invariants）的视角探索多体纠缠结构，该不变量与彩色图（colored graphs）组合对象一一对应。首先解释迹不变量评估如何标记多体纯态的局部幺正轨道，如何扩展到随机态，以及如何通过此类数据分析局部操作（LO）效应。然后聚焦于参考态（reference states）子空间中的纠缠分类，其基本构建块是不同维度的GHZ态。

Result: 研究表明相对简单的迹不变量子类足以分离参考态的局部幺正轨道，并能在纠缠资源理论中实现局部操作（LO）关系的完整表征（以及LOCC关系的不完整表征）。此外，研究探讨了如何在渐近大N展开中高效区分局部维度为N的参考态子类（包括与Haar随机态的区分），该分析依赖于与彩色图相关的组合量，其中部分已在随机张量文献中发挥重要作用。

Conclusion: 通过迹不变量和彩色图组合框架，该工作为多体纠缠结构分类提供了系统方法，特别在参考态子空间中实现了局部幺正轨道的有效分离和纠缠资源理论关系的表征。研究还展示了如何在渐近极限下高效区分特定参考态类别，为多体纠缠分析提供了新的组合数学工具。

Abstract: Organising the space of entanglement structures of a multipartite quantum system is a much more challenging task than its bipartite version: while the local unitary (LU) orbit of a bipartite pure state can be conveniently characterized by its entanglement spectrum, invariants of multipartite entanglement structures are comparatively difficult to define and work with. The root cause of this difference is that the bipartite problem can be reduced to the analysis of matrix invariants, while its multipartite version is governed by a much richer space of tensor invariants. The present work explores the latter through the lens of so-called trace-invariants, which are in one-to-one correspondence with combinatorial objects known as colored graphs. We first explain why trace-invariant evaluations can serve as labels of LU-orbits of multipartite pure states, how this strategy extends to random states, and how the effect of local operations (LO) can be analyzed through such data. We then focus on entanglement classification within an (infinite-dimensional) subspace of reference states, whose basic building blocks are GHZ states of various dimensions. We show that relatively simple subclasses of trace-invariants are sufficient to separate the LU-orbits of reference states, and enable a complete (resp. an incomplete) characterization of their relations in the LO (resp. LOCC) resource theory of entanglement. Finally, we investigate how a (still infinite) subclass of reference states of local dimension N can be efficiently distinguished at leading and subleading orders in an asymptotic large-N expansion (among themselves, or from Haar-random states). This analysis relies crucially on combinatorial quantities associated to colored graphs, some of which have already played instrumental roles in the recent literature on random tensors. Results of broader relevance are reported along the way.

</details>

### [80] [Quantum structure of the chiral vortical effect and boundary-induced vortical pumping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01293)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性涡旋效应（chiral vortical effect, CVE）存在于从相对论性流体到外尔半金属的多种系统中，但其量子起源尚不明确，因为现有推导都是半经典的。需要建立完全量子的理论框架来理解这一效应。

Method: 提出了有限圆柱中旋转外尔费米子的精确量子解。通过分析体响应和边界条件，特别是自旋极化边界条件，揭示了涡旋响应的量子机制。

Result: 发现体涡旋响应完全由磁化电流（magnetization current）贡献，而旋转轴上的电流密度保持有限且与半经典预测一致。对于自旋极化边界条件，发现了超出已知CVE的额外效应：一个稳健的手性模式家族，能够在旋转角度Δθ下输运轴荷ΔQ=χN²Δθ/4π。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了CVE的完全量子图像，揭示了外尔系统中涡旋响应背后的边界强制手性谱结构。泵浦效应与温度、费米能级和外尔速度无关，但依赖于紫外敏感数N。

Abstract: The chiral vortical effect (CVE) -- an axial current driven by rotation in chiral matter -- appears in systems ranging from relativistic fluids to Weyl semimetals, yet its quantum origin remains unclear because existing derivations are semiclassical. We present an exact quantum solution of a rotating Weyl fermion in a finite cylinder. We show that the bulk vortical response is entirely a magnetization current while the current density on the rotation axis remains finite and matches semiclassical predictions. For spin-polarized boundary conditions, we uncover an additional effect beyond the known CVE: a robust family of chiral modes that transport axial charge, $ΔQ=χN^2\,Δθ/4π$, under rotation by angle $Δθ$, where $χ$ is the Weyl node chirality and $N$ is the number of chiral modes. The pump is independent of temperature, Fermi level and Weyl velocities, but depends on the UV-sensitive number $N$. These results establish a fully quantum picture of the CVE and reveal a boundary-enforced chiral spectral structure underlying vortical response in Weyl systems.

### [81] [Bond-density-wave orders induced by geometric frustration in the kagome metal CeRu3Si2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01691)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何阻挫在自旋和电荷系统中产生了丰富的简并基态和竞争有序相，但基于化学键的类似相尚未得到明确证实。本研究旨在探索kagome金属中由几何阻挫约束的复杂键有序态。

Method: 通过同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）、实空间透射电子显微镜（real-space transmission electron microscopy）和模型计算，研究团队观测了CeRu₃Si₂中的结构调制。

Result: 在室温以上发现了两种不同的长周期超晶格，分别具有谐波和非谐波结构调制。kagome平面之间的层间键以子晶格选择性的方式调制，以满足kagome晶格上的零和约束。

Conclusion: 研究证明了kagome金属具有承载由几何阻跃约束的复杂键有序态的潜力，并确立了化学键作为量子材料中阻挫物理的独特途径，即使在室温以上也能实现。

Abstract: Geometric frustration gives rise to vast manifolds of degenerate ground states and competing orders in spin and charge systems. Typically, classical ground states are governed by a local ``zero-sum constraint" that relieves frustrated antiferromagnetic interactions or Coulomb repulsion. To date, the paradigm of geometric frustration has yielded a rich landscape of emergent phases, from spin ices and quantum spin liquids to charge glasses. However, an analogous phase rooted in chemical bonding has yet to be firmly demonstrated. Here we report the discovery of bond-density-wave orders induced by geometric frustration in the kagome metal CeRu$_3$Si$_2$ above room temperature. Through synchrotron X-ray diffraction, real-space transmission electron microscopy, and model calculations, we observe two distinct long-period superlattices with harmonic and anharmonic structural modulations. Crucially, interlayer bonds between kagome planes modulate in a sublattice-selective manner to fulfill the zero-sum constraint on the kagome lattice. We demonstrate the potential of kagome metals to host complex bond-ordered states constrained by geometric frustration and establish chemical bonding as a distinct pathway to frustration physics in quantum materials even above room temperature.

### [82] [Sign-Free Evidence for a d-Wave Superfluid Stiffness Dome in the Doped Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01737)
*Xidi Wang,H. Q. Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过行列式量子蒙特卡罗（DQMC）方法，从虚时传播子的蒙特卡罗平均矩阵对数构造有效单粒子哈密顿量K_eff，将乘法符号问题转化为加性框架，从而消除符号问题。应用于哈伯德模型时，K_eff揭示了d波赝隙和自旋涨落配对的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子蒙特卡罗方法中的符号问题（sign problem）限制了强关联系统的研究。本文旨在通过构造有效单粒子哈密顿量K_eff，将乘法符号问题转化为加性框架，从而消除符号问题，实现对强关联系统非微扰特性的准确描述。

Method: 从行列式量子蒙特卡罗（determinant quantum Monte Carlo, DQMC）的虚时传播子（imaginary-time propagator）的蒙特卡罗平均矩阵对数构造有效单粒子哈密顿量K_eff。该方法将乘法符号问题映射到加性框架，利用中心极限定理保证收敛，使K_eff成为无符号问题的可观测量。

Result: 应用于哈伯德模型（t'/t = -0.30, U/t = 4）时，K_eff揭示了低于计算相变温度T*的d波赝隙（d-wave pseudogap）和强节点-反节点二分性。三个无符号问题的可观测量支持自旋涨落配对机制：1）能隙比R_g > 1确认d波对称性；2）超流刚度ρ_s在掺杂范围内形成穹顶结构；3）S(π,π)在掺杂范围内近似平坦，表明穹顶结构源于费米面几何对均匀自旋涨落胶水的响应。

Conclusion: K_eff方法成功消除了符号问题，能够非微扰地捕捉精确关联单粒子谱。赝隙随半填充单调增长而超流刚度形成穹顶，这与铜氧化物超导体中Tc受超流密度限制的Uemura关系现象学一致。顶点修正（vertex corrections）仍有待量化。

Abstract: We construct an effective single-particle Hamiltonian $K_{\mathrm{eff}}$ from Monte Carlo--averaged matrix logarithms of the imaginary-time propagator in determinant quantum Monte Carlo (DQMC). The logarithm maps the multiplicative sign problem into an additive framework where the central limit theorem guarantees convergence, rendering $K_{\mathrm{eff}}$ sign-problem-free: both sign sectors yield identical dispersions to $<1\%$. $K_{\mathrm{eff}}$ captures the exact correlated single-particle spectrum, incorporating all self-energy effects non-perturbatively. Applied to the Hubbard model ($t'/t = -0.30$, $U/t = 4$), $K_{\mathrm{eff}}$ reveals a $d$-wave pseudogap with strong nodal-antinodal dichotomy below a computational phase transition at $T^*$. Three sign-free observables provide evidence consistent with spin-fluctuation pairing: (i) the gap ratio $R_g > 1$ confirms $d$-wave symmetry -- a temperature-independent property of the correlated band structure that provides the medium for pairing; (ii) the superfluid stiffness $ρ_s$ forms a dome across doping at $L = 8$, $10$, and $12$, exceeding the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless threshold by $5$-$7\times$ at the dome peak; (iii) $S(π,π)$ is approximately flat across doping, establishing that the dome originates from Fermi-surface geometry responding to uniform spin-fluctuation glue. The pseudogap grows monotonically toward half-filling while $ρ_s$ forms a dome, mirroring cuprate phenomenology where $T_c$ is limited by the superfluid density (Uemura relation). Vertex corrections remain to be quantified.

### [83] [Bond-Length-Driven Magnetic Transition in Quasi-One-Dimensional CrSb$X_3$ ($X$=S, Se)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01810)
*Kang Lee,Hong-Suk Choi,K. -W. Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算研究了准一维绝缘体CrSbX₃（X=S, Se）的磁性基态，发现磁有序对Cr-Cr键长高度敏感，键长增加会导致反铁磁到铁磁的转变，这一转变由最近邻超交换作用J₁的符号反转主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究准一维绝缘体CrSbX₃（X=S, Se）的磁性基态，探索其磁有序对结构参数的敏感性，特别是Cr-Cr键长变化如何影响磁相变。

Method: 采用第一性原理（ab initio）计算，在传统能带理论框架下进行，未显式考虑库仑关联作用（U），通过分析交换相互作用来理解磁相变机制。

Result: 发现磁有序对Cr-Cr键长d_Cr-Cr高度敏感：键长增加在临界距离d^c_Cr-Cr ≈ 3.53 (±0.05) Å处诱导反铁磁到铁磁的转变。CrSbS₃位于转变边界附近，而CrSbSe₃为稳定的铁磁态，与实验一致。

Conclusion: 一级相变主要由硫族离子介导的链内最近邻超交换作用J₁的符号反转主导，而链内直接交换作用J₂保持铁磁性且变化平缓。这种行为反映了准一维过渡金属系统中竞争交换路径驱动的类Bethe-Slater行为。

Abstract: Using {\it ab initio} calculations, we investigate the magnetic ground states of quasi-one-dimensional insulating CrSb$X_3$ ($X$ = S, Se) with infinite double-rutile chains. Within conventional band theory, without explicit Coulomb correlations ($U$), we obtain band gaps in close agreement with experiment. Remarkably, we find that the magnetic order is highly sensitive to the Cr-Cr bond length $d_{\rm Cr-Cr}$: increasing the bond length induces a transition from antiferromagnetic to ferromagnetic order at a critical distance $d^c_{\rm Cr-Cr} \approx 3.53 (\pm 0.05)$ Å. Accordingly, CrSbS$_3$ lies near the transition boundary, whereas CrSbSe$_3$ is robustly ferromagnetic, in good agreement with experiment. Analysis of the exchange interactions reveals that the first-order phase transition is dominated by a sign reversal of the intrachain nearest-neighbor superexchange $J_1$ mediated by chalcogen ions, while the intrachain direct exchange $J_2$ remains ferromagnetic and changes only gradually. This behavior reflects an emergent Bethe-Slater-like behavior driven by competing exchange pathways in a quasi-1D transition-metal system, where the competition between $J_1$ and $J_2$ dictates the magnetic ground state. Besides, the electronic structures of the ground states of each compound are investigated.

</details>


### [84] [Detecting Symmetry-Resolved Entanglement: A Quantum Monte Carlo Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02307)
*Kuangjie Chen,Weizhen Jia,Xiaopeng Li,René Meyer,Jiarui Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）方法，用于计算大规模相互作用系统中的对称性分解的Rényi熵（SRRE），通过测量副本流形上的无序（对称性扭曲）算符并从相应的带电矩重建SRRE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性和纠缠是量子多体物理中的两个基本概念，它们的相互作用通过对称性分解的纠缠（symmetry-resolved entanglement）来刻画。然而，在强相互作用的高维量子系统中计算对称性分解的纠缠仍然具有挑战性。

Method: 本文引入了一种量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo, QMC）方法，通过测量副本流形（replica manifolds）上的无序（对称性扭曲）算符（disorder/symmetry-twisted operators），并从相应的带电矩（charged moments）重建对称性分解的Rényi熵（symmetry-resolved Rényi entropies, SRRE）。

Result: 在一维横向场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model, TFIM）中，恢复了无序算符对数标度的共形场论预测，并观察到预期的纠缠等分（entanglement equipartition）趋近。在二维中，数据提供了与(2+1)D伊辛临界点处纠缠等分一致的数值证据。在一维海森堡链（Heisenberg chain）中，获得了与U(1)分解扇区中预期渐近标度和有限尺寸修正一致的结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为相互作用晶格模型中的对称性分解纠缠建立了一条实用的数值路径，并为超越一维的未来研究提供了一个有用的框架。

Abstract: Symmetry and entanglement are two fundamental concepts in quantum many-body physics. Their interplay is captured by symmetry-resolved entanglement, which decomposes the total entanglement into contributions from different symmetry sectors. Computing symmetry-resolved entanglement in strongly interacting higher-dimensional quantum systems remains challenging. Here, we introduce a quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) approach for computing symmetry-resolved Rényi entropies (SRRE) in large-scale interacting systems by measuring disorder (symmetry-twisted) operators on replica manifolds and reconstructing SRRE from the corresponding charged moments. We apply this method to the transverse-field Ising model (TFIM) in one and two dimensions. In one dimension, we recover the conformal-field-theory prediction for the logarithmic scaling of the disorder operator and observe the expected approach to entanglement equipartition. In two dimensions, our data provide numerical evidence consistent with entanglement equipartition at the (2+1)D Ising critical point. We further apply the framework to the 1D Heisenberg chain and obtain results consistent with the expected asymptotic scaling and finite-size corrections in the U(1)-resolved sectors. Our work establishes a practical numerical route to symmetry-resolved entanglement in interacting lattice models and provides a useful framework for future studies beyond one dimension.

### [85] [Hydrodynamic Backflow for Easing the Fermion Sign in Finite-Temperature Electron Path Integral Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01963)
*Ingvars Vitenburgs,Jarvist Moore Frost*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种结合流体动力学回流坐标变换与机器学习的方法，以缓解有限温度量子物质模拟中的费米子符号问题，并在二维电子气系统中实现了多个数量级的误差降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室温超导体和可控核聚变材料等系统需要精确描述有限温度量子物质。随机路径积分方法虽能精确处理有限温度问题，但受制于费米子符号问题（Fermion sign problem），其计算复杂度随系统规模急剧增加。

Method: 首先采用连续归一化流（continuous normalizing flow）机器学习方法确定最优参数，但训练存在数值问题。随后开发了半解析方法，通过依赖玻色子可观测量（Bosonic observable）的推导表达式来估计最优参数，避免了符号问题。

Result: 回流变换（backflow transformation）将问题降低了多个数量级，特别是在有限温度下谐波阱中的二维电子气系统。系统总能量与先前未经回流变换的研究结果一致，并计算了最多32个电子的能量。主要限制因素来自回流坐标变换中雅可比矩阵（Jacobian）的O(N³)计算。

Conclusion: 该方法为模拟当前无法触及的电子系统提供了途径。作为具体应用案例，计算了石墨烯量子点材料的量子电容（quantum capacitance），展示了在储能系统中的实际应用潜力。

Abstract: Some notable systems, such as room-temperature superconductors and materials for controlled nuclear fusion, require an accurate description of finite-temperature quantum matter. Stochastic path integral methods are finite-temperature and numerically exact, but scale poorly with system size due the notorious Fermion sign problem. To somewhat mitigate this, we use a hydrodynamical backflow coordinate transformation. Our first attempt was a continuous normalizing flow machine learning approach to determine the optimal parameters. We found this to reduce the error of the total energy, approximately, three times at medium sign severity. Numerical issues challenged training effectively. Thus, a semi-analytic approach was developed to estimate the optimal parameters. We do this by using a derived expression dependent on a Bosonic observable. Hence, the calculation of these values does not have a sign problem. The resulting backflow transformations reduce the problem by multiple orders of magnitude, specifically, in the case of a harmonically trapped, two-dimensional electron gas at finite-temperature. The total energy of the system agrees with previous, backflow untransformed, studies and we calculate energies for up to 32 electrons. The limiting factor is found to be, primarily, the $O(N^3)$ calculation of the Jacobian, stemming from the coordinate transformation of the backflow. A more thorough implementation may further improve this scaling. Otherwise, a pathway for simulating electron systems at currently unreachable regimes is obtained. Finally, as a specific practical use case in energy storage systems, the quantum capacitance for graphene quantum dot materials is calculated.

</details>

Abstract: The tunability and twist engineering of van der Waals materials enable the emergence of electronic states not present in individual monolayers. Interestingly, in its bulk form, the insulating gap is not correlation-driven, but stems from interlayer coupling. Here, we exploit the stacking-dependent nature of the insulating gap to show that in twisted 1T-TaS$_2$ bilayers, the spatially dependent competition between many-body and single-particle gaps creates Mott-trivial mosaic superlattices, featuring regions with local magnetic moments and non-magnetic insulating regions. We further demonstrate the tunability of the mosaic correlated state with an interlayer bias, giving rise to controllable charge transfer and quenching of correlations. Abstract: The entangled charge and spin dynamics in strongly electron correlated system has been a fruitful playground for exploring new physical phenomena. Here with resonant inelastic X-ray scattering we studied the spin dynamics of SrIrO$_3$, a half-filled paramagnetic semimetal hosting highly itinerant Dirac Fermions due to its topological band structure. Our results show that its magnetic excitations share much similarity to the ordered compounds upon Sn substitution in exchange strength and AFM instability, while the system maintains spin non-ordered. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛模拟（Markov-chain Monte Carlo simulation）并结合平行回火技术（parallel tempering technique）以加速弛豫动力学。

Result: 发现系统经历二阶相变进入具有${\mathbb Z_3}\times {\mathbb Z_2}$对称性破缺的磁有序相；低温相保持宏观简并性，残余熵约为$\mathcal{S}\sim0.1767/{\rm spin}$。

Conclusion: 残余熵在磁有序形成中起主要作用：畴壁生成受到抑制，因其会减少二十面体中储存的局部残余熵；磁有序作为熵结晶（entropic crystallization）从这种竞争中产生，揭示了具有大几何单元的强阻挫系统的普遍机制。

Abstract: We have studied the antiferromagnetic Ising model on the icosahedral bcc lattice, as a model system of 1/1 approximant Tsai-type quasicrystals. We addressed thermal equilibrium properties of this system with Markov-chain Monte Carlo simulation supplemented with the parallel tempering technique to accelerate the relaxation dynamics. As a result, we found a second-order phase transition takes place to the magnetic ordered phase with ${\mathbb Z_3}\times {\mathbb Z_2}$ symmetry breaking. Despite the ordering, the low-temperature phase keeps macroscopic degeneracy as identified by finite residual entropy, $\mathcal{S}\sim0.1767/{\rm spin}$. Remarkably, the existence of residual entropy turns out to play a major role in the formation of magnetic order. Generation of domain wall is suppressed, as it reduces the residual entropy locally stored in icosahedra, beyond the gain of configurational entropy due to domain wall patterns. Magnetic order arises out of this competition as entropic crystallization, which manifest universal mechanism of strongly frustrated systems with large geometrical units.

### [89] [Taste-splitting mass and edge modes in $3+1$~D staggered fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02078)
*Tatsuhiro Misumi,Tetsuya Onogi,Tatsuya Yamaoka*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 研究3+1维交错费米子（staggered fermion）哈密顿量的对称性结构及其异常（anomaly）含义，发现特定单链质量项（one-link mass term）保留较大剩余对称性，其畴壁（domain wall）系统在低能极限下产生2+1维边界上的无质量狄拉克费米子，并实现边界理论的宇称异常（parity anomaly）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究3+1维交错费米子哈密顿量的对称性结构及其对异常现象的影响。由于狄拉克费米子的自旋和味道自由度分布在晶格上，交错费米子系统除了标准在位质量项外，还允许单链、双链和三链双线性项作为局域、电荷守恒的质量项。

Method: 识别所有双线性质量项的自旋味道结构，确定每种质量项所保留的对称性。特别关注保留较大剩余对称性的单链质量项，并分析其畴壁剖面（kink profile）产生的畴壁系统。在低能极限下研究3+1维体态（bulk）和2+1维畴壁上的物理。

Result: 发现特定单链质量项保留与昂萨格代数（Onsager algebra）相关的守恒电荷所生成的较大剩余对称性。在畴壁系统中，3+1维体态出现能隙（gapped），而2+1维畴壁上出现两味道无质量狄拉克费米子作为局域模式。体态守恒电荷在畴壁上作为味道SU(2)对称性的生成元作用。

Conclusion: 当边界理论同时施加SU(2)对称性和空间反射对称性时，不允许对称质量能隙，这实现了边界理论的宇称异常。表明边界味道对称性和异常来源于紫外交错费米子哈密顿量，而非仅在红外极限下涌现。

Abstract: We investigate the symmetry structure of the $3+1$ D staggered fermion Hamiltonian and its implications for anomalies. Since the spin and flavor degrees of freedom of Dirac fermions are distributed over the lattice, in addition to the standard on-site mass term, the staggered fermion system also admits one-, two-, and three-link bilinear terms within a unit cube as local, charge conserving mass terms with different spin and flavor dependence. We identify the spin flavor structures of all those bilinear mass terms and determine the symmetries preserved by each of them. Among them, one of the one-link mass terms preserves a larger residual symmetry associated with conserved charges that generate the Onsager algebra. Motivated by this structure, we consider a kink profile of the one-link mass and analyze the resulting domain-wall system. In the low-energy limit, the $3+1$ D bulk becomes gapped, while two-flavor massless Dirac fermions appear as localized modes on the $2+1$ D domain wall. We show that the bulk conserved charges act on the wall as generators of a flavor $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ symmetry, and that no symmetric mass gap is allowed for the boundary theory when this $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ symmetry and space reflection symmetry are both imposed. This realizes the parity anomaly of the boundary theory and shows that the boundary flavor symmetry and anomaly descend from the ultraviolet staggered-fermion Hamiltonian rather than emerging only in the infrared.
