### [91] [Temperature and integrability-breaking correspondence via adiabatic transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01285)
*Hyeongjin Kim,Souvik Bandyopadhyay,Anatoli Polkovnikov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了温度与可积性破坏之间的对应关系，表明降低温度可将系统导向可积点，即使存在强可积性破坏相互作用。局域可观测量自相关函数呈现慢弛豫动力学，违反遍历性，而稳态的平均保真度磁化率在可积点附近满足标度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在通过几何和绝热变换的视角，揭示经典和量子多体系统中温度与可积性破坏之间的对应关系。核心动机是探索温度作为混沌可调控制参数的可能性，并将其置于与可积性破坏微扰同等重要的地位。

Method: 采用几何和绝热变换（adiabatic transformations）方法，通过标准方式（熵对能量的导数）降低温度。分析局域可观测量（local observables）的自相关函数（auto-correlation functions）和稳态的平均保真度磁化率（average fidelity susceptibility），研究系统在可积点附近的动力学行为和标度关系。

Result: 降低温度可将系统导向可积点，即使存在强可积性破坏相互作用。自相关函数呈现慢弛豫动力学，违反遍历性（ergodicity）。稳态的平均保真度磁化率在可积点附近满足标度关系，类似于连续相变（continuous phase transitions）。弛豫动力学指数在量子与经典模型中可能不同，取决于系统维度。

Conclusion: 研究确立了温度作为混沌可调控制参数的地位，将其置于与可积性破坏微扰同等重要的地位。温度降低可将系统导向可积点，导致慢弛豫动力学和遍历性破坏，而稳态性质在可积点附近呈现类似相变的标度行为。

Abstract: We reveal a correspondence between temperature and integrability-breaking in classical and quantum many-body systems through the lens of geometry and adiabatic transformations. Decreasing the temperature, obtained in a standard way through the derivative of entropy with respect to energy, steers the system towards an integrable point despite strong integrability-breaking interactions. Auto-correlation functions of local observables exhibit slow relaxation dynamics, which violates ergodicity on the approach to this integrable point. Subsequently, the average fidelity susceptibility of stationary states satisfies scaling relations near the integrable point, in close analogy with continuous phase transitions. We further find that the dynamical exponent encompassing relaxation can be different in the quantum and classical models, depending on dimension of the systems. Collectively, our results establish temperature as a tunable control parameter for chaos and puts it on equal footing with integrability-breaking perturbations.

### [92] [The topological gap at criticality: scaling exponent d + η, universality, and scope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01484)
*Matthew Loftus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出拓扑间隙Δ作为自旋模型临界相关性的度量，建立了有限尺寸标度律，并在二维伊辛模型和三维态Potts模型中验证了标度指数α = d+η的关系，同时确定了该框架的适用范围边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索拓扑间隙（topological gap）Δ作为自旋模型临界相关性的有效度量，该间隙定义为多数自旋α复形与密度匹配零模型之间的H1总持久性差异。

Method: 方法基于建立有限尺寸标度律：Δ(L,T) = A L^{d+η} G_-(L|t/T_c|)，其中G_-(x) ∼ (1+x/x_0)^{-(1+β/ν)}。通过分析二维伊辛模型和二维三维态Potts模型的大规模模拟数据（L最大至1024），验证标度指数关系。

Result: 对于二维伊辛模型，α = 2.249 ± 0.038，与d+η = 9/4的理论值高度一致（0.03σ差异）；G_-指数γ = 1.089 ± 0.077，符合1+β/ν = 9/8的理论预测。对于二维三维态Potts模型，α = 2.272 ± 0.024，与d+η = 2.267的理论值接近（0.2σ差异）。

Conclusion: 结论表明标度关系α = d+η在修正项为代数形式（ω > 0）时成立，但在对数修正（ω → 0）时失效。该框架不适用于一级相变、BKT相变和渗流相变，且对于二维四态Potts模型和原始三维伊辛模型需要密度归一化处理才能恢复标度关系。

Abstract: The topological gap $Δ= TP_{H_1}^{real} - TP_{H_1}^{shuf}$ -- the excess $H_1$ total persistence of the majority-spin alpha complex over a density-matched null -- encodes critical correlations in spin models. We establish finite-size scaling: $Δ(L,T) = A L^{d+η} G_-(L|t/T_c|)$, with $G_-(x) \sim (1+x/x_0)^{-(1+β/ν)}$. For 2D Ising, $α= 2.249 \pm 0.038$, matching $d+η= 9/4$ to $0.03σ$; the $G_-$ exponent $γ= 1.089 \pm 0.077$ is consistent with $1+β/ν= 9/8$ ($ΔR^2 < 10^{-5}$). For 2D Potts $q=3$ with $L$ up to 1024, $α= 2.272 \pm 0.024$ ($0.2σ$ from $d+η= 2.267$), with two-term corrections to scaling ($R^2 = 0.9999$). The $G_-$ exponent $γ= 1.114$ (68% CI $[1.053, 1.173]$) matches $1+β/ν= 17/15$. Scope boundaries: the law fails for 2D Potts $q=4$ ($α= 2.347 \pm 0.017$, $9.3σ$ from $d+η= 5/2$) where logarithmic corrections prevent convergence, and for raw 3D Ising ($4σ$ from $d+η$), but density normalization $Δ/|M|^{1/2}$ recovers $α= 3.06 \pm 0.04$ ($0.6σ$). The framework fails for first-order, BKT, and percolation. The criterion: $α= d+η$ holds when corrections to scaling are algebraic ($ω> 0$) but fails when logarithmic ($ω\to 0$).

</details>

Abstract: In networks that grow by isotropic redirection (IR), a new node selects an initial target node uniformly at random and attaches to a randomly chosen neighbor of the target. The emerging networks exhibit leaf proliferation, in which the number of nonleaves scales sublinearly as $N^μ$ and the degree distribution has an algebraic tail with exponent $1+μ$. To understand these mysterious properties, we introduce a class of models with redirection to leaves whenever possible. The resulting networks exhibit qualitatively similar phenomenology to IR networks, but avoid the inherent non-locality of the IR growth rule. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制方程（governing equations）的发现是物理学及相关领域的核心问题，通常受对称性约束。手动构建方程时，利用对称性约束限制项是首要步骤，但对于具有高阶导数或多场的复杂系统往往难以处理。数据驱动方法中施加物理约束通常需要手动预处理或计算昂贵的迭代过程。

Result: 该方法能够识别具有二面体对称性（dihedral symmetry）系统的不变项，并恢复Toner-Tu和Kardar-Parisi-Zhang系统的控制方程，包括对扩展已知模型有用的高阶项。解提供了对称性允许项的完整列表。

Abstract: Discovering governing equations, whether manually or by data-driven methods, has been central in physics and related areas. Since governing equations are typically constrained by a set of symmetries, using symmetry constraints to restrict terms is usually the first step in manually formulating a governing equation, but it often becomes intractable for complex systems with high-order derivatives or multiple fields. When a data-driven method is used, on the other hand, imposing physical constraints such as symmetries typically requires manual preprocessing or computationally expensive iterative procedures. Here, we propose an algebraic filtering method that enumerates all symmetry-allowed terms for continuum equations within a finite candidate space. By treating symmetry generators as linear operators on the candidate space, we reduce the problem of enforcing both discrete and continuous symmetries to solving a set of linear kernel equations. The solution yields a provably complete list of permitted terms. We demonstrate the method's effectiveness by identifying invariant terms for systems with dihedral symmetry and recovering the governing equations for the Toner--Tu and Kardar--Parisi--Zhang systems, including higher-order terms useful for extending known models. The method provides a systematic way to obtain a symmetry-allowed search space for data-driven equation discovery, e.g., the sparse identification of nonlinear dynamics method.

### [100] [Spatial Correlations Restore Zwanzig's Mean-Field Diffusion Result in Rugged Energy Landscapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02143)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序环境中的输运通常由罕见的极端事件主导，而非典型涨落。Zwanzig经典平均场理论预测能量粗糙度会降低扩散系数，但该预测在无关联高斯景观中失效，因为罕见但深的多位点陷阱主导输运并导致更强的扩散抑制。

Method: 提出了一个统一的理论框架，将Zwanzig的局域平均解释为高斯累积展开（Gaussian cumulant expansion）。通过引入高斯空间关联（Gaussian spatial correlations）来重塑能量景观，分析空间关联如何修改陷阱统计并恢复平均场扩散。

Abstract: Transport in disordered environments is often controlled not by typical fluctuations but by rare, extreme events that dominate long-time dynamics. In such settings, Zwanzig's classic mean-field theory predicts that energetic roughness reduces the diffusion coefficient by an exponential factor governed solely by the variance of the disorder. However, this prediction breaks down in uncorrelated Gaussian landscapes, where rare but deep multi-site traps dominate transport and lead to a much stronger suppression of diffusion. Here, we present a unified theoretical framework that clarifies both the origin of this breakdown and its resolution. We show that Zwanzig's local averaging can be interpreted as a Gaussian cumulant expansion whose validity is destroyed by uncorrelated disorder through the emergence of extreme trapping events. Introducing Gaussian spatial correlations fundamentally reshapes the landscape: roughness increments become smoother, asymmetric multi-site traps are suppressed, and the statistics of escape pathways are regularized. As a result, Zwanzig's exponential scaling is recovered. We provide an explicit analytical derivation demonstrating how spatial correlations modify trap statistics and restore mean-field diffusion, complemented by illustrative numerical examples showing the dramatic reduction of escape times in correlated landscapes.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索各向异性（anisotropic）反射对称跳跃的守恒质量输运过程中，质心（center-of-mass, CoM）守恒如何影响稳态密度关联函数的幂律衰减行为。

Method: 通过协调的多方向（multidirectional）跳跃机制实现质心守恒动力学，并采用静电势类比方法分析关联函数与电荷分布的关系。

Result: 当质心在所有方向守恒时，关联函数衰减更快，表现为$C({\bf x}) \sim 1/|{\bf x}|^{(d+2)}$的超均匀性（hyperuniformity）；当仅沿特定方向守恒时，则恢复较慢的$1/|{\bf x}|^{d}$衰减。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了各向异性与质心守恒在非平衡稳态中的丰富相互作用，其中$1/|{\bf x}|^{d}$衰减源于二阶四极矩电荷分布，而$1/|{\bf x}|^{(d+2)}$衰减则源于更高阶多极矩分布。

Abstract: We present exact results for steady-state density correlation functions in conserved-mass transport processes with {\it anisotropic}, reflection-symmetric hopping on a $d-$dimensional hypercubic lattice. In addition to mass conservation, we consider center-of-mass (CoM) conservation, imposed either along a specific axis or along all axes. CoM-conserving dynamics is implemented through coordinated {\it multidirectional} hopping of two equal chunks of masses in {\it opposite} directions. While anisotropy and mass conservation are known to generate power-law density correlations $C({\bf x}) \sim 1/|{\bf x}|^d$ at large distance $|{\bf x}| \gg 1$ {\it [Phys. Rev. A {\bf 42}, 1954 (1990)]}, an additional CoM conservation can qualitatively alter the nature of the power law. Indeed, when CoM is conserved in {\it all} directions, the correlations decay faster $-$ typically as $C({\bf x}) \sim 1/|{\bf x}|^{(d+2)}$, regardless of the presence (or absence) of anisotropy. Consequently, the systems exhibit an extreme {\it hyperuniformity} (``class I''), where the long-wavelength density fluctuations, despite the slow power-law decay, are anomalously suppressed. When CoM is conserved along particular ({\it not} all) directions, the slower $1/|{\bf x}|^{d}$ power-law decay is recovered. The above behavior can be understood from an analogy between the correlation function and an electrostatic potential: While a (rank-$2$) quadrupolar charge distribution gives rise to the $1/|{\bf x}|^{d}$ power law, the $1/|{\bf x}|^{(d+2)}$ power law originates from a higher-order (rank-$4$) multipolar charge distribution. These findings reveal a rich interplay between anisotropy and CoM conservation in nonequilibrium steady states.

</details>

### [102] [Enantiopurity-Controlled Magnetism in a Two-Dimensional Organic-Inorganic Material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01317)
*P. Garrett Hegel,Oscar Gonzalez,Mingrui Li,Shannon S. Fender,Harishankar Jayakumar,Archana Raja,Ariana Ray,Isaac M. Craig,D. Kwabena Bediako*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究报道了通过手性有机分子阳离子交换制备具有可控对映体过量（ee）的二维插层化合物，发现材料的磁性由插层剂ee而非绝对手性决定，低ee材料表现出对映纯类似物所没有的热激活动态磁性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结合未配对电子自旋和结构手性的扩展固体可承载非常规磁性行为，但现有研究主要关注绝对手性，对对映体过量（enantiomeric excess, ee）作为调控参数的研究不足。该工作旨在探索ee如何影响手性有机-无机杂化材料的磁性。

Method: 通过MnPS₃与手性有机分子的阳离子交换（cation exchange）制备具有可控对映体过量（ee）的二维（2D）插层化合物（intercalation compounds）。研究分析了这些材料的磁性行为与ee的关系。

Result: 材料的磁性由插层剂的对映体过量（ee）而非绝对手性决定；低ee材料表现出对映纯类似物所没有的热激活动态磁性（thermally activated dynamic magnetism）。这些ee依赖的磁性行为可通过Mn空位的局域有序化解释，该有序化由相关的空位-插层剂静电作用和受限分子堆积所引导。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了一种独特的分子-材料杂化调控策略，并建立了二维手性和磁性动态材料的设计原则，为利用对映体过量（ee）作为调控参数开发新型功能材料提供了新途径。

Abstract: Extended solids that combine unpaired electron spin and structural chirality can host unconventional magnetic behaviors with potential for electronic technologies. A versatile strategy for creating chiral solids is incorporation of chiral organic molecules into inorganic crystals. However, such hybrid organic-inorganic materials have so far been examined through the lens of absolute chirality, leaving enantiomeric excess (ee) underexplored as a tuning parameter. Here, we report two-dimensional (2D) intercalation compounds with controllable ee produced by cation exchange of MnPS$_3$ with chiral organic molecules. We show that these materials' magnetism is determined by intercalant ee rather than absolute chirality. Moreover, low-ee materials display thermally activated dynamic magnetism absent from enantiopure analogs. These ee-dependent magnetic behaviors are explained by local ordering of Mn vacancies, directed by correlated vacancy-intercalant electrostatics and confined molecular packing. Together, these results demonstrate a distinctive tuning strategy for molecule-material hybrids and establish design principles for 2D chiral and magnetically dynamic materials.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统光学或光致发光强度成像难以检测单层过渡金属二硫化物（TMDs）中激子特征的细微变化。高光谱光致发光（HSPL）成像能够提供空间分辨的光谱信息，从而揭示材料中应变和微观无序的空间分布。

Method: 研究采用高光谱光致发光（hyperspectral photoluminescence, HSPL）成像技术，对六方氮化硼（hBN）封装的MoSe₂和WSe₂样品进行空间映射。通过定量提取激子（exciton）、三子（trion）和双激子（biexciton）的能量和线宽，分析应变梯度和局部变形。

Result: HSPL成像成功揭示了hBN封装TMDs样品中的应变梯度和局部变形（如褶皱和波纹）。该技术能够表征具有均匀光学特性的区域，并识别受微观尺度无序影响的区域，这些区域可能被光学显微镜遗漏。

Conclusion: 通过对不同器件结构和制备工艺样品的测量，证明了高光谱光致发光成像在评估二维材料空间异质性和光电质量方面的通用性。该技术为二维材料微观缺陷和应变分布的检测提供了有效手段。

Abstract: Hyperspectral photoluminescence (HSPL) imaging provides spatially resolved spectral information for monolayer transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs), enabling the detection of subtle variations in excitonic features that are not accessible with conventional optical or photoluminescence intensity imaging. We employ HSPL to map the microscopic spatial distribution of strain and disorder in hBN-encapsulated MoSe$_2$ and WSe$_2$ samples. Quantitative extraction of exciton, trion, and biexciton energies and linewidths reveals strain gradients and localized deformations, such as wrinkles and ripples. The technique allows for characterization of regions with uniform optical properties and identification of areas affected by micro-scale disorder, which may be missed by optical microscopy. Measurements on samples with different device architectures and fabrication processes demonstrate the general utility of hyperspectral PL imaging for assessing spatial heterogeneity and optoelectronic quality in two-dimensional materials.

### [104] [Insulator-to-Metal Transitions Driven by Quantized Formal Polarization Mismatch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01530)
*Hongsheng Pang,Lixin He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种由量子化形式极化（QFP）不匹配驱动的绝缘体-金属（IM）相变机制，这是一种受对称性保护的体态不变量。当低对称性绝缘相与高对称性相具有不同的QFP时，任何保持低对称性相对称性的连续演化路径都必须经历IM相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在探索对称性驱动的绝缘体-金属（insulator-to-metal, IM）相变的新机制。传统相变理论主要关注序参量和对称性破缺，而本研究关注量子化形式极化（quantized formal polarization, QFP）这一对称性保护的体态不变量在相变中的作用。

Method: 研究基于对称性约束的拓扑分析，提出QFP不匹配导致IM相变的机制。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证该机制，选取了二维InPS₃和三维CdBiO₃两个代表性体系进行具体计算分析。

Result: 计算结果表明，在保持低对称性相对称性的连续演化路径上，QFP保持不变；而高对称性相需要不同的QFP，这只能通过能隙闭合（gap closing）实现。两个代表性体系的计算结果均证实了QFP不匹配驱动IM相变的机制。

Conclusion: 研究确立了QFP不匹配作为相演化的一般对称性约束，揭示了高对称性材料中对称性驱动IM相变的新途径。该机制为理解材料相变提供了新的理论框架，将对称性保护的拓扑不变量与电子结构演化联系起来。

Abstract: We propose a mechanism for insulator-to-metal (IM) transitions driven by the mismatch of quantized formal polarization (QFP), a symmetry-protected bulk invariant. For a material with a low-symmetry insulating phase and a high-symmetry phase that allow distinct QFPs, any continuous path connecting them while preserving the symmetry of the low-symmetry phase must inevitably pass through an IM transition. The reason is that QFP remains invariant along any gapped symmetry-preserving evolution, whereas the high-symmetry phase requires a different QFP, which can only be accommodated by gap closing. First-principles calculations on two representative systems, two-dimensional InPS$_3$ and three-dimensional CdBiO$_3$, confirm this mechanism. Our results establish QFP mismatch as a general symmetry constraint on phase evolution and reveal a new route to symmetry-driven IM transitions in high-symmetry materials.

</details>


### [105] [Precipitate-Induced Dynamic Strain Aging and Its Effect on the Strain Rate Sensitivity of Precipitation Hardened Aluminum Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01537)
*Sahar Choukir,Derek Warner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过多尺度模拟方法揭示了沉淀强化Al-Cu合金中低应变率敏感性（low strain-rate sensitivity）的微观机制，发现位错-沉淀物界面处的Cu-Al原子交换动力学是导致这一现象的关键原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究沉淀强化铝合金中低应变率敏感性（low strain-rate sensitivity）的微观机制起源，该现象在实验中被广泛观察到但缺乏明确的机理解释。

Method: 采用多尺度模拟方法：原子尺度模拟（atomistic simulations）表征位错-沉淀物界面处的Cu-Al原子交换能量学；动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟位错钉扎过程中障碍强度的演化；解析速率理论（analytical rate theory）预测应变率敏感性参数。

Result: 模型预测在广泛的准静态应变率范围内存在低应变率敏感性，与沉淀强化合金的实验观测一致。研究识别出位错-沉淀物相互作用动力学，特别是最近邻Cu-Al原子交换，是低应变率敏感性的微观机制起源。

Conclusion: 沉淀强化铝合金的低应变率敏感性直接源于位错-沉淀物相互作用动力学，当考虑最近邻Cu-Al原子交换时，这一微观机制能够解释实验观察到的宏观力学行为。

Abstract: We examine precipitate-induced dynamic strain aging in precipitation-hardened Al-Cu alloys by combining atomistic simulations, kinetic Monte Carlo, and analytical rate theory. Atomistic simulations were used to characterize (1) the energetics of nearest neighbour Cu<->Al exchanges at dislocation - precipitate junctions and (2) the subsequent change in obstacle strength. For robustness, the simulations were performed with two distinct interatomic potentials. The resulting catalog of local Cu-Al exchange events was used as input for a kinetic Monte Carlo model of the time-dependent evolution of obstacle strength during dislocation pinning at the precipitate. The predicted strengthening kinetics were then embedded in an analytical dynamic strain aging model to predict the strain-rate sensitivity parameter. On the whole, the modeling predicts a low strain-rate sensitivity across a broad range of intermediate quasi-static strain rates, consistent with experimental observations for precipitate-strengthened alloys. The results therefore identify a mechanistic origin of the low strain-rate sensitivity in precipitation hardened aluminum alloys, emerging directly from the kinetics of dislocation-precipitate interactions when nearest neighbour Cu<->Al exchanges are considered.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文主要采用综述性方法，描述了多铁性材料的基本特性及其应用潜力。同时介绍了磁电复合材料（magnetoelectric composites）的合成方法，即通过组合独立的磁性和电性材料来实现独特的磁电耦合功能。

Abstract: A material that reveals two or more ferroelectric properties at the same time is called multiferroic materials. The most commonly multiferroic materials shows ferroelectricity and ferromagnetism property within a single phase. Accordingly such materials can possess both spontaneous magnetization and electric polarization and which can be individually controlled through external electric or magnetic fields. The unique coexistence of ferroelectric properties opens up possibilities for innovative applications, including memory devices, sensors, and actuators that are responsive to both electrical and magneticstimuli. Multiferroics gives a valuable foundation for generating cutting edge multifunctional devices, exhibiting their versatility across broad area technological fields. Applications include sensors, transducers, spintronics, terahertz emitters, miniature antennas, energy harvesting, multiple state memory storage, electric field controlled ferromagnetic resonance devices, and nanoscale electronics. Researchers are continually work to discovering new materials exploring the fundamental mechanisms involved, and optimizing their performance for various application. Multiferroic materials has a promising area for innovation and exploration the field of advance technologies this type of materials contributing not only to device development but also enhancing the understanding of the interactions between ferroelectric and magnetic orders. Additionally, magnetoelectric composites is a type of multifunctional material showing strong coupling between magnetic and electric properties for further technological applications. Magnetoelectric (ME) composites are synthesis by combining separate magnetic and electric materials to produce unique functionalities through their interactions. This coupling enables the control of magnetic properties by an electric field and vice versa.

### [107] [Abrupt crystallization from shock-compressed CaSiO3 glass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01566)
*A. Amouretti,K. Nonaka,X. Liu,Y. Hironaka,H. Huang,R. Kodama,K. Lawler,K. Miyanishi,H. Nakamura,C. Schwartz,Y. Seto,K. Sueda,Y. Wu,M. Yabashi,T. Yabuuchi,N. Ozaki*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用原位时间分辨X射线衍射（in situ time-resolved X-ray diffraction）技术，在约100 GPa高压下对激光冲击（laser-shocked）的CaSiO3玻璃进行实时观测。

Result: 观察到CaSiO3钙钛矿结构从压缩非晶相的快速结晶，典型成核时间（nucleation time）为1.69±0.10 ns，最终晶粒尺寸约20 nm；晶粒尺寸时间演化表明转变受扩散控制，爆炸性晶粒生长与释放波到达同时发生。

Conclusion: 在极端高压条件下，CaSiO3玻璃向钙钛矿结构的结晶过程具有超快动力学特征，且释放波（release wave）在成核过程中可能发挥重要作用，转变机制受扩散控制。

Abstract: We have performed in situ time-resolved X-ray diffraction at ~100 GPa on laser-shocked CaSiO3 glass to investigate the glass-to-crystal transition. At this extreme pressure, we observe the ultrafast crystallization of the CaSiO3 perovskite structure from the compressed amorphous phase, with a typical nucleation time of 1.69 +/- 0.10 ns and a final grainsize of ~20 nm. The grain size temporal evolution suggest a diffusion controlled transformation. Moreover, the observed concomitant explosive grain growth together with the release wave arrival into shocked CaSiO3 also suggests a role of the release in the nucleation process.

### [108] [Machine Learning Interatomic Potentials for Million-Atom Simulations of Multicomponent Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01642)
*Fei Shuang,Penghua Ying,Kai Liu,Zixiong Wei,Fengxian Liu,Zheyong Fan,Minqiang Jiang,Poulumi Dey*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究比较了两种先进的机器学习原子间势（MLIP）框架——神经进化势（NEP）和图原子团簇展开（GRACE），在16种元素金属和多组分合金中的表现。GRACE在训练效率和准确性方面略优，而NEP在推理速度上具有约60倍优势，适合大规模分子动力学模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有广泛化学灵活性的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials, MLIPs）对于高熵合金等成分复杂材料的原子尺度模拟至关重要。研究旨在评估两种先进MLIP框架在金属和合金系统中的性能差异。

Method: 研究比较了神经进化势（neuroevolution potential, NEP）和图原子团簇展开（graph atomic cluster expansion, GRACE）两种框架。GRACE采用Finnis-Sinclair类型，研究评估了它们在16种元素金属和多组分合金中的训练效率、准确性及不确定性量化策略。

Result: GRACE势表现出显著更高的训练效率，在力学性能、热稳定性和化学外推方面具有略微更好的准确性。相比之下，NEP实现了约60倍更高的推理速度，适合百万原子分子动力学模拟。基于集成的不确定性量化与模型误差稳健相关，而D-最优性在研究的系统中可靠性较低。

Conclusion: 结合基于集成的不确定性量化，NEP能够在极端动态条件下实现高效可靠的模拟。研究为不同模拟需求下的MLIP选择提供了指导：GRACE适合准确性优先的任务，而NEP更适合大规模动力学模拟。

Abstract: Machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) with broad chemical flexibility are important for atomistic simulations of compositionally complex materials such as high-entropy alloys. Here, we study two state-of-the-art MLIP frameworks, the neuroevolution potential (NEP) and the graph atomic cluster expansion (GRACE), for 16 elemental metals and multicomponent alloys. GRACE potential with Finnis-Sinclair type shows substantially higher training efficiency and consistently, though only slightly, better accuracy for mechanical properties, thermal stability, and chemical extrapolation. In contrast, NEP achieves an approximately 60-fold higher inference speed, making it attractive for million-atom molecular dynamics simulations. We further examine uncertainty quantification strategies and find that ensemble-based uncertainty correlates robustly with model error, whereas D-optimality is less reliable for the systems considered here. Large-scale nonequilibrium molecular dynamics simulations of shock propagation further show that NEP, combined with ensemble-based uncertainty quantification, enables efficient and reliable simulations under extreme dynamic conditions.

</details>


### [109] [Quantum-Information Measure of Electron Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01688)
*Stefano Pittalis,Filippo Troiani,Celestino Angeli,Irene D'Amico,Tim Gould*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于量子信息理论中相关双自旋混合态并发度（concurrence）的全非经验性电子局域化度量方法，取代了传统电子局域化函数（ELF）中的经验性成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解分子和材料中的电子局域化在电子结构理论中至关重要，随着数据驱动方法的兴起其重要性将进一步提升。虽然电子局域化函数（ELF）被广泛用于可视化电子组织，但其公式仍保留高度经验性成分。

Method: 引入了一种完全非经验性的电子局域化度量方法，该方法源自相关双自旋混合态（correlated two spin mixed state）的并发度（concurrence）。这一构造产生了一个基于量子信息理论的真实两点局域化指标。

Result: 该方法能够准确捕捉原子壳层、共价键和离子键、孤对电子、分子解离以及电荷转移过程。该方法在数值计算上易于评估。

Conclusion: 新方法消除了电子局域化函数（ELF）中的临时性步骤，提供了一个基于量子信息理论原理的电子局域化度量框架。

Abstract: Understanding electron localization in molecules and materials plays a central role in electronic structure theory, and will increase in importance with the rise of data driven approaches. The electron localization function (ELF) is widely used to visualize electron organization in molecules and materials, and it remains a central ingredient in modern density functional approximations. Yet its formulation retains highly empirical elements. Here we introduce a fully non empirical measure of electron localization derived from the concurrence of a correlated two spin mixed state. This construction yields a genuine two point localization indicator grounded in quantum information theory, removing the ad hoc steps underlying the ELF. We show that atomic shells, covalent and ionic bonds, lone pairs, molecular dissociation, and charge transfer processes are captured. The method is straightforward to evaluate numerically.

</details>

Abstract: The p-type surface conductivity of H-terminated diamond (HD, H-diamond) has created new path ways for developing diamond based electronic devices as well as chemical and bio-sensors. Herein, we report the study on polymer electrolyte-gated field effect transistors (EGFETs) fabricated using pristine and partially O-terminated HD films. The HD surface is transformed from hydrophobic to moderate hydrophilic by partial O-termination. Also, the sheet resistance of the HD surface increases from 7.6 to 18.7 k-Ohms per sq. while the sheet hole density decreases from 10.5 to 4.8 x 10^12 cm^-2 upon partial O-termination. Consequently, the ON - OFF ratio of the EGFET devices decreases from ~ 40 to 14 and the maximum transconductance declines from of -150 to -7.9 micro-seimens per V, but the areal capacitance increases from ~ 7.8 to 27.1 microFarad per cm^2 with partial ozonation on HD surface. This work highlights the significant impact of the partial O-termination on the performance of the HD EGFET devices and effect of electrochemical gating on the phonon behaviour of the H-diamond.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用远场叠层衍射成像技术（tele-ptychography）在衍射方向对完美晶体中产生的多束X射线进行成像，分辨率约为100纳米，基于动力学衍射理论（dynamical diffraction theory）描述这些多波场。

Result: 在成像的衍射峰中观察到10个回波极大值，总信号长度为78微米，对应小于108飞秒的总时间延迟；这些回波由衍射X射线在晶体样品出射表面的相长干涉产生。

Conclusion: X射线衍射回波对X射线自由电子激光源的光学应用至关重要，该效应可用于未来超快X射线分束器；此外，回波还可用于追踪单晶微结构中的超快过程，如熔融或应变传播。

Abstract: Multiple x-ray beams generated by interference processes in perfect crystals were imaged with a resolution of about 100nm using tele-ptychography in the diffraction direction. These multiple wave-fields, also known as x-ray diffraction echoes, are related to the process known as the Pendelloesung effect and are described by dynamical diffraction theory. The echoes are produced by the constructive interference of diffracted x-rays at the exit surface of the crystal sample. In the imaged diffraction peak, we observed 10 echoes maxima with a total signal length of 78 um. Which translates into a total temporal delay in the signal of less than 108 fs.This makes the echoes of high importance for x-ray optics at x-ray Free Electron Laser sources, as the effect could be used for future ultrafast x-ray beam splitters. In addition to this application, echoes can be exploited to follow ultrafast processes in single crystal micro-structures such as melting or strain propagation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用含可控随机分布激光切割孔的PMMA试样进行拉伸试验，结合数字图像相关技术（digital image correlation）测量变形。通过显微镜观察孔隙几何形态和合并情况，并采用威布尔模型（Weibull model）分析断裂应力分布。

Result: 杨氏模量随孔隙率近线性下降，但下降速率远超经典有效介质理论和Hashin-Shtrikman界限。外推临界孔隙率远低于二维渗流阈值，表明理想圆柱孔模型无法描述观测行为。孔隙不规则形态和频繁合并使其类似裂纹缺陷，显著增强柔度。断裂应力分布可用考虑承载面积减少和孔边应力集中的威布尔模型良好描述。

Conclusion: 孔隙形态缺陷在控制多孔准脆性材料的刚度退化和断裂统计中起主导作用。不规则孔隙几何和合并效应使其类似裂纹缺陷，导致材料柔度显著增强，这超出了传统有效介质理论的预测范围。

Abstract: We study the mechanical response of quasi-brittle polymethyl methacrylate (PMMA) specimens containing controlled random distributions of laser-cut holes. Tensile tests combined with digital image correlation reveal a nearly linear decrease of the Young's modulus with porosity, but with a softening rate far exceeding classical effective medium theory and the Hashin-Shtrikman bound. The extrapolated critical porosity at which the modulus vanishes is well below the 2D percolation threshold, indicating that ideal cylindrical void models fail to capture the observed behavior. Microscopy shows irregular pore geometries and frequent coalescence, which effectively act as crack-like defects and strongly enhance compliance. The rupture stress distributions are well described by a Weibull model accounting for both load-bearing area reduction and stress concentration at hole edges. Digital image correlation reveals heterogeneous but non-localized deformation, with strain increasingly correlated with the hole pattern, indicating a growing influence of defect-induced stress concentrations. These results highlight the dominant role of defect morphology in governing stiffness degradation and fracture statistics in porous quasi-brittle materials.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（AFM）和铁磁（FM）斯格明子各具优势：AFM斯格明子消除了斯格明子霍尔效应（skyrmion Hall effect）且动力学更快，而FM斯格明子更易成核和操控。然而，在同一二维（2D）材料中实现AFM和FM斯格明子之间的相变仍具挑战。

Method: 研究采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和原子自旋模拟（atomistic spin simulations）对Janus单层Cr2Ge2Te3S3进行分析，通过应变驱动调控磁相互作用来实现相变切换。

Conclusion: 这些发现为在单一二维材料中实现拓扑磁态的可控相变建立了理论框架，为自旋电子学（spintronic）应用提供了新的材料平台。

Abstract: Antiferromagnetic (AFM) and ferromagnetic (FM) skyrmions possess unique advantages for spintronic applications. AFM skyrmions eliminate the skyrmion Hall effect and exhibit fast dynamics, whereas FM skyrmions are easier to nucleate and manipulate. However, realizing a transition between AFM and FM skyrmions within the same two-dimensional (2D) material has remained elusive. Here, using first-principles calculations and atomistic spin simulations on the Janus monolayer Cr2Ge2Te3S3, we demonstrate that strain-driven modulation of magnetic interactions enables switching between AFM and FM skyrmion phases. A compressive strain of $-3\%$ induces an AFM ground state hosting AFM skyrmions, while a tensile strain of $+2\%$ drives the system into a FM skyrmion phase. Moreover, under an out-of-plane magnetic field, FM skyrmions are rapidly transformed into a uniform FM phase, while AFM skyrmions transform into AFM bimerons under stronger fields. These findings establish a framework for controllable transitions between topological magnetic states in a single 2D material.

### [114] [Atomistic theory of the phonon angular momentum Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01899)
*Daniel A. Bustamante Lopez,Verena Brehm,Dominik M. Juraschek*

TL;DR: 该研究发展了一种原子尺度理论，用于解释声子角动量霍尔效应（phonon angular momentum Hall effect）——一种由热梯度驱动的纵向热流转化为横向声子角动量流的晶格振动现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立自旋和轨道霍尔效应的晶格振动类比理论。自旋和轨道霍尔效应将纵向电荷电流转化为电子角动量的横向流动，而本研究关注其声子对应物，即热梯度驱动的纵向热流如何转化为声子角动量的横向流动。

Method: 研究发展了一种原子尺度的实空间理论，推导了声子角动量流的微观表达式。通过最小化的方晶格和蜂窝晶格模型进行演示，并基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对多种示例材料计算了相应的声子角动量积累。

Result: 研究表明该效应源于热诱导的极化振动模式混合，导致声子角动量在边缘的特征性积累。计算结果证实声子角动量霍尔效应是晶体固体的普遍响应，且该理论框架可普遍应用于所有材料。

Conclusion: 声子角动量霍尔效应是晶体固体中普遍存在的物理响应现象。所发展的原子尺度理论框架具有通用性，适用于所有材料体系，为理解热流与角动量输运的耦合提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The spin and orbital Hall effects convert longitudinal charge currents into transverse flows of electronic angular momentum. Here we develop an atomistic theory of the recently proposed lattice-vibrational analogue, in which a longitudinal heat current driven by a thermal gradient is converted into a transverse current of phonon angular momentum. We derive a microscopic real-space expression for this current and show that it originates from thermally induced mixing of polarized vibrational motion, leading to a characteristic edge accumulation of phonon angular momentum. We demonstrate the effect in minimal square- and honeycomb-lattice models and compute the resulting phonon angular momentum accumulations for a range of example materials using input from first-principles calculations. Our results confirm that the phonon angular momentum Hall effect is a universal response of crystalline solids and our framework is generically applicable to all materials.

### [115] [Phonon Thermal Hall Effect in quartz and its absence in silica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01908)
*Yu Ling,Benoît Fauqué,Kamran Behnia*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比晶体和玻璃态SiO₂的热输运实验，发现声子热霍尔效应（phonon thermal Hall effect）仅存在于晶体样品中，且更纯净的晶体表现出更大的热霍尔电导率，排除了无序性作为效应驱动因素的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝缘固体中施加热流与测量温度梯度在磁场下的不对齐现象已成为实验研究和理论争议的焦点。为识别声子热霍尔效应的起源，需要对晶体和玻璃态材料进行对比研究。

Method: 采用相同的实验装置和温度计，对晶体（石英）和玻璃态（二氧化硅）SiO₂进行纵向和横向热输运的对比研究，比较不同纯度晶体的热霍尔响应。

Result: 在晶体样品中检测到有限信号，而在非晶样品中未检测到；更纯净的晶体表现出更大的热霍尔电导率，但两个晶体样品的横向热电阻率幅度几乎相同（W⊥/B≈10⁻⁶ m·K·W⁻¹·T⁻¹）。

Conclusion: 声子热霍尔效应源于两个热传导通道在熵产生和磁场耦合方面的差异，导致守恒的能量流和非守恒的熵流不再平行；横向热电阻率的大小可通过晶格核的微小漂移速度、磁场施加的横向贝里力（Berry force）与熵恢复力平衡的简单图像来解释。

Abstract: The observation of a misalignment between the applied heat flux and the measured temperature gradient in insulating solids induced by magnetic field has become a subject of experimental investigation, theoretical speculation, and unsettled controversy. To identify the origin of this phonon thermal Hall effect, we performed a comparative study of longitudinal and transverse heat transport in crystalline (quartz) and vitreous (silica) SiO$_2$ using identical experimental set-ups and thermometers. A finite signal was detected in the crystalline samples and none in the amorphous sample, within our resolution. The cleaner crystal exhibited a larger thermal Hall conductivity than the dirtier one, ruling out disorder as the driver of the effect. On the other hand, the amplitude of the transverse thermal resistivity is almost identical in the two crystalline samples (W$_{\perp}$/B$\approx 10^{-6}$ m.K.W$^{-1}$.T$^{-1}$). We show that in a phonon gas, as in a molecular gas displaying the Senftleben-Beenakker effect, heat is conducted through two channels, and argue that a thermal Hall response is unavoidable whenever these channels differ both in entropy production and in their coupling to the magnetic field. Under such conditions, the conserved energy current and the non-conserved entropy current cease to be parallel. Finally, the magnitude of the transverse thermal resistivity can be accounted for by a surprisingly simple picture. The heat flux induces a tiny drift velocity of the lattice nuclei, the magnetic field exerts a transverse Berry force on this drift, and this force is balanced by an entropic restoring force.

</details>

Abstract: Antiperovskite derivatives have recently emerged as promising lead-free alternatives to halide perovskites for optoelectronic applications. Here, using a comprehensive first-principles calculations including density functional perturbation theory and many-body perturbation theory (involving GW and Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE)), we investigate the stability, excitonic, polaronic, and optoelectronic properties of cubic Ba$_3$MA$_3$ (M = P, As, Sb, Bi; A = Cl, Br, I). The resulting spectroscopic limited maximum efficiencies reach $\sim$ 19-32%, surpassing several lead-based perovskites. Our results establish Ba-based antiperovskite derivatives as a robust, eco-friendly platform for next-generation optoelectronic devices.

### [117] [Altermagnetism and Room-Temperature Metal-to-Insulator Transition in CsCr$_2$S$_2$O](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02114)
*Yi Liu,Chen-Chao Xu,Jin-Ke Bao,Bai-Jiang Lv,Hao Li,Jing Li,Yi-Qiang Lin,Hua-Xun Li,Yi-Ming Lu,Xin-Yu Zhao,Wu-Zhang Yang,Zhen-Yi Zhang,Xian-Yan Chen,Wen-he Jiao,Ji-Yong Liu,Bai-Ren Zhu,Guang-Han Cao*

Motivation: 金属-绝缘体转变（MIT）在非磁性和传统铁磁/反铁磁系统中已有广泛研究，但MIT与交变磁性（altermagnetism）的共存现象尚未被探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，探索这两种重要物理现象在单一材料中的共同出现。

Method: 合成了层状铬基化合物CsCr₂S₂O，该材料在CeCr₂Si₂C型结构中结晶。通过实验测量发现Cr磁矩在TN = 326 K以下呈现C型反铁磁构型。结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）分析了自旋分裂电子结构。

Result: CsCr₂S₂O在326 K以下形成室温d波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet），随后在305 K发生Verwey型金属-绝缘体转变（MIT）。该转变由四方到正交的结构畸变和Cr²⁺/Cr³⁺离子的条纹电荷有序驱动，同时保持交变磁性特征。计算显示金属态和绝缘态的最大自旋分裂能量分别为~0.6 eV和~0.3 eV。

Conclusion: 该工作首次将金属-绝缘体转变（MIT）和交变磁性（altermagnetism）这两种重要现象关联在单一材料中，建立了一个潜在的自旋电子学（spintronic）应用新平台。

Abstract: Metal-to-insulator transitions (MITs), particularly near room temperature, have been extensively studied in nonmagnetic and conventional ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic systems, yet the co-emergence of MIT and altermagnetism (AM) remains unexplored. Here, a layered chromium-based compound CsCr$_2$S$_2$O that realizes this coexistence was synthesized. It crystalizes in CeCr$_2$Si$_2$C-type structure with Cr moments orders in a C-type antiferromagnetic configuration below $T_\mathrm{N}$ = 326 K, constituting a room-temperature d-wave altermagnet. In the altermagnetic state, a subsequent Verwey-type MIT appears at $T_\mathrm{MI}$ = 305 K, driven by a tetragonal-to-orthorhombic structural distortion and stripe charge ordering of Cr$^{+2}$/Cr$^{+3}$ ions, while maintaining its altermagnetic character. First-principles calculations show moment-dependent spin-split electronic structures with maximum splitting energies of ~0.6 eV and ~0.3 eV in the metallic and insulating states, respectively. Our work links the two prominent phenomena, MIT and AM, in a single material, establishing a new platform for potential spintronic applications.

</details>


### [118] [Terahertz optical activity near crystal field transitions of Tm3+ ions in magnetoelectric alumoborates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02193)
*A. M. Kuzmenko,V. Yu. Ivanov,S. V. Garnov,A. Shuvaev,A. Pimenov,K. N. Boldyrev,I. A. Gudim,A. A. Mukhin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究Tm³⁺离子在磁电材料TmAl₃(BO₃)₄及其掺杂体系中的晶体场（crystal field）激发特性，特别是D₃对称性下的精细结构和光学活性现象。

Method: 采用太赫兹（terahertz）透射光谱技术，分析纯TmAl₃(BO₃)₄和掺杂Tm₀.₀₅Yb₀.₁Y₀.₈₅Al₃(BO₃)₄样品，在低温下解析晶体场激发的精细结构。

Result: 晶体场激发主要被识别为从基态单重态A₁到激发双重态E的磁偶极跃迁（magnetic dipole transitions），在轻掺杂和纯Tm硼酸盐中表现出不同的精细结构，反映了局部晶体场的不同畸变。在晶体场跃迁附近观测到高达25度的强自然光学活性（natural optical activity）。

Conclusion: 光学活性可通过磁偶极和电偶极跃迁对动态磁电极化率（dynamic magnetoelectric susceptibility）的贡献进行定量描述，并考虑局部畸变的分类，为理解磁电材料中的晶体场效应提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Crystal field (CF) excitations in the ground multiplet $^3H_6$ of Tm$^{3+}$ ions were investigated using terahertz transmission spectra of magnetoelectric TmAl$_3$(BO$_3$)$_4$ and Tm$_{0.05}$Yb$_{0.1}$Y$_{0.85}$Al$_3$(BO$_3$)$_4$. These excitations were identified as mainly magnetic dipole transitions from the ground singlet A$_1$ to the next excited doublet E, split by the crystal field of the D$_3$ symmetry. The fine structure of the modes was resolved at low temperatures. It manifested differently in lightly doped and in pure Tm borates, consistent with different distortions of the local crystal field with the D$_3$ symmetry. Strong natural optical activity was observed near the CF transitions resulting in a polarization plane rotation up to 25 degrees. The optical activity is quantitatively described by contributions of magnetic and electric dipole transitions to dynamic magnetoelectric susceptibility and taking into account the classification of local distortions.

### [119] [AlloyVAE: A generative model for complex probabilistic field-to-field relationships in alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02281)
*Ningyu Yan,Zhuocheng Xie,Kai Guo,Yejun Gu,Huajian Gao,Yang Xiang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: AlloyVAE是一个物理信息生成框架，用于学习多主元合金（MPEAs）中机械场的完整条件分布，解决传统确定性方法无法处理的结构-性能多对一映射问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多主元合金（multi-principal element alloys, MPEAs）固有的成分异质性导致复杂的空间变化机械场，这些场无法从粗粒度成分描述符唯一确定。这种非唯一性引入了本质上的概率性结构-性能关系，对传统确定性建模和机器学习方法构成了根本性挑战。

Method: AlloyVAE基于条件变分自编码器（conditional variational autoencoder）架构，包含学习平滑算子以增强函数规律性，以及自洽机制以确保物理合理性。模型在原子尺度模拟数据上进行训练。

Result: AlloyVAE能够准确预测基于成分和短程有序（short-range order）的残余应力场分布，并在相同输入条件下生成多个物理一致的真实化结果。该框架还支持通过优化成分场实现目标机械响应的逆向设计（inverse design）。

Conclusion: 通过捕捉异质材料中的一对多结构-性能关系，这项工作建立了材料建模和设计的概率范式，为探索高维成分空间提供了可扩展的替代传统模拟方法。

Abstract: The inherent compositional heterogeneity of multi-principal element alloys (MPEAs) gives rise to complex, spatially varying mechanical fields that cannot be uniquely determined from coarse-grained composition descriptors. This non-uniqueness introduces intrinsically probabilistic structure-property relationships, posing a fundamental challenge to conventional deterministic modeling and machine learning approaches that collapse such mappings into average predictions. Here, we present AlloyVAE, a physics-informed generative framework that learns the full conditional distribution of mechanical fields from microstructural inputs. Built upon a conditional variational autoencoder architecture, the model incorporates learned smoothing operators to enhance functional regularity and a self-consistency mechanism to enforce physical plausibility. Trained on atomistic simulation data, AlloyVAE accurately predicts distributions of residual stress fields from composition and short-range order, and enables the generation of multiple physically consistent realizations under identical input conditions. Beyond forward prediction, the framework supports inverse design by optimizing composition fields to achieve targeted mechanical responses, and is extensible to coupled mappings involving eigenstrain. By capturing one-to-many structure-property relationships in heterogeneous materials, this work establishes a probabilistic paradigm for materials modeling and design, providing a scalable alternative to conventional simulations for navigating high-dimensional compositional spaces.

</details>


### [120] [Loop-level surrogate modeling of dopant-distribution effects in Ba(Zr,Ti)O$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02325)
*Heiko Röthl,Elke Kraker,Julien Magnien,Manfred Mücke,Florian Mayer*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锆掺杂钛酸钡（BZT）是重要的无铅介电和机电技术候选材料，但现有研究通常仅关注平均掺杂浓度，而掺杂剂空间分布对功能行为的影响尚未被充分理解且难以系统探索。

Method: 研究提出加速材料设计工作流：首先生成涵盖纳米尺度排列连续谱的锆分布（包括层状、棒状、点状和片层状等代表性端元图案），使用紧凑参数化描述符模型编码每个配置；采用有效哈密顿量分子动力学计算极化-电场和应变-场磁滞回线；训练条件自编码器替代模型直接从分布参数预测完整回线。

Result: 替代模型实现了大规模快速筛选和密集属性选择性设计图，支持在感兴趣区域进行针对性后续模拟；通过预测回线数据库筛选分布空间，识别了不同功能目标（储能性能、机电响应、开关行为）对应的掺杂剂分布图案家族；设计图显示掺杂剂分布是独立调控参数，能显著影响磁滞行为和回线衍生品质因数。

Conclusion: 掺杂剂空间分布是影响铁电性能的独立调控参数，层状图案、垂直片层和纳米板状夹杂物在不同性能区间出现；预测完整响应曲线的方法支持其他回线衍生目标的筛选和替代铁电材料中的多目标设计。

Abstract: Barium titanate-based perovskites are important candidates for lead-free dielectric and electromechanical technologies. In Zr-substituted BaTiO$_3$ (BZT), functional behavior is usually discussed in terms of the average Zr concentration, while the influence of dopant spatial distribution beyond average concentration is less understood and difficult to explore systematically. Here we present an accelerated materials-design workflow that links controlled dopant distributions to full field-driven response curves. We generate a broad set of Zr distributions spanning a continuum of nanoscale arrangements, with layers, rods, dots, and lamellae serving as representative end-member motifs, and encode each configuration using a compact, parametrized descriptor model. Effective-Hamiltonian molecular dynamics is used to compute polarization-electric-field and strain-field hysteresis loops, and we train a conditional autoencoder surrogate to predict complete loops directly from the distribution parameters. This surrogate enables rapid screening and dense, property-selective design maps at scales that are not feasible with direct simulations alone, and it supports targeted follow-up simulations in regions of interest. Using the predicted loop database, we screen the distribution space for multiple functional targets, including energy-storage performance, electromechanical response, and switching behavior, and identify the corresponding dopant distribution motif families. The resulting design maps show that dopant distribution is an independent tuning parameter that can strongly affect hysteresis behavior and loop-derived figures of merit: layer-like motifs, vertical lamellae, and nanoplate-like inclusions emerge in different performance regimes. More generally, predicting full response curves enables screening of other loop-derived targets and multi-objective design in substituted ferroelectrics.

### [121] [Numerically Optimizing Shortcuts to Adiabaticity: A Hybrid Control Strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01301)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现快速且无激发（excitation-free）的量子控制是现代量子技术中的关键挑战。虽然绝热捷径（shortcuts to adiabaticity）能够实现快速绝热协议，但在复杂系统中确定满足实际约束的控制参数通常很困难。

Method: 结合解析的绝热捷径方法与多种数值优化技术，形成混合方法以提升协议性能。以双离子分离（separation of two trapped ions）这一复杂控制问题作为原理验证。

Result: 这种解析-数值混合方法及其通过多种次优解获得的物理洞察，能够在复杂参数空间中探索新解，实现高达3个数量级的性能提升。从实验角度看，这种改进无需额外成本。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了结合解析与数值方法的混合策略在解决复杂量子控制问题中的有效性，为实际量子技术应用提供了性能显著提升且实验可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Achieving fast, excitation-free quantum control is a vital challenge in modern quantum technologies. Here, we combine an analytical shortcut to adiabaticity approach with several numerical optimization methods to boost the performance of the protocol. As a proof-of-principle for this hybrid approach, we study a particularly intricate control problem, the separation of two trapped ions. We show that this analytical-numerical approach, along with the physical insight gained through the variety of suboptimal solutions, leads to the exploration of new solutions in a complex landscape that yield improvements of up to 3 orders of magnitude. Moreover, this improvement comes with no additional cost from an experimental point of view.

### [122] [Transversal non-Clifford gates on almost-good quantum LDPC and quantum locally testable codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01874)
*Yiming Li,Zimu Li,Zi-Wen Liu*

TL;DR: 该论文展示了在具有近乎最优参数的量子低密度奇偶校验码和量子局部可测试码上实现非平凡横向逻辑多控制-Z门，首次将优良编码参数与容错非克利福德门相结合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在解决量子纠错码中同时实现优良编码参数和容错非克利福德门（non-Clifford gates）的挑战，特别是横向逻辑多控制-Z门（transversal logical multi-controlled-$Z$ gates）的构造问题。

Method: 研究开发了一个通用框架，构建了一类新的同调不变形式（homological invariant forms），称为"cupcap gates"，并基于[Li et al.]的见解，利用覆盖空间方法（covering space methods）来证明其非平凡性。

Result: 在$[\![N,Θ(N),\tildeΘ(N)]\!]$量子低密度奇偶校验码和$[\![N,Θ(N),\tildeΘ(N)]\!]$量子局部可测试码上实现了非平凡横向逻辑多控制-Z门，这些编码具有$\tildeΘ(1)$的健全性（soundness），首次将近乎最优的编码参数与容错非克利福德门相结合。

Conclusion: 该研究表明这些看似复杂的逻辑门实际上作为基本拓扑现象自然出现，证明过程几乎完全是代数拓扑的，所声称的近乎优良编码结果作为该框架的实例立即得到。

Abstract: We exhibit nontrivial transversal logical multi-controlled-$Z$ gates on $[\![N,Θ(N),\tildeΘ(N)]\!]$ quantum low-density parity-check codes and $[\![N,Θ(N),\tildeΘ(N)]\!]$ quantum locally testable codes with soundness $\tildeΘ(1)$, combining nearly optimal code parameters with fault-tolerant non-Clifford gates for the first time. Remarkably, our proofs are almost entirely algebraic-topological, showing that such presumably intricate logical gates naturally arise as a fundamental topological phenomenon. We develop a general framework for constructing a rich new family of homological invariant forms which we call ''cupcap gates'' that induce transversal logical multi-controlled-$Z$ and, building on insights from [Li et al., arXiv:2603.25831], covering space methods to certify their nontriviality. The claimed almost-good code results follow immediately as examples.

### [123] [Explicit constructions of mutually unbiased bases via Hadamard matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02234)
*Jean-Christophe Pain*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究对有限维希尔伯特空间中的相互无偏基（MUBs）进行了详细的计算与代数分析，重点探讨了维度2、3、4及具有挑战性的维度6的情况，并推广至任意素数幂维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在深入理解相互无偏基（Mutually Unbiased Bases, MUBs）在量子信息科学中的理论性质与构造方法，特别关注非素数幂维度（如维度6）中MUBs构造的困难与约束。

Method: 采用Hadamard-相位参数化方法推导维度4中相互无偏性的显式解析条件；通过Pauli算符的张量积构造研究两量子比特系统中的MUBs；在维度6中探索傅里叶族方法，并建立系统的计算框架测试候选相位向量。

Result: 在维度4中获得了完整的5个MUBs集合；在维度6中验证了已知构造最多只能得到3个MUBs；建立了连接解析洞察与数值探索的验证方法，并推广到任意素数幂维度的有限域结构、Heisenberg-Weyl算符和离散对称性分析。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了透明、逐行验证的方法论，揭示了MUBs的几何与代数丰富性，阐明了某些维度难以获得完整解析构造的原因，为量子信息科学研究人员提供了全面的理论与实用构造资源。

Abstract: We present a detailed computational and algebraic study of Mutually Unbiased Bases (MUBs) in finite-dimensional Hilbert spaces, with a particular focus on dimensions 2, 3, 4, and the challenging case of 6. Starting from the Hadamard-phase parametrization, we derive explicit analytical conditions for mutual unbiasedness in dimension 4, providing a tractable system of trigonometric constraints on the phase parameters. We then explore a tensor-product construction via Pauli operators, highlighting the algebraic and group-theoretical origin of MUBs in two-qubit systems, and demonstrating how these constructions yield a complete set of 5 MUBs in dimension 4. Extending our approach, we investigate the Fourier-family method in dimension 6, where the absence of a prime-power structure imposes strong rigidity constraints and limits the known constructions to sets of 3 MUBs. We provide a systematic computational framework for testing candidate phase vectors, bridging the gap between analytical insight and numerical exploration. Finally, we generalize the discussion to arbitrary prime-power dimensions, emphasizing the role of finite-field structures, Heisenberg-Weyl operators, and discrete symmetries in generating complete sets of MUBs. Our work offers a transparent, line-by-line verification methodology, highlighting both the geometric and algebraic richness of MUBs, and clarifying why certain dimensions resist full analytical constructions. This study serves as a comprehensive resource for researchers seeking both theoretical understanding and practical construction of MUBs in quantum information science.

### [124] [Bootstrapping Symmetries in Quantum Many-Body Systems from the Cross Spectral Form Factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01296)
*Chen Bai,Zihan Zhou,Bastien Lapierre,Shinsei Ryu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种自举框架（bootstrap framework），用于从已知子群N和其对称性扇区间的谱关联中，重建量子多体晶格哈密顿量隐藏有限群对称性的表示论数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性在量子多体物理中至关重要，但系统性地揭示隐藏对称性仍具挑战性。现有方法难以仅从已知对称子群和谱数据中重建完整的对称群表示论。

Method: 引入交叉谱形状因子（cross spectral form factor, xSFF）作为新变体，通过精确对角化计算。结合融合规则（fusion rules）的代数条件，构建自举算法来约束候选群G的集合。

Result: 该方法能系统恢复完整对称群G的表示论数据，包括不可约表示的数量与维度、相对于N的分支规则（branching rules）、融合代数（fusion algebra）和完整特征标表（character table）。框架适用于混沌和可积系统，兼容幺正和反幺正对称性。

Conclusion: 该自举框架为直接从动力学谱可观测量识别对称性提供了实用途径，成功应用于多个模型，包括三态量子环面链、驱动玻色-哈伯德模型和一维费米-哈伯德模型。

Abstract: Symmetries play a central role in quantum many-body physics, yet uncovering them systematically remains challenging. We introduce a bootstrap framework designed to reconstruct the representation theory of hidden finite group symmetries of quantum many-body lattice Hamiltonians, using only a known symmetry subgroup $N$ and spectral correlations between its symmetry sectors. We introduce a novel variant of the spectral form factor, the cross spectral form factor (xSFF), which we compute via exact diagonalization to seed the bootstrap algorithm. By applying the constraints derived from these data alongside the algebraic conditions of the fusion rules, our bootstrap procedure sharply restricts the set of candidate groups $G$. Remarkably, without any prior assumptions regarding the full symmetry group $G$, our method can systematically recover its representation-theoretic data, including the number and dimensions of the irreducible representations, their branching rules with respect to $N$, the fusion algebra, and the full character table. This framework applies equally well to chaotic and integrable many-body systems and accommodates both unitary and anti-unitary symmetries. Through various examples, we demonstrate that the underlying group $G$ can be uniquely identified. In particular, our bootstrap independently recovers the $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry at the self-dual point of the three-state quantum torus chain, detects signatures of projective representations in the effective Hamiltonian of the driven Bose-Hubbard model, and rediscovers the $η$-pairing $\mathrm{SO}(4)$ symmetry of the one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model. Our framework thus establishes a practical route to identify symmetries directly from dynamical spectral observables.

</details>


### [125] [Codimension-controlled universality of quantum Fisher information singularities at topological band-touching defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01515)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了拓扑相变中量子费希尔信息（QFI）的奇异标度行为由能带接触缺陷的余维数（codimension）p决定，而非空间维度或能带结构，建立了动量空间拓扑分类与参数空间量子可区分性之间的直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管针对特定模型已计算了保真度敏感性和量子费希尔信息的奇异行为，但尚未建立统一原理来解释这些结果：控制变量究竟是空间维度、能带结构还是缺陷的内在几何性质仍不明确。

Method: 通过分析能带接触缺陷的余维数p，推导了量子费希尔信息相对于调谐参数m的奇异贡献的普适幂律标度行为，并利用重整化群论证在线性化不动点处的保护性。

Result: 量子费希尔信息的奇异贡献遵循普适标度律：当p≠2时标度为∼|m|^{p-2}，在边际余维数p=2时呈现对数发散∼ln(1/|m|)。该指数独立于空间维度、各向异性、紫外正规化和额外有能隙能带。

Conclusion: 该结果将SSH链（p=1）、陈绝缘体（p=2）和外尔半金属（p=3）等先前孤立观察统一为单一余维数依赖的普适类，并揭示只有p≤2的缺陷会产生发散的信息几何响应，建立了动量空间拓扑分类与参数空间量子可区分性之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Topological phase transitions in generic multiband systems are mediated by band-touching defects whose codimension -- the number of momentum directions along which the gap closes linearly -- varies across universality classes. Although singular behavior of fidelity susceptibilities and quantum Fisher information (QFI) has been computed for specific models, no unifying principle connecting these results has been identified: it has remained unclear whether the controlling variable is spatial dimensionality, band structure, or an intrinsic geometric property of the defect. We resolve this question by showing that the singular contribution to the QFI with respect to the tuning parameter $m$ obeys a universal power-law scaling $\sim |m|^{p-2}$ for $p \neq 2$, with a logarithmic divergence $\sim \ln(1/|m|)$ at the marginal codimension $p = 2$, where $p$ denotes the codimension of the band-touching defect. This exponent is independent of spatial dimensionality, anisotropies, ultraviolet regularization, and additional gapped bands, and is protected by renormalization-group arguments at the linearized fixed point. The result unifies previously isolated observations for SSH chains ($p=1$), Chern insulators ($p=2$), and Weyl semimetals ($p=3$) as instances of a single codimension-dependent universality class, and reveals that only defects with $p \leq 2$ generate divergent information-geometric responses. This establishes a direct and previously missing link between topological classification in momentum space and quantum distinguishability in parameter space, with implications for metrological sensitivity near topological transitions and for the experimental detection of topological criticality via quantum geometric observables.

</details>

Further, SFSE is discovered in $1$-dimensional Hermitian chain with pure imaginary impurity at the end. ### [127] [Universal critical timescales in slow non-Hermitian dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01918)
*Giorgos Pappas,Diego Bautista Avilés,Luis E. F. Foa Torres,Vassos Achilleos*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究推导了非厄米系统中临界时间尺度 $T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ 的显式公式，该公式区分了平均主导本征态保持区与瞬时主导本征态接管区，并揭示了精度诱导不可逆性在正向演化中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统在缓慢参数循环驱动下会发生非绝热跃迁，其结果对驱动速度高度敏感，但此前缺乏临界时间尺度 $T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ 的显式公式来准确描述这些跃迁的发展。

Method: 使用具有圆形参数轨迹的 $2\times 2$ 哈密顿量，针对非环绕、相移、偏移以及环绕例外点（exceptional points）的循环，推导出 $T_{\mathrm{cr}} = \mathcal{G}\,\ln(1/|Δ|)$ 的闭式解，其中 $\mathcal{G}$ 为几何相关增长因子，$Δ$ 为不稳定性种子。

Result: 该公式清晰划分了两个区域：系统保持在平均主导本征态的区域（$T< T_{\mathrm{cr}}$）与瞬时主导本征态接管的超绝热区域（$T> T_{\mathrm{cr}}$），解决了先前文献中的明显矛盾。研究识别出两个竞争种子：几何斯托克斯乘子（geometric Stokes multiplier）与有限精度下限。

Conclusion: 当几何种子消失时，精度单独控制跃迁，导致 $T_{\mathrm{cr}} \propto m\lnβ$，与精度比特数 $m$ 呈线性关系。这提供了精度诱导不可逆性（precision-induced irreversibility, PIR）的纯正向演化表现，表明通过回波协议识别的基本极限也控制着无需时间反演的缓慢非厄米动力学结果。对于PT对称能谱，$T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ 还决定了手性（chirality）的出现：$T< T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ 时动力学非手性，$T> T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ 时手性。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian systems driven along slow parametric loops undergo non-adiabatic transitions whose outcome depends sensitively on the driving speed, yet no explicit formula has been available for the critical timescale $T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ at which these transitions develop. Using a $2\times 2$ Hamiltonian with circular parameter trajectories, we derive $T_{\mathrm{cr}} = \mathcal{G}\,\ln(1/|Δ|)$ in closed form for non-encircling loops, phase-shifted loops, offset loops, and loops encircling exceptional points, where $\mathcal{G}$ is a geometry-dependent growth factor and $Δ$ is the instability seed. This formula sharply separates the regime where the system remains in the averagely dominant eigenstate ($T< T_{\mathrm{cr}}$) from the superadiabatic regime where the instantaneous dominant eigenstate takes over ($T> T_{\mathrm{cr}}$), resolving the apparent tension between the previous literature. We identify two competing seeds: a geometric Stokes multiplier and the finite-precision floor. When the geometric seed vanishes, precision alone governs the transition, yielding $T_{\mathrm{cr}} \propto m\lnβ$, linear in the number of precision bits $m$. This provides a purely forward-evolution manifestation of precision-induced irreversibility (PIR)~\cite{PIR}, demonstrating that the fundamental limit identified through echo protocols also controls the outcome of slow non-Hermitian dynamics without requiring time reversal. For PT-symmetric energy spectra, $T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ additionally determines the onset of chirality: the dynamics is non-chiral for $T< T_{\mathrm{cr}}$ and chiral for $T> T_{\mathrm{cr}}$.

</details>

Method: 采用基于半导体量子点发射器的机架式移动量子光源架构，通过模块化系统集成实现光学激发、收集、低温操作和控制电子器件的整合。系统采用标准化机架尺寸和自动化监控，实现了自动化操作。

Conclusion: 该工作通过展示在行业对齐系统架构中同时实现高纠缠质量、持续亮度和长期操作稳定性，推动了半导体量子点源向可部署纠缠光子源的发展，为应用量子光子学提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Entangled photon pair sources are a key enabling technology for quantum communication and networking, yet their deployment beyond laboratory environments is hindered by system-level complexity, limited operational stability, and insufficient industry compatibility. Here, we demonstrate a rack-based, mobile quantum light source architecture based on a semiconductor quantum dot emitter that directly addresses these challenges through modular system integration and automated operation. The source generates polarization-entangled photon pairs with an entanglement negativity 2n of up to $0.98(1)$, confirming near-maximal entanglement quality. In continuous, hands-off operation over a six-hour time window, the system achieves an average single-photon emission rate of $697(8)$ kHz and a maximum rate of $740(7)$ kHz, while maintaining 2n-value of more than $95$ $\%$. These results are enabled by the integration of optical excitation, collection, cryogenic operation, and control electronics within a standardized rack footprint, together with automated monitoring. By demonstrating simultaneously high entanglement quality, sustained brightness, and long-term operational stability in an industry-aligned system architecture, this work advances semiconductor quantum dot sources toward deployable entangled photon sources for applied quantum photonics.

### [129] [High-threshold decoding of non-Pauli codes for 2D universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02033)
*Julio C. Magdalena de la Fuente,Noa Feldman,Jens Eisert,Andreas Bauer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种非泡利稳定子码（non-Pauli stabilizer code），用于在严格二维拓扑环面码和表面码上实现低开销通用门集，并开发了即时匹配解码器（JIT matching decoder）来处理所需的中间X校正，获得了约2.5%的高阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑量子码虽具有容错量子计算的优越特性，但在有限连接性下实现低开销通用门集仍面临核心挑战。本研究旨在探索非泡利稳定子码，以在严格二维拓扑码上完成通用门集。

Method: 采用非泡利稳定子码（non-Pauli stabilizer code）构建二维拓扑码的通用门集，并开发即时匹配解码器（just-in-time matching decoder）来处理容错综合征提取所需的中间X校正（mid-circuit X corrections）。同时研究了利用X校正知识改进Z解码的方法。

Result: 在物理错误和测量错误等概率的唯象错误模型下，获得了约2.5%的高阈值，接近完整综合征历史解码器的约2.9%阈值。有限尺寸标度分析显示逻辑错误率在阈值以下随物理错误率和系统尺寸呈指数抑制。通过改进Z解码，阈值可从约1.8%提升至约2.2%。

Conclusion: 结果表明二维码中的非克利福德逻辑（non-Clifford logic）性能可与二维量子存储器相媲美。该高效基准测试和解码形式可直接推广到更广泛的CSS码族，其X稳定子被对角克利福德算子扭曲，并由CCZ、CS和T门丰富的类CSS电路定义。

Abstract: Topological codes have many desirable properties that allow fault-tolerant quantum computation with relatively low overhead. A core challenge for these codes, however, is to achieve a low-overhead universal gate set with limited connectivity. In this work, we explore a non-Pauli stabilizer code that can be used to complete a universal gate set on topological toric and surface codes in strictly two dimensions. Fault-tolerant syndrome extraction for the non-Pauli code requires mid-circuit $X$ corrections, a key difference to conventional Pauli codes. We construct and benchmark a just-in-time (JIT) matching decoder to reliably decide these corrections. Under a phenomenological error model with equally likely physical and measurement errors, we find a high threshold of $\approx 2.5\,\%$, close to the $\approx 2.9\,\%$ of a decoder with access to the full syndrome history. We also perform a finite-size scaling analysis to estimate how the logical error rate scales below threshold and verify an exponential suppression in both physical error rate and in the system size. A second global decoding step for $Z$ errors is required and the non-Clifford gates in the circuit reduce the threshold from $\approx 2.9\,\%$ to $\approx 1.8\,\%$ with a naive decoder. We show how $Z$ decoding can be improved using knowledge of the $X$ corrections, pushing the threshold to $\approx 2.2\,\%$. Our results suggest non-Clifford logic in 2D codes could perform comparably to 2D quantum memory. Our formalism for efficient benchmarking and decoding directly generalizes to a broader family of CSS codes whose $X$ stabilizers are twisted by diagonal Clifford operators, and spacetime versions thereof, defined by CSS-like circuits enriched by $CCZ$, $CS$, and $T$ gates.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用鲁棒的前馈架构，回收并解调现有的主从拍频信号，驱动单个电光调制器（electro-optic modulator）实现近瞬时噪声消除，同时通过主动稳定拍频幅度和解调相位确保系统稳定性。

Abstract: Ultra-narrow-linewidth lasers with suppressed high-frequency phase noise are critical for quantum control and precision metrology. While optical phase locking (OPL) is the standard technique for cloning the coherence of such sources, its effectiveness is often limited at high frequencies by feedback latency. This approach eliminates the extraneous sidebands and transmission losses typical of more complex modulators. This hardware-efficient framework is readily compatible with standard OPL setups, offering a scalable solution for high-fidelity coherent control.

### [131] [Sven: Singular Value Descent as a Computationally Efficient Natural Gradient Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01279)
*Samuel Bright-Thonney,Thomas R. Harvey,Andre Lukas,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Sven（奇异值下降）算法，一种利用损失函数在数据点层面分解特性的新型神经网络优化方法，通过伪逆近似实现高效优化，在回归任务中显著优于Adam等一阶方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统优化方法将完整损失函数简化为单一标量后再计算参数更新，而Sven利用损失函数自然分解为各数据点贡献的特性，将每个数据点的残差视为需同时满足的独立条件。

Method: Sven使用损失雅可比矩阵（loss Jacobian）的Moore-Penrose伪逆（pseudoinverse）寻找最小范数参数更新，通过截断奇异值分解（truncated singular value decomposition）保留k个最重要方向，计算开销仅比随机梯度下降（stochastic gradient descent）增加k倍。

Result: 在回归任务中，Sven显著优于包括Adam在内的标准一阶方法，收敛更快且达到更低的最终损失，同时与LBFGS相比在计算时间成本上具有竞争力；该方法可理解为过参数化（over-parametrized）机制下自然梯度方法（natural gradient methods）的推广。

Conclusion: Sven在标准机器学习基准测试中表现优异，主要挑战在于内存开销，作者提出了缓解策略；该方法在科学计算领域具有自然应用前景，特别是针对可分解为多个条件的自定义损失函数场景。

Abstract: We introduce Sven (Singular Value dEsceNt), a new optimization algorithm for neural networks that exploits the natural decomposition of loss functions into a sum over individual data points, rather than reducing the full loss to a single scalar before computing a parameter update. Sven treats each data point's residual as a separate condition to be satisfied simultaneously, using the Moore-Penrose pseudoinverse of the loss Jacobian to find the minimum-norm parameter update that best satisfies all conditions at once. In practice, this pseudoinverse is approximated via a truncated singular value decomposition, retaining only the $k$ most significant directions and incurring a computational overhead of only a factor of $k$ relative to stochastic gradient descent. This is in comparison to traditional natural gradient methods, which scale as the square of the number of parameters. We show that Sven can be understood as a natural gradient method generalized to the over-parametrized regime, recovering natural gradient descent in the under-parametrized limit. On regression tasks, Sven significantly outperforms standard first-order methods including Adam, converging faster and to a lower final loss, while remaining competitive with LBFGS at a fraction of the wall-time cost. We discuss the primary challenge to scaling, namely memory overhead, and propose mitigation strategies. Beyond standard machine learning benchmarks, we anticipate that Sven will find natural application in scientific computing settings where custom loss functions decompose into several conditions.

</details>

### [132] [Relativistic Effects on Photoabsorption Cross Sections of Highly Charged Ions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01971)
*Anvar Khujakulov,Caterina Cocchi*

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比含时薛定谔方程（TDSE）和含时狄拉克方程（TDDE）模拟，系统分析了高电荷离子（highly charged ions）在极端电磁环境下的光吸收特性，揭示了相对论效应随核电荷增加而增强的规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高电荷离子为研究极端电磁环境下非相对论理论的失效提供了独特平台。研究旨在探究相对论效应对高电荷离子光吸收特性的影响，并评估不同理论框架的适用性。

Method: 采用含时薛定谔方程（TDSE）和含时狄拉克方程（TDDE）在偶极近似下模拟高电荷离子的光吸收过程，将外场建模为瞬时宽带激发。利用非相对论标度关系（nonrelativistic scaling relations）作为诊断工具，系统识别和量化相对论贡献。

Result: 在纯非相对论TDSE框架下，标度关系精确成立，任意高电荷离子的吸收谱可直接从中性氢参考系推断。但随着核电荷增加，相对论效应通过吸收截面的显著蓝移（blue shift）占据主导地位，这源于结合能的相对论增强（relativistic enhancement of the binding energy）。

Conclusion: 通过直接对比全TDDE模拟，评估了半相对论TDSE近似的预测能力，并确立了全狄拉克处理对于定量精度不可或缺的适用范围。研究为理解极端电磁环境下的相对论效应提供了系统分析框架。

Abstract: The study of highly charged ions offers a unique platform for probing the breakdown of non-relativistic theory under the influence of extreme electromagnetic environments. Here, we investigate the photoabsorption of highly charged ions within the dipole approximation using both the time-dependent Schrödinger equation (TDSE) and the time-dependent Dirac equation (TDDE), modelling the external field as an instantaneous broadband excitation. Nonrelativistic scaling relations with respect to the nuclear charge are utilized as a diagnostic tool to systematically identify and quantify relativistic contributions. Within the purely nonrelativistic TDSE framework, these scaling relations hold exactly, allowing the absorption spectra of arbitrary highly charged ions to be inferred directly from a neutral hydrogenic reference. However, as the nuclear charge increases, relativistic effects become dominant through a sizeable blue shift in the absorption cross section, due to the relativistic enhancement of the binding energy. We further evaluate semi-relativistic TDSE approximations by direct comparison with full TDDE simulations, assessing their predictive power and establishing the regimes where a full Dirac treatment is indispensable for quantitative accuracy.

### [133] [On topological frustration and graphene magnonics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01227)

Motivation: 研究旨在探索蜂窝晶格中的图论拓扑阻挫（graph-theoretic topological frustration）现象在二维系统中的持续存在性，特别是针对被归类为隐蔽非凯库勒烃（concealed non-Kekulean hydrocarbons）的有机分子，这些分子代表特殊的双自由基体系。

Method: 研究基于蜂窝晶格的二维系统进行分析，展示了拓扑阻挫现象如何导致完全平坦的电子能带（fully flat electronic energy bands）位于费米能级，并系统构建了石墨烯单层纳米网（graphene monolayer nanomeshes）的最终平坦能带。

Result: 二维系统表现出位于费米能级的完全平坦电子能带，这些系统倾向于反铁磁有序（antiferromagnetic ordering）和混合自旋波激发（hybrid spin-wave excitations），同时混合了弱铁磁和强反铁磁特征。

Conclusion: 该研究为低功耗、紧凑、超快且能在接近室温条件下工作的有机自旋电子学（organic spintronics）开辟了新途径，通过可预测构建的平坦能带系统实现了对自旋有序和激发的控制。

Abstract: The graph-theoretic topological frustration is a peculiar situation on a finite piece of the honeycomb lattice that prevents a full pairwise coupling of the lattice sites via nearest neighbor links, even when the total number of sites is an even number. This type of frustration is inherent for organic molecules that are classified as concealed non-Kekulean hydrocarbons, representing peculiar diradicals. Here we show that this topological frustration persists in 2D systems based on honeycomb lattice. Such systems exhibit fully flat electronic energy bands located at the Fermi level. Therefore, 2D ultimately flat bands can be systematically and predictably constructed for graphene monolayer nanomeshes. These systems are prone to antiferromagnetic ordering and hybrid spin-wave excitations mixing weak ferromagnetic and strong antiferromagnetic features, which could pave the way towards low-power, compact, and ultrafast organic spintronics with near room-temperature operation.

</details>


### [134] [Time-evolving matrix product operators for off-diagonal system-bath coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01556)
*Chu Guo,Wei Wu,Xiansong Xu,Tian Jiang,Ping-Xing Chen,Ruofan Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TEMPO方法在受限条件下发展，需要扩展至更一般的量子杂质问题，特别是处理非对角系统-浴耦合的情况。

Method: 基于过程张量框架，扩展时间演化矩阵乘积算子方法，适用于任何浴为非相互作用且系统与浴线性耦合的量子杂质问题。

Result: 通过研究Jaynes-Cummings型系统-浴耦合的自旋与亚欧姆浴的实时动力学，发现常用旋波近似在结构浴存在时容易失效。

Conclusion: 该方法为理解不同TEMPO变体提供了统一框架，可直接推广至尚未探索的费米子系统，并可作为玻色动力学平均场理论中的杂质求解器。

Abstract: Based on the process tensor framework, we extend the time-evolving matrix product operator (TEMPO) method to solve bosonic quantum impurity problems (QIPs) with off-diagonal system-bath coupling. Our method is a most generic extension of TEMPO, which applies for any QIPs as long as the bath is noninteracting and the system is linearly coupled to the bath. It naturally contains all the current developments of TEMPO in more restricted settings. As an application, we study the real-time dynamics of a spin that is coupled to a sub-ohmic bath via the Jaynes-Cummings-type system-bath coupling, and compare it against that of the standard spin-boson model. Our results show that the commonly used secular approximation could easily fail in presence of a structural bath. Our method provides a unified framework to understand different variants of TEMPO and directly suggests a fermionic generalization which has not been explored so far, it could also be straightforwardly used as an impurity solver in the bosonic dynamical mean field theory.

### [135] [Optimal skyrmion stability in antisymmetric ultrathin ferromagnetic bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02070)
*Anne Bernand-Mantel,Valeriy V. Slastikov,Cyrill B. Muratov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了基于传统过渡金属材料的超薄交换解耦反对称铁磁双层结构通过杂散场介导稳定斯格明子（skyrmion）的能力，为实验观测10纳米半径零场斯格明子提供了新途径。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决单层结构中Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用与偶极相互作用相互竞争的问题，探索通过反对称双层结构实现这两种相互作用协同作用以稳定斯格明子的新方法。

Method: 采用在超薄薄膜极限下有效的渐近精确微磁模型，对分离斯格明子与退磁状态的鞍点解进行渐近分析，并通过基于传统Pt/Co/AlO$_x$系统磁参数的广泛微磁模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 反对称双层结构使Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用与偶极相互作用协同作用稳定斯格明子，在有效Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用强度和有效薄膜厚度的无量纲参数空间中获得了紧凑斯格明子的最优稳定性线。

Conclusion: 该研究为实验观测10纳米半径零场斯格明子提供了新途径，其寿命与信息技术应用兼容，展示了反对称铁磁双层结构在稳定纳米尺度斯格明子方面的潜力。

Abstract: We demonstrate the stray-field-mediated skyrmion stabilizing
  capabilities of ultrathin exchange-decoupled antisymmetric
  ferromagnetic bilayers based on conventional transition metal
  materials. Using an asymptotically exact micromagnetic model valid
  in the ultrathin film limit, we show that the antisymmetric
  tailoring of the bilayer allows the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya
  interaction and the dipolar interaction to act synergistically to
  stabilize skyrmions, in contrast to the monolayer case, in which
  these energies compete. To obtain optimal stability of these
  skyrmions against collapse and bursting -- the two fundamental
  processes determining skyrmion lifetime, we carry out an asymptotic
  analysis of the saddle point solution that separates the skyrmion
  from the demagnetized state. The result is an optimal stability line
  for compact skyrmions in the non-dimensional parameter space of the
  effective Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction strength and the
  effective film thickness. Our predictions are confirmed by extensive
  micromagnetic simulations of antisymmetric bilayers, using magnetic
  parameters of the conventional Pt/Co/AlO$_x$ systems. Our results
  provide a new pathway for experimental observations of 10 nm radius
  zero-field skyrmions with lifetimes compatible with information
  technology applications.

Conclusion: 该研究强调了在二维材料电子输运特性分析中必须考虑动态屏蔽效应的重要性，特别是对于极性声子散射过程，无论这些声子来源于半导体本身还是周围层，这一理论框架具有广泛的适用性。

Abstract: We study the interplay between long-range electron-phonon and electron-electron interactions in electrostatically doped two-dimensional semiconductors, including interlayer couplings in van der Waals heterostructures. We evaluate the effects of those interactions on transport properties by writing dynamically coupled Boltzmann equations for the electrons and for the electrodynamically active excitations. We develop a theory with a general validity, and apply it both to simplified parabolic models, and to the realistic BN-encapsulated graphene system which we present in an accompanying paper [arXiv:2604.00678]. We show that dynamical screening effects are of fundamental importance in order to correctly describe the electronic transport properties of two-dimensional materials, and in particular the scattering from polar phonons, whether those come from the semiconductor itself or the surrounding layers.

### [137] [Quasi-1D Planar Magnetic Topological Heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01823)
*Z. Z. Alisultanov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文理论提出了一种准一维磁性异质结构，由交替的二维拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）和普通绝缘体（normal insulator）条带组成。该结构展现出丰富的拓扑相，并可通过磁性缺陷（magnetic defect）作为局域探针进行探测，多层结构则呈现莫比乌斯带（Möbius band）拓扑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于通过异质结构设计和磁性图案化（magnetic patterning）建立高阶拓扑（higher-order topology）的研究平台。具体而言，旨在探索由交替的二维拓扑绝缘体和普通绝缘体条带构成的准一维磁性异质结构中的拓扑物理。

Method: 研究方法基于理论引入的准一维磁性异质结构模型。其低能物理由混合哈密顿量（hybrid Hamiltonian）描述，该哈密顿量交织了Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型和Shockley模型，并包含自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）和局域塞曼劈裂（local Zeeman splitting）。通过对称性分析确定其属于AIII类（class AIII），并计算哈密顿量块非对角结构（block-off-diagonal structure）的绕数（winding number）来揭示拓扑相。

Result: 研究结果揭示了由拓扑不变量ν=0、1和2表征的拓扑相。单个磁性缺陷（magnetic defect）可作为灵敏的局域探针，其带隙内谱（in-gap spectrum）提供了区分拓扑相的光谱指纹（spectroscopic fingerprint）。将平台扩展到多层几何结构时，发现了一种非简单（nonsymmorphic）投影对称性，导致了莫比乌斯带拓扑（Möbius band topology），并使布里渊区（Brillouin zone）紧致化为克莱因瓶（Klein bottle）。

Conclusion: 本文通过异质结构设计和磁性图案化建立了一个研究高阶拓扑的平台。该工作展示了准一维磁性异质结构中丰富的拓扑物理，包括由整数拓扑不变量表征的相、磁性缺陷的探测能力，以及多层结构中出现的奇特莫比乌斯带拓扑。

Abstract: We theoretically introduce a quasi-1D magnetic heterostructure of alternating 2D topological and normal insulator strips. Its low-energy physics is governed by a hybrid Hamiltonian intertwining the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger and Shockley models, with spin-momentum locking and local Zeeman splitting. Symmetry analysis places it in class AIII, characterized by chiral symmetry and a $\mathbb{Z}$ topological invariant. Computing the winding number from the block-off-diagonal structure of the Hamiltonian reveals topological phases characterized by invariants $ν= 0$, $1$, and $2$. Furthermore, a single magnetic defect acts as a sensitive local probe, whose in-gap spectrum provides a spectroscopic fingerprint to distinguish topological phases. Extending the platform to a multilayer geometry uncovers a nonsymmorphic projective symmetry that gives rise to Möbius band topology, with the Brillouin zone compactifying into a Klein bottle. Our work establishes a platform for higher-order topology via heterostructure design and magnetic patterning.

### [138] [Quantum anomalous Hall conductivity in altermagnets under applied magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01948)
*Meysam Bagheri Tagani,Amar Fakhredine,Carmine Autieri*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维d波交变磁体（altermagnet）在磁场下的量子反常霍尔电导（quantum anomalous Hall conductivity）涌现机制。通过分析Lieb晶格上的能带结构和拓扑性质，揭示了谷依赖（valley-dependent）的拓扑相变和快速磁调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究交变磁体（altermagnet）在磁场下的拓扑性质，探索量子反常霍尔效应（quantum anomalous Hall effect）的新调控机制。交变磁序产生动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）而无净磁化，为拓扑相变提供了独特平台。

Method: 采用二维d波交变磁体在Lieb晶格上的模型，施加外磁场。通过分析能带结构、相图（phase diagram）和贝里曲率（Berry curvature），研究谷依赖的拓扑性质。重点关注磁场对谷间旋转对称性（rotational symmetry between valleys）的破坏效应。

Result: 相图包含正常绝缘体（normal insulator）和自旋陈绝缘体（spin Chern insulator），由偶然狄拉克半金属（accidental Dirac semimetal）分隔。磁场使谷间旋转对称性破缺，导致谷依赖的拓扑贡献：一个谷支持陈数C=-1或0，另一个谷支持C=0或+1。贝里曲率分析显示总陈数为C=±1的全隙相（fully gapped phases），通过谷选择性能隙闭合（valley-selective gap closings）分隔。

Conclusion: 揭示了交变磁体中量子反常霍尔效应的快速磁调控机制，该机制发生在半金属相附近。研究结果突出了交变磁体系统与铁谷电子学（ferro-valleytronic）和量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）系统的关键区别，为拓扑物态调控提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of quantum anomalous Hall conductivity in a two-dimensional $d$-wave altermagnet on a Lieb lattice under an external magnetic field. Altermagnetic order induces momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization in the relativistic limit, producing distinct spin-resolved bands at the $X$ and $Y$ valleys. The phase diagram features a normal insulator and a spin Chern insulator separated by an accidental Dirac semimetal. The magnetic field breaks rotational symmetry between valleys while maintaining vanishing total magnetization, enabling independent valley contributions to topology. One valley supports Chern numbers $C=-1$ or $0$, while the other hosts $C=0$ or $+1$, governed by field strength and bandwidth. This competition yields valley-dependent topology. Berry curvature analysis reveals fully gapped phases with total Chern numbers $C=\pm1$, separated by valley-selective gap closings. We uncover a mechanism for rapid magnetic control of the quantum anomalous Hall effect near the semimetal phase and highlight key distinctions from ferro-valleytronic and quantum spin Hall systems.

</details>


### [139] [Strong nonlinear thermoelectricity generation and close-to-Carnot efficient heat engines in Superconductor-Insulator-2D electron gas junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02123)
*Leonardo Lucchesi,Federico Paolucci*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该SISm结产生的塞贝克电势（Seebeck potential）可达$6.75Δ_0$，具有巨大的非线性塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）。热电效率接近卡诺效率$η=0.96η_C$，创下固态器件模型的记录。

Abstract: We find that a novel Superconductor-Insulator-2D electron gas tunnel junction (SISm) strongly and efficiently generates thermoelectricity via a nonlinear mechanism. We simulate across the parameter space of the junction, finding and discussing different regimes with features useful for thermoelectricity generation or for specific applications. The generated Seebeck potential can go up to $6.75Δ_0$ with a huge nonlinear Seebeck coefficient, and efficiency can get very close to Carnot efficiency $η=0.96η_C$, a record for a solid-state device model. Thermoelectric performance is far better than analogous junctions, with fewer fabrication challenges, as the device can be fabricated via standard methods.
