### [140] [Generalized Beth-Uhlenbeck Approach to the 2+1D Gross-Neveu Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02246)
*Biplab Mahato,David Blaschke*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了受石墨烯启发的(2+1)维Gross-Neveu模型的热力学，特别关注高斯涨落对熵密度的贡献。研究发现涨落贡献显著，甚至可与平均场相比，并采用广义Beth-Uhlenbeck方法自洽处理涨落对平均场的反作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于理解(2+1)维Gross-Neveu模型在石墨烯背景下的热力学性质，特别关注超越平均场的高斯涨落对熵密度的贡献。需要自洽处理涨落对平均场的反作用，以准确描述二维材料中的物理过程。

Method: 采用广义Beth-Uhlenbeck方法（generalized Beth-Uhlenbeck approach）计算熵密度，该方法能够自洽处理涨落对平均场的反作用。通过全介质、动量依赖的评估来研究高斯涨落，相比标准Beth-Uhlenbeck公式，广义版本抑制了低能贡献同时保留了束缚态效应。

Result: 研究发现高斯涨落对熵密度有显著贡献，甚至可与平均场贡献相比。涨落对平均场的反作用主要减少了来自朗道阻尼区域（Landau-damping region）的贡献。广义Beth-Uhlenbeck方法揭示了束缚激子（bound excitons）和自由费米子（free fermions）携带的分数熵，显示出更尖锐的自由度交叉（crossover）。

Conclusion: 广义Beth-Uhlenbeck方法能够更准确地描述二维材料中的Mott转变物理（Mott-transition physics）。该方法通过抑制低能贡献同时保留束缚态效应，提供了对涨落贡献的自洽处理，与二维材料中的物理现象一致。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics of the (2+1) dimensional Gross-Neveu model inspired from graphene. We focus on the entropy density of the Gaussian fluctuation beyond the mean field. The full in-medium, momentum-dependent evaluation reveals that the fluctuations give a substantial contribution, even comparable to that of the mean field. We argue that the back-reaction from the fluctuations to the mean field should be included, which reduces the contribution mainly coming from the Landau-damping region. To treat this self-consistently, we use the generalized version of the Beth-Uhlenbeck approach for the entropy density. Compared with the standard Beth-Uhlenbeck formulation, the generalized version suppresses the low-energy contributions while preserving the bound-state effects. The fractional entropy carried by bound excitons and free fermions reveals a sharper crossover of the degrees of freedom in the generalized version, which is consistent with Mott-transition physics in two-dimensional materials.

</details>

### [141] [Smoluchowski Coagulation Equation and the Evolution of Primordial Black Hole Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01684)
*Borui Zhang,Wei-Xiang Feng,Haipeng An*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文通过求解Smoluchowski凝聚方程，模拟了原始黑洞（PBH）在星系团内的连续合并过程，解释了JWST发现的"小红点"中高红移超大质量黑洞的成因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（James Webb Space Telescope, JWST）发现的"小红点（little red dots）"中高红移（high-redshift）超大质量黑洞的起源问题，探索原始黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）在小尺度上的聚集机制。

Method: 通过求解Smoluchowski凝聚方程（Smoluchowski coagulation equation）模拟PBH在星系团内的连续合并过程，推导了考虑质量分层（mass segregation）效应和无此效应两种情况下的凝聚核（coagulation kernel）。采用蒙特卡洛方法（Monte Carlo method）求解方程，并利用离散逆变换方法（discrete inverse transformation method）实现全条件方案（full-conditioning scheme）。

Result: 模拟确定了星系团的失控时间尺度（runaway timescales）以及PBH质量种群在广泛宇宙红移范围内的演化规律，这些结果依赖于星系团内PBH的数量和相关密度参数。

Conclusion: 研究表明，小尺度上原始黑洞的聚集和连续合并过程能够合理解释JWST观测到的高红移超大质量黑洞现象，为"小红点"的物理本质提供了理论解释。

Abstract: In arXiv:2507.07171, we demonstrate that the high-redshift supermassive black holes in the so-called "little red dots" discovered by James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) can be explained by the primordial black hole (PBH) clustering on small scales. In this paper, we present a comprehensive simulation of the successive PBH mergers within a cluster by solving the Smoluchowski coagulation equation. We derive the coagulation kernel considering both cases with and without the effects of mass segregation. Then we employ the Monte Carlo method to solve the equation, implementing the full-conditioning scheme using the discrete inverse transformation method. Our simulations determine the runaway timescales of clusters and the mass population evolution of PBHs across a wide range of cosmic redshifts, depending on the number of PBHs within the cluster and the associated density.

</details>

Through this modification, we can reveal the effects of the minimal length on the late-time structure of the universe. We employ the $f$ and $fσ_8$ measurements of the growth rate combined with background data, including cosmic chronometers, baryon acoustic oscillations and Type Ia supernova observations. The observational constraints reveal a systematically negative value for the deformation parameter $β$, with the $Λ$CDM limit lying within the 95\% credible interval. When supernova data are included, the Akaike Information Criterion indicates weak-to-strong support in favour of the GUP-modified model depending on the SNIa catalogue, while the Bayesian evidence suggests a weak preference.

### [143] [Gradient estimators for parameter inference in discrete stochastic kinetic models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02121)
*Ludwig Burger,Annalena Kofler,Lukas Heinrich,Ulrich Gerland*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了将机器学习中的梯度估计器应用于Gillespie随机模拟算法（SSA）进行参数推断，比较了三种梯度估计器在弛豫和振荡系统中的表现，发现不同估计器具有互补优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机动力学模型（stochastic kinetic models）在物理学中普遍存在，但从实验数据推断其参数仍然具有挑战性。确定性模型中的参数推断通常依赖梯度，但传统自动微分工具无法直接应用于Gillespie算法等随机模拟算法，因为从离散反应集合中采样引入了不可微操作。

Method: 本研究采用三种来自机器学习的梯度估计器应用于Gillespie SSA：Gumbel-Softmax Straight-Through (GS-ST)估计器、Score Function估计器和Alternative Path估计器。在两种代表性系统（弛豫或振荡动力学）中比较所有估计器的特性，其中振荡系统需要估计时间依赖目标函数的梯度。

Result: 研究发现GS-ST估计器通常产生行为良好的梯度估计，但在具有挑战性的参数区域表现出发散方差，导致参数推断失败。在这些情况下，其他估计器提供更稳健、更低方差的梯度。不同估计器在Gillespie SSA中展现出互补优势。

Conclusion: 结果表明基于梯度的参数推断可以有效地与Gillespie SSA集成，不同估计器提供互补优势，为随机动力学模型的参数推断提供了新的有效工具。

Abstract: Stochastic kinetic models are ubiquitous in physics, yet inferring their parameters from experimental data remains challenging. In deterministic models, parameter inference often relies on gradients, as they can be obtained efficiently through automatic differentiation. However, these tools cannot be directly applied to stochastic simulation algorithms (SSA) such as the Gillespie algorithm, since sampling from a discrete set of reactions introduces non-differentiable operations. In this work, we adopt three gradient estimators from machine learning for the Gillespie SSA: the Gumbel-Softmax Straight-Through (GS-ST) estimator, the Score Function estimator, and the Alternative Path estimator. We compare the properties of all estimators in two representative systems exhibiting relaxation or oscillatory dynamics, where the latter requires gradient estimation of time-dependent objective functions. We find that the GS-ST estimator mostly yields well-behaved gradient estimates, but exhibits diverging variance in challenging parameter regimes, resulting in unsuccessful parameter inference. In these cases, the other estimators provide more robust, lower variance gradients. Our results demonstrate that gradient-based parameter inference can be integrated effectively with the Gillespie SSA, with different estimators offering complementary advantages.

Abstract: Some algorithms for the numerically exact treatment of fermion determinants are summarised. This is not supposed to be a review, rather a concise handbook. The audience is expected to have a basic understanding of how to put fermions on a computer. We primarily discuss different ways to work with the fermion matrix in the "sausage" (Green's function) formulation for quantum Monte Carlo (QMC). We emphasise the need for varied approaches in different space-time volume regimes. In particular, for small spatial volumes we describe a numerically stable method based on dense matrix operations. It is designed specifically to deal with very low temperature regimes. On the other hand, for (relatively) large volumes we describe a highly efficient and scalable sparse matrix approach.

### [147] [Approximating the Permanent of a Random Matrix with Polynomially Small Mean: Zeros and Universality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01367)
*Frederic Koehler,Pui Kuen Leung*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该研究分析了随机矩阵永久式（permanent）的近似算法，针对条目略微偏离零的情况。通过建立多项式$\mathrm{per}(zJ + W)$的零自由区域（zero-free region），为线性光学和玻色子采样（boson sampling）的经典复杂性理解提供了算法基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于理解线性光学和玻色子采样（boson sampling）的经典计算复杂性。具体关注当矩阵条目略微偏离零时，永久式（permanent）的近似算法问题，这关系到Barvinok插值方法（Barvinok's interpolation method）的有效应用条件。

Method: 采用Barvinok插值方法，通过分析随机多项式$\mathrm{per}(zJ + W)$的零分布来建立零自由区域（zero-free region）。其中$J$是全1矩阵，$W$是具有独立零均值条目的随机矩阵。研究特别关注标准复高斯（standard complex Gaussians）条目的情况。

Result: 当$W$的条目为标准复高斯时，随机多项式$\mathrm{per}(zJ + W)$的所有零点位于半径$\tilde{O}(n^{-1/3})$的圆盘内，这为条目偏差（bias）$\tildeΩ(n^{-1/3})$时提供了近似算法。同时发现$(1 - ε)n$个零点具有量级$Θ(n^{-1/2})$，这避免了与永久式近似平均情况硬度（average-case hardness）猜想的矛盾。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了随机矩阵永久式的零自由区域，为线性光学和玻色子采样的经典复杂性分析提供了算法基础。同时证明了对于具有独立同分布（i.i.d.）次指数（subexponential）条目的随机矩阵$W$的零自由区域的普适性（universality）结果。

Abstract: We study algorithms for approximating the permanent of a random matrix when the entries are slightly biased away from zero. This question is motivated by the goal of understanding the classical complexity of linear optics and \emph{boson sampling} (Aaronson and Arkhipov '11; Eldar and Mehraban '17). Barvinok's interpolation method enables efficient approximation of the permanent, provided one can establish a sufficiently large zero-free region for the polynomial $\mathrm{per}(zJ + W)$, where $J$ is the all-ones matrix and $W$ is a random matrix with independent mean-zero entries.
  We show that when the entries of $W$ are standard complex Gaussians, all zeros of the random polynomial $\mathrm{per}(zJ + W)$ lie within a disk of radius $\tilde{O}(n^{-1/3})$, which yields an approximation algorithm when the bias of the entries is $\tildeΩ(n^{-1/3})$. Previously, there were no efficient algorithms at biases smaller than $1/\mathrm{polylog}(n)$, and it was unknown whether there typically exist zeros $z$ with $|z| \ge 1$. As a complementary result, we show that the bulk of the zeros, namely $(1 - ε)n$ of them, have magnitude $Θ(n^{-1/2})$. This prevents our interpolation method from contradicting the conjectured average-case hardness of approximating the permanent. We also establish analogous zero-free regions for the hardcore model on general graphs with complex vertex fugacities. In addition, we prove universality results establishing zero-free regions for random matrices $W$ with i.i.d. subexponential entries.

### [148] [Hierarchical symmetry selects log-Poisson cascades: classification, uniqueness, and stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01632)
*E. M. Freeburg*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明在独立同分布（i.i.d.）乘法级联中，层次对称性（hierarchical symmetry）这一单一公理是乘子具有对数泊松（log-Poisson）分布的必要充分条件，并建立了三个核心定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索乘法级联中层次对称性与乘子分布类型之间的精确对应关系。具体而言，旨在确定层次对称性这一公理是否能够唯一地刻画对数泊松分布，并阐明其在更广泛的对数无穷可分（log-infinitely-divisible）分布族中的特殊地位。

Method: 研究方法基于公理化框架，将层次对称性定义为增量缩放指数（incremental scaling exponents）的线性收缩。证明过程通过变量替换 $u = e^{kx}$ 将问题约化为 $[0,1]$ 区间上的Hausdorff矩问题（Hausdorff moment problem），并利用经典结果推导确定性（determinacy）和稳定性（stability）。

Result: 论文建立了三个主要结果：1）特征定理证明层次对称性唯一确定具有显式参数的对数泊松分布；2）分类定理证明层次对称性从完整的对数无穷可分族中精确选择了对数泊松类，排除了对数正态（log-normal）、对数稳定（log-stable）及所有中间生成元；3）稳定性定理证明近似层次对称性意味着近似对数泊松分布，并给出了显式的 $O(\sqrt{\varepsilon})$ Wasserstein界。

Conclusion: 结论表明层次对称性是乘法级联中乘子服从对数泊松分布的完整刻画。该公理不仅唯一确定分布类型，而且具有稳定性，即近似对称性导致近似对数泊松分布，为相关随机过程的理论分析提供了坚实基础。

Abstract: Within i.i.d. multiplicative cascades, a single axiom -- the hierarchical symmetry, a linear contraction on incremental scaling exponents -- is shown to be necessary and sufficient for the cascade multiplier to be log-Poisson. We establish three results: (1) a characterization theorem proving that the hierarchical symmetry uniquely determines the log-Poisson distribution with explicit parameters; (2) a classification theorem proving that the hierarchical symmetry selects exactly the log-Poisson class from the full log-infinitely-divisible family, excluding log-normal, log-stable, and all intermediate generators; and (3) a stability theorem proving that approximate hierarchical symmetry implies approximate log-Poisson, with an explicit $O(\sqrt{\varepsilon})$ Wasserstein bound. The proofs reduce the problem to the Hausdorff moment problem on $[0,1]$ via the change of variables $u = e^{kx}$, where determinacy and stability follow from classical results.

</details>


### [149] [Semicircle laws with combined variance for non-uniform Erdős-Rényi hypergraphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01877)
*Luca Avena,Elia Bisi,Eleonora Bordiga*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了非均匀、非齐次随机超图（random hypergraph）的邻接矩阵谱分布，建立了高斯化（Gaussianization）条件，并在非稀疏条件下推导出半圆律（semicircle law）的极限谱分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析非均匀（non-uniform）且非齐次（inhomogeneous）的随机超图模型，其中超边（hyperedges）可以具有不同尺寸，且连接概率（connection probabilities）可能依赖于超边大小。所有参数允许随超图规模缩放，这扩展了传统均匀模型的研究范围。

Method: 方法包括：1) 构建随机邻接矩阵，其(u,v)-项统计包含顶点u和v的超边数量；2) 基于Chatterjee (2005)的Pastur型条件，建立矩阵高斯化条件；3) 提出更严格但更简单的充分条件，基于模型的广义平均度（generalized average degree）。

Result: 主要结果包括：1) 刻画了期望极限谱分布（limiting spectral distribution）与连接概率和超边尺寸的关系；2) 在非稀疏条件下，极限谱分布表现为具有显式参数方差的半圆律；3) 该方差可表示为均匀情形方差的凸组合（convex combination），系数由不同非齐次源之间的权衡决定。

Conclusion: 结论表明，非均匀非齐次随机超图的谱特性可通过高斯化方法分析，并在适当条件下收敛到参数化的半圆分布。该结果统一了均匀情形，揭示了非齐次性对谱分布的定量影响。

Abstract: We consider Erdős-Rényi-type random hypergraphs that are non-uniform, in the sense that hyperedges of different sizes may coexist, and inhomogeneous, in that connection probabilities may depend on the hyperedge size. All parameters are allowed to scale with the hypergraph size. We study the random adjacency matrix whose $(u,v)$-entry counts the number of hyperedges containing both vertices $u$ and $v$, and characterize its expected limiting spectral distribution in terms of the connection probabilities and the hyperedge sizes. We provide a Pastur-type condition, in the sense of Chatterjee (2005), under which the matrix can be Gaussianized, as well as a more restrictive but simpler sufficient condition in terms of the generalized average degree of the model. As a second main result, based on such a Gaussianization, we characterize the limiting spectral distributions under non-sparse conditions as semicircle laws with an explicit parametric variance. The latter can be expressed as a convex combination of the variances arising in the uniform cases, with coefficients determined by the trade-off between the different sources of inhomogeneity.

</details>

*Raphael T. Husistein,Markus Reiher*

TL;DR: 该论文讨论了计算化学中势能超曲面（potential energy hypersurface）的重要性，以及密度泛函理论（DFT）作为主要方法的局限性。近期发展的基础机器学习原子间势（foundation machine learning interatomic potentials）有望在十年内取代DFT，实现量子精度与力场速度的结合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算化学已成为实验化学各分支不可或缺的工具，其核心概念是势能超曲面（potential energy hypersurface），为分子结构分配能量，是反应机理阐明和反应速率计算的必要基础。密度泛函理论（DFT）在实践中一直是获取这些能量的最重要方法，但计算成本高昂。

Method: 论文主要讨论了两种方法：传统的密度泛函理论（DFT）作为第一性原理方法，以及新兴的基础机器学习原子间势（foundation machine learning interatomic potentials）。后者属于一类具有量子精度与力场速度结合的替代势能函数。

Result: 基础机器学习原子间势（foundation machine learning interatomic potentials）最近克服了先前需要大量系统特定数据集进行训练的限制。这一突破有望彻底改变计算化学的研究方式，可能在十年内促使研究者放弃将DFT作为主要方法。

Conclusion: 基础机器学习原子间势（foundation machine learning interatomic potentials）将完全改变计算化学的研究范式，很可能在不到十年内取代密度泛函理论（DFT）作为获取势能超曲面能量的首选方法。

Abstract: Computational chemistry has become an indispensable tool for generating data and insights, pervading all branches of experimental chemistry. Its most central concept is the potential energy hypersurface, key to all chemistry and materials science, as it assigns an energy to a molecular structure, the necessary ingredient for reaction mechanism elucidation and reaction rate calculation. Density functional theory (DFT) has been the most important method in practice for obtaining such energies, which is mirrored in the use of high-performance computing hardware. In the last two decades, a new class of surrogate potential energy functions has been evolving with remarkable properties: quantum accuracy combined with force-field speed. Until very recently, their application was hampered by the fact that they needed to be trained on truly large system-specific data sets, generated before a computational chemistry study could be started (in sharp contrast to DFT, which, as a first-principles method, works out of the box, but at a far higher price of computational cost). Very recently, this roadblock has been overcome by so-called foundation machine learning interatomic potentials, which are poised to completely change the way we do computational chemistry, likely prompting us to abandon DFT as the prime method of choice for this purpose in less than a decade.

</details>


### [151] [Efficient Auxiliary-Field Quantum Monte Carlo using Isometric Tensor Hypercontraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02054)
*Maxine Luo,Victor Chen,Yu Wang,Christian B. Mendl*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于等距张量超压缩（isometric tensor hypercontraction, ITHC）技术的新型辅助场量子蒙特卡罗（AFQMC）方法，通过引入额外的虚构费米子模式来对角化分子电子哈密顿量中的双体库仑相互作用，降低了理论复杂度并提升了计算性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 辅助场量子蒙特卡罗（Auxiliary Field Quantum Monte Carlo, AFQMC）已成为处理强关联电子系统的有力框架，在计算成本与精度之间提供了良好的平衡。然而，标准AFQMC方法在处理双体相互作用时存在理论复杂度和计算效率方面的挑战。

Method: 本文提出了一种新颖的AFQMC方法，采用等距张量超压缩（isometric tensor hypercontraction, ITHC）技术，通过引入额外的虚构费米子模式（fictitious fermionic modes）来对角化分子电子哈密顿量中的双体库仑相互作用。与标准AFQMC方法相比，该方法在传播和局域能量评估方面具有降低的理论复杂度和更好的实际性能。

Result: 通过计算线性H10链和苯分子的基态能量，证明了该方法的有效性。扩展基组AFQMC（extended-basis AFQMC）能够以与耦合簇（Coupled Clusters, CC）或密度矩阵重整化群（Density Matrix Renormalization Group, DMRG）等高精度波函数方法相当的精度恢复多体关联效应，同时提供了显著改进的标度行为。

Conclusion: 基于ITHC技术的新型AFQMC方法在保持高精度的同时，显著降低了计算复杂度并提升了性能，为强关联电子系统的精确计算提供了更高效的框架，在计算标度方面展现出明显优势。

Abstract: Auxiliary Field Quantum Monte Carlo (AFQMC) has emerged as a powerful framework for treating strongly correlated electronic systems, offering a favorable balance between computational cost and accuracy. In this paper, we present a novel AFQMC method that uses the isometric tensor hypercontraction (ITHC) technique to diagonalize the two-body Coulomb interaction of molecular electronic Hamiltonians by introducing additional fictitious fermionic modes. Our method shows reduced theoretical complexity and better practical performance for both propagation and local energy evaluation compared to the standard AFQMC method. We demonstrate the efficacy of this approach by computing the ground-state energies of a linear $\ce{H10}$-chain and the benzene molecule. Our results show that the extended-basis AFQMC recovers many-body correlations with a precision comparable to that of high-level wavefunction methods such as Coupled Clusters (CC) or Density Matrix Renormalization Group (DMRG), while offering significantly improved scaling.

</details>

### [152] [Dissipative Floquet engineering of gapped many-body phases using thermal baths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01291)
*Lorenz Wanckel,André Eckardt*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种通用的耗散策略，用于制备和稳定受能隙保护的Floquet有效基态，通过将驱动系统耦合到特定性质的热浴来同时抑制Floquet加热并引导系统进入非平衡稳态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）通过时间周期驱动控制量子系统，使其由近似有效时间无关哈密顿量描述。然而，存在相互作用时，这类有效哈密顿量中有趣多体基态的稳定仅在一定时间尺度内可能，超过该尺度会出现Floquet加热（Floquet heating）。此外，由于非完美绝热动力学，特别是当需要穿过相变时，这类态的制备本身也受到激发挑战。

Method: 研究提出了一种通用的耗散策略，用于制备和稳定受能隙保护的有效基态。该方法依赖于将驱动系统耦合到热浴（thermal bath），热浴的性质经过选择，既能抑制Floquet加热，又能引导系统进入非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady state），使有效基态占据数大，但有效哈密顿量激发态通常具有非热占据。

Result: 研究使用Floquet-Born-Markov主方程（Floquet-Born-Markov master equation）验证了所提出的策略，以强驱动Bose-Hubbard链（Bose-Hubbard chain）为例，该链具有有效带隙的Mott绝缘体基态（gapped Mott-insulator ground state）。

Conclusion: 该耗散策略为Floquet工程中有效基态的制备和稳定提供了通用解决方案，通过热浴耦合同时解决了Floquet加热和绝热制备的挑战，实现了有效基态的高占据非平衡稳态。

Abstract: Floquet engineering, the control of a quantum system by means of time-periodic driving, allows to modify the properties of the system so that it becomes described by an approximate effective time-independent Hamiltonian. However, in the presence of interactions the stabilization of interesting many-body ground states of such effective Hamiltonians is possible only on a certain time scale, beyond which Floquet heating sets in, as it results from unwanted driving induced resonant excitation. Moreover, already the preparation of such states is challenged by excitations due to imperfect adiabatic dynamics, especially when a phase transition has to be passed. Here, we propose a general dissipative strategy for the preparation and stabilization of effective ground states that are protected by an energy gap. Our approach relies on coupling the driven system to a thermal bath, the properties of which are chosen so that it both suppresses Floquet heating and guides the system into a non-equilibrium steady state with a large occupation of the effective ground-state, but generally non-thermal occupations of excited states of the effective Hamiltonian. We use the Floquet-Born-Markov master equation to verify the proposed strategy for the example of a strongly driven Bose-Hubbard chain with an effective gapped Mott-insulator ground state.

</details>


### [153] [Sound propagation in striped supersolid cold gases at zero temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01751)
*Elena Poli,Giovanni I. Martone,Sandro Stringari,Alessio Recati*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的水动力学方法，用于描述零温下超冷偶极气体和自旋轨道耦合BEC平台中实现的条纹相（stripe phases）的声传播。尽管两个平台在微观层面存在显著差异，但在宏观层面可以建立相似的水动力学描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为超冷偶极气体和自旋轨道耦合玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BEC）平台中的条纹相（stripe phases）建立统一的声传播理论框架。尽管这两个系统在微观层面存在深刻差异，但需要探索它们在宏观水动力学描述上的相似性。

Method: 采用统一的水动力学方法（unified hydrodynamic approach）分析声传播。该方法特别关注自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit-coupled）情况下伽利略不变性（Galilean invariance）的缺失，这导致对密度正常（非超流）分量的不同识别，并在电流方程中引入新项。

Result: 两种情况下频谱都包含两种声模式，反映了U(1)对称性和平移对称性（translational symmetries）的自发破缺。两种声模式都表现出各向异性行为（anisotropic behavior）。研究还展示了与近晶A相液晶（smectic-A liquid crystal）的第一和第二声模式的比较。

Conclusion: 尽管超冷偶极气体和自旋轨道耦合BEC平台在微观层面存在深刻差异，但在宏观层面可以建立统一的条纹相声传播水动力学描述。自旋轨道耦合情况下伽利略不变性的缺失导致正常分量的不同识别，但两种系统都表现出相似的对称性破缺特征和各向异性声模式。

Abstract: We present a unified hydrodynamic approach for the sound propagation in the stripe phases realized in ultracold dipolar gas and spin-orbit-coupled BEC platforms at zero temperature. Despite the deep difference of the two platforms at a microscopic level, a similar hydrodynamic description can be formulated at a macroscopic level. The main difference between the two platforms is the lack of Galilean invariance in the spin-orbit case, resulting in a different identification of the normal (nonsuperfluid) component of the density, which leads to new terms in the equation for the current. In both cases the spectrum comprises two sounds, reflecting the spontaneous breaking of the U(1) and translational symmetries. Both sounds exhibit an anisotropic behavior. A comparison with the first and second sounds of the smectic-A liquid crystal is also presented.

</details>


### [154] [Merging and oscillations of dipolar Bose-Einstein condensate droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02011)
*Wojciech Orłowski,Bartłomiej Szafran*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过求解偶极Gross-Pitaevskii方程，分析了双势阱中偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体液滴在移除势垒后的动力学行为，揭示了液滴振荡、合并及阻尼机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）液滴在双势阱（double-well potential）中移除势垒后的动力学行为，特别是自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）对基态构型的影响。

Method: 通过求解偶极Gross-Pitaevskii方程（dipolar Gross-Pitaevskii equation），计算了双势阱中$^{164}$Dy原子构成的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体液滴的基态相图（ground-state phase diagrams），并分析了移除中心势垒后的时间演化。

Result: 强偶极相互作用下，最低能量构型源于液滴结构的自发对称破缺，以优化相互作用能。移除势垒后观察到液滴振荡（droplet oscillations）和合并事件（merger events），形成更大液滴。振荡由外势和偶极相互作用的平面内分量排斥尾部驱动，合并则需要初始过剩能量克服液滴间势垒。

Conclusion: 液滴振荡动力学对原子数、偶极相互作用强度和初始构型对称性敏感。单个液滴振荡以及液滴近距离相遇引起的原子泄漏共同导致振荡阻尼（damping of the oscillations）。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of Bose-Einstein condensate droplets composed of $^{164}$Dy atoms formed in a double-well potential following removal of the interwell barrier. By solving the dipolar Gross-Pitaevskii equation, we determine phase diagrams of ground-state configurations as functions of the atom number confined in the double-well potential. For strong dipolar interactions, some of the lowest-energy configurations arise from spontaneous symmetry breaking of the droplet structure, which optimizes the interaction energy. We analyze the subsequent time evolution after removal of the central barrier, revealing both droplet oscillations and merger events leading to the formation of larger droplets. The oscillations are driven by the external potential and by the repulsive tails of the in-plane component of the dipolar interaction. Merger events occur when the initial excess energy is sufficient to overcome the interdroplet potential barrier. The oscillatory dynamics depend sensitively on the atom number, the strength of dipolar interactions, and the initial symmetry of the configuration. We find that both oscillations of individual droplets and atom leakage from the droplets, induced by close droplet-droplet encounters, contribute to the damping of the oscillations.

</details>


### [155] [Quantum droplets in dipolar quasi-one-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensates in optical lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02163)
*Sk Siddik,Golam Ali Sekh*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究分析了嵌入光晶格中的偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BECs）中的量子液滴（quantum droplets），发现偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）增强会增大量子液滴的最优宽度，且稳定液滴的宽度呈现周期性振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索偶极玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（dipolar BECs）中量子液滴的特性，特别是长程且各向异性的偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interaction）如何影响量子液滴的自束缚机制和动力学行为。

Method: 研究方法基于Gross-Pitaevskii方程框架，分析了量子液滴的线性稳定性（linear stability）和动力学特性，研究了宽度有效势（effective potential for the width），并考察了光晶格（optical lattices）存在时的影响。

Result: 研究结果表明：偶极-偶极相互作用增强会增大量子液滴形成的最优宽度；稳定液滴的宽度呈现周期性振荡，且振荡幅度随偶极-偶极相互作用增强而增大；在光晶格存在时，稳定液滴的宽度变化呈现准周期性，而密度分布（density profile）在空间上周期性振荡。

Conclusion: 结论指出：量子液滴的振荡频率对光晶格参数高度敏感，这为通过调控晶格参数来控制量子液滴动力学行为提供了理论基础，揭示了偶极相互作用在量子液滴形成和稳定中的关键作用。

Abstract: We consider quantum droplets in dipolar Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) embedded in optical lattices within the framework of Gross-Pitaevskii equations. In dipolar BECs, the long-range and anistropic dipole-dipole interaction provides an additional mechanism for self-binding. We analyze the linear stability as well dynamics of quantum droplets. We find effective potential for the width and show that the optimum width for formation of quantum droplet increases as the dipole-dipole interaction increases. We study dynamics of the stable droplets and see that its width oscillates periodically, and the amplitude of oscillation increases with the increase of dipole-dipole interaction. In presence of optical lattices, width of a stable droplet changes quasi-periodically while the density profile oscillating periodically in space. The frequency of oscillation are found to depend sensitively on the lattice parameters.

</details>
